### Lesson 32: Data Export and Backup

#### Learning Objectives
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:
- Export all business data (dogs, litters, customers, expenses, reports)
- Select export formats (CSV, Excel, PDF, JSON)
- Schedule regular data exports
- Perform full and partial backups
- Restore data from backup
- Ensure data security and compliance
- Use exports for migration or analysis
- Maintain reliable data protection

#### Overview
The Data Export and Backup system ensures your breeder business data is safe, portable, and always accessible. It supports exporting all key records, scheduling backups, and restoring data in case of loss or migration.

#### Key Features
- Export all or selected data (dogs, litters, customers, expenses, reports)
- Multiple formats: CSV, Excel, PDF, JSON
- Scheduled and manual exports
- Full and incremental backups
- Restore from backup
- Secure storage and encryption
- Migration tools

![Screenshot: Data export and backup dashboard]

#### Step-by-Step Instructions

**1. Exporting Data**
1. Go to "Data Export" in the main menu
2. Select data type (dogs, litters, customers, expenses, reports)
3. Choose export format (CSV, Excel, PDF, JSON)
4. Set date range or filters (optional)
5. Click "Export"
6. Download file

**2. Scheduling Regular Exports**
1. Go to "Export Scheduler"
2. Select data types and formats
3. Set frequency (daily, weekly, monthly)
4. Enter recipient email(s)
5. Enable notifications
6. Save schedule

**3. Performing a Full Backup**
1. Go to "Backup" section
2. Click "Create Full Backup"
3. System compiles all data
4. Download backup file
5. Store securely (cloud, external drive)

**4. Performing an Incremental Backup**
1. Go to "Backup" section
2. Click "Create Incremental Backup"
3. Select date range or changes since last backup
4. Download file

**5. Restoring Data from Backup**
1. Go to "Restore" section
2. Upload backup file
3. Select data types to restore
4. Confirm restoration
5. Review restored records

**6. Ensuring Data Security**
1. Enable encryption for exports and backups
2. Use strong passwords for backup files
3. Store backups in secure locations
4. Limit access to authorized users

**7. Migrating Data to Another System**
1. Export data in compatible format (CSV, JSON)
2. Use migration tool or import function in new system
3. Verify data integrity after migration

#### Practice Exercises

**Exercise 1: Export All Customer Records**
1. Go to Data Export
2. Select "Customers"
3. Choose CSV format
4. Export and download file
5. Open in Excel

**Exercise 2: Schedule Weekly Expense Export**
1. Go to Export Scheduler
2. Select "Expenses"
3. Set frequency to weekly
4. Enter your email
5. Save schedule

**Exercise 3: Perform a Full Backup**
1. Go to Backup
2. Click "Create Full Backup"
3. Download file
4. Store on external drive

**Exercise 4: Restore Data from Backup**
1. Go to Restore
2. Upload backup file
3. Select "Litters" and "Dogs"
4. Confirm restoration
5. Verify records

**Exercise 5: Export Data for Migration**
1. Go to Data Export
2. Select all data types
3. Choose JSON format
4. Export and download
5. Import to new system

**Exercise 6: Enable Encryption for Backups**
1. Go to Backup Settings
2. Enable encryption
3. Set strong password
4. Save settings

#### Tooltips and Quick Help

> ðŸ’¾ **Export Everything**: Download all your data for analysis or migration
> ðŸ”’ **Encrypted Backups**: Keep backups secure with encryption
> ðŸ“… **Automate Exports**: Schedule regular exports for peace of mind
> ðŸ› ï¸ **Restore Easily**: Recover data quickly from backup files
> ðŸ“¤ **Multiple Formats**: Choose the format that fits your needs
> ðŸ§‘â€ðŸ’» **Migration Ready**: Export data for use in other systems

#### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Export file not downloading**
- Solution: Check browser settings, disable pop-up blockers, try another browser

**Problem: Backup file corrupted**
- Solution: Recreate backup, verify storage device, enable encryption

**Problem: Restore not working**
- Solution: Check file format, ensure correct backup version, contact support

**Problem: Scheduled exports not arriving**
- Solution: Verify email settings, check spam folder, review scheduler

**Problem: Data missing after migration**
- Solution: Check export filters, verify import process, compare record counts

#### Advanced Features

- Incremental and differential backups
- Cloud backup integration (Google Drive, Dropbox)
- Automated backup verification
- Data integrity checks
- API access for automated exports
- Audit logs for export and restore actions

#### Knowledge Check
- â˜ I can export all business data
- â˜ I know how to select export formats
- â˜ I can schedule regular exports
- â˜ I can perform full and incremental backups
- â˜ I can restore data from backup
- â˜ I understand data security and encryption
- â˜ I can migrate data to other systems
- â˜ I maintain reliable data protection

### Lesson 31: Reporting and Analytics

#### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Generate key business reports
- Visualize data with charts and graphs
- Track performance metrics (sales, health, customer engagement)
- Customize report parameters and filters
- Schedule automated reports
- Export and share reports
- Use analytics to improve decision-making
- Monitor trends and KPIs

#### Overview

The Reporting and Analytics system provides insights into your breeding business, helping you make data-driven decisions. It covers sales, health, customer, financial, and operational metrics, with customizable dashboards and export options.

#### Key Features

- Sales, health, customer, and financial reports
- Customizable dashboards
- Interactive charts and graphs
- Report scheduling and automation
- Export to PDF, CSV, Excel
- KPI tracking and trend analysis

![Screenshot: Analytics dashboard with charts]

#### Step-by-Step Instructions

**1. Accessing the Analytics Dashboard**

1. Go to "Reports" or "Analytics" in the main menu
2. View summary dashboard
3. Select report type (sales, health, customer, financial)
4. Review key metrics and visualizations

**2. Generating a Sales Report**

1. Click "Sales Report"
2. Set date range and filters (breed, litter, customer)
3. View total sales, deposits, refunds
4. Analyze top-performing litters and dogs
5. Export report

**3. Health and Wellness Reporting**

1. Select "Health Report"
2. Filter by dog, litter, or date
3. Track vaccinations, vet visits, health issues
4. View trends and compliance
5. Export for vet or records

**4. Customer Engagement Analytics**

1. Open "Customer Report"
2. Analyze inquiries, applications, conversions
3. Track communication frequency
4. Identify top sources of leads
5. Export for marketing review

**5. Financial Performance Reports**

1. Select "Financial Report"
2. View income, expenses, net profit
3. Compare periods (month, quarter, year)
4. Identify cost drivers and savings
5. Export for accounting

**6. Customizing Reports**

1. Use filters (date, breed, status, etc.)
2. Add/remove columns
3. Save custom report templates
4. Schedule recurring reports

**7. Visualizing Data**

1. Use built-in charts (bar, line, pie, area)
2. Hover for details
3. Download chart images
4. Embed charts in presentations

**8. Scheduling Automated Reports**

1. Go to "Report Scheduler"
2. Select report and frequency (daily, weekly, monthly)
3. Set recipients (email)
4. Enable notifications
5. Review scheduled reports

#### Practice Exercises

1. Go to Reports > Sales

3. Filter by breed
4. Export to PDF

1. Go to Reports > Health
2. Select a litter

4. Export for vet

1. Go to Reports > Customer
2. Track inquiries and conversions
3. Identify top lead sources

2. Compare last quarter to previous
3. Identify cost savings
4. Export to Excel

1. Generate a custom report
2. Add/remove columns
3. Save as template
4. Schedule for monthly delivery

**Exercise 6: Visualize Data with Charts**

1. Open Analytics dashboard
2. Select bar chart for sales
3. Download chart image
4. Embed in a presentation

#### Tooltips and Quick Help

> ðŸ“Š **Visualize Trends**: Interactive charts make data easy to understand
> ðŸ—‚ï¸ **Custom Reports**: Filter, sort, and save your favorite views
> ðŸ“… **Automate Delivery**: Schedule reports to arrive in your inbox
> ðŸ“ˆ **Track KPIs**: Monitor key metrics for business health
> ðŸ“¤ **Export Easily**: Download reports for sharing or accounting
> ðŸ” **Drill Down**: Click any chart for detailed breakdowns

#### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Report not generating**

- Solution: Check filters, ensure data exists for selected range

**Problem: Charts not displaying**

- Solution: Update browser, clear cache, check data completeness

**Problem: Scheduled reports not arriving**

- Solution: Verify email settings, check spam folder, review scheduler

**Problem: Exported report missing data**

- Solution: Check filters, ensure all columns included

**Problem: Custom report template not saving**

- Solution: Confirm all required fields, try saving again

#### Advanced Features

### Lesson 30: Expense Tracking and Financial Management

#### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Record and categorize breeding-related expenses
- Track income and payments
- Generate financial reports
- Set budgets and monitor spending
- Attach receipts and invoices
- Analyze profitability by litter, dog, or program
- Export financial data for accounting
- Use financial tools for business growth

#### Overview

The Expense Tracking and Financial Management system helps you monitor costs, manage income, and keep your breeding business financially healthy. It supports detailed expense entry, income tracking, reporting, and integration with accounting tools.

#### Key Features

- Expense entry with categories and tags
- Income tracking (sales, deposits, fees)
- Receipt and invoice uploads
- Budget setting and alerts
- Financial dashboard and analytics
- Export to CSV/Excel
- Integration with accounting software

![Screenshot: Expense dashboard and entry form]

#### Step-by-Step Instructions

**1. Recording an Expense**

1. Go to "Expenses" in the main menu
2. Click "Add Expense"
3. Enter details:
   - Date
   - Category (food, vet, supplies, travel, etc.)
   - Amount
   - Description
   - Attach receipt (optional)
4. Assign to dog, litter, or program
5. Save expense

**2. Tracking Income**

1. Go to "Income" section
2. Click "Add Income"
3. Enter details:
   - Date
   - Source (puppy sale, deposit, stud fee, refund)
   - Amount
   - Description
   - Attach invoice (optional)
4. Assign to dog, litter, or program
5. Save income

**3. Categorizing and Tagging**

1. Use built-in categories (food, vet, travel, etc.)
2. Add custom categories
3. Tag expenses (annual, recurring, one-time)
4. Filter by category or tag

**4. Attaching Receipts and Invoices**

1. When adding expense/income, click "Attach File"
2. Upload PDF, JPG, or PNG
3. Preview attachment
4. Save with record

**5. Setting Budgets and Alerts**

1. Go to "Budgets" in Expenses
2. Set monthly/annual budget per category
3. Enable alerts for overspending
4. Monitor budget status on dashboard

**6. Generating Financial Reports**

1. Go to "Reports" in Expenses
2. Select report type (summary, by dog, by litter, by category)
3. Set date range
4. View charts and tables
5. Export to CSV/Excel

**7. Analyzing Profitability**

1. Open "Profitability" dashboard
2. Select dog, litter, or program
3. View total income vs. expenses
4. See net profit/loss
5. Review trends over time

**8. Exporting Data for Accounting**

1. Go to "Export" in Expenses
2. Choose format (CSV, Excel)
3. Select date range and filters
4. Download file
5. Import to accounting software

#### Practice Exercises

**Exercise 1: Add a New Expense**

1. Go to Expenses > Add Expense
2. Enter a recent vet bill
3. Attach the receipt
4. Assign to a specific dog
5. Save and verify entry

**Exercise 2: Record Income from Puppy Sale**

1. Go to Income > Add Income
2. Enter sale details
3. Attach invoice
4. Assign to litter
5. Save and verify entry

**Exercise 3: Set a Monthly Budget**

1. Go to Budgets
2. Set budget for "Food" category
3. Enable alerts
4. Track spending for the month

**Exercise 4: Generate a Profitability Report**

1. Go to Reports
2. Select "By Litter"
3. Choose a recent litter
4. View income, expenses, and net profit
5. Export report

**Exercise 5: Attach Receipts to Expenses**

1. Edit an existing expense
2. Click "Attach File"
3. Upload a PDF receipt
4. Save and preview

**Exercise 6: Export Financial Data**

1. Go to Export
2. Select last quarter
3. Download CSV
4. Open in Excel
5. Review data

#### Tooltips and Quick Help

> ðŸ’¸ **Track Every Dollar**: Record all expenses and income for full visibility
> ðŸ“ **Attach Receipts**: Keep digital copies of all bills and invoices
> ðŸ“Š **Analyze Profitability**: See which litters and dogs are most profitable
> ðŸ”” **Budget Alerts**: Get notified before you overspend
> ðŸ“ˆ **Export Easily**: Download data for your accountant or tax prep
> ðŸ·ï¸ **Custom Categories**: Organize expenses your way

#### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Expense not saving**

- Solution: Check required fields, verify file type for attachments

**Problem: Income not showing in reports**

- Solution: Confirm correct date and assignment, refresh dashboard

**Problem: Budget alerts not working**

- Solution: Ensure alerts enabled, check notification settings

**Problem: File upload fails**

- Solution: Check file size/type, try a different browser

**Problem: Exported data missing entries**

- Solution: Check filters/date range, verify all records included

#### Advanced Features

- Recurring expenses and income
- Multi-currency support
- Tax calculation and reporting
- Integration with QuickBooks, Xero, etc.
- Automated receipt scanning (OCR)
- Financial forecasting tools

- â˜ I can record and categorize expenses
- â˜ I know how to track income and payments
- â˜ I can generate financial reports
- â˜ I can set and monitor budgets
- â˜ I can attach receipts and invoices
- â˜ I can analyze profitability
- â˜ I can export financial data

# Module 1: Getting Started

## Lesson 1: Account Setup and Login

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Create a new account
- Verify your email address
- Log in and out securely
- Reset your password if needed

### Step-by-Step Instructions

#### Creating Your Account

1. **Navigate to the Login Page**

   - Open your web browser
   - Go to the app URL
   - You'll see the login screen

2. **Click Sign Up**

   - Locate the "Sign Up" button
   - Click to open the registration form

3. **Enter Your Information**

   - Email Address: Use a valid email you check regularly
   - Password: Create a strong password with:
     - At least 8 characters
     - Mix of uppercase and lowercase letters
     - Numbers
     - Special characters (recommended)

4. **Submit Registration**

   - Click "Create Account"
   - Wait for confirmation message

5. **Verify Your Email**
   - Check your email inbox
   - Look for verification email (check spam folder if not in inbox)
   - Click the verification link
   - You'll be redirected to the login page

#### Logging In

1. **Enter Credentials**

   - Email: Your registered email
   - Password: Your password
   - â˜‘ Remember Me (optional - keeps you logged in)

2. **Click Sign In**
   - You'll be taken to your dashboard

#### Troubleshooting Login Issues

**Problem: "Invalid email or password"**

- Solution: Double-check spelling and Caps Lock
- Try "Forgot Password" to reset

**Problem: Email not verified**

- Solution: Check spam folder for verification email
- Click "Resend Verification Email" if needed

**Problem: Can't receive verification email**

- Solution: Check spam/junk folders
- Try a different email address
- Contact support

### Practice Exercise

1. Create a test account (if allowed)
2. Log in and out 3 times
3. Practice password reset process

### Knowledge Check

- â˜ I can create an account
- â˜ I can verify my email
- â˜ I can log in successfully
- â˜ I know how to reset my password

---

## Lesson 2: Breeder Profile Configuration

### Learning Objectives

- Complete breeder profile information
- Upload kennel logo
- Configure contact preferences
- Enable public features

### Your Breeder Profile

Your breeder profile is the foundation of your presence in the app. It contains:

- Kennel information that appears on your public website
- Contact details for customer communication
- Business information for contracts and documents

### Profile Setup Walkthrough

#### Accessing Settings

1. **Open Settings**
   - Look at the sidebar (left side of screen)
   - Scroll to bottom of navigation
   - Click "Settings"
   - Settings page opens

#### Kennel Information Section

**Kennel Name**

- Purpose: Your business/kennel name
- Example: "Golden Dreams Kennel"
- Tip: Use the name you want on contracts

**Kennel Description**

- Purpose: Brief description of your breeding program
- Example: "Family-raised golden retrievers with champion bloodlines"
- Tip: This appears on your public website
- Recommended: 2-3 sentences

**Breed(s)**

- Purpose: Primary breed(s) you work with
- Example: "Golden Retriever" or "Golden Retriever, Labrador Retriever"
- Tip: Separate multiple breeds with commas

#### Location Information

**City and State**

- Purpose: Your location
- Example: "San Diego, California"
- Privacy Note: Only city/state shows publicly (not full address)

**Full Address** (Optional)

- Purpose: For contracts and private records
- Not displayed publicly
- Used for shipping/pickup documentation

#### Contact Details

**Phone Number**

- Format: (555) 123-4567 or 555-123-4567
- Tip: Use your preferred contact number
- Can be shown/hidden on public site

**Email Address**

- Your primary business email
- Used for inquiry notifications
- Can be shown/hidden on public site

**Website** (Optional)

- Your existing website URL
- Example: "https://www.yourkennel.com"
- Shows as link on public profile

#### Social Media Links

**Why Add Social Media?**

- Builds trust with potential buyers
- Shows active breeding program
- Provides additional ways to connect

**Supported Platforms**

- Facebook: Full URL to your page
- Instagram: Full URL to your profile
- Twitter: Full URL to your profile

**Format Examples**

- Facebook: `https://facebook.com/yourkennel`
- Instagram: `https://instagram.com/yourkennel`
- Twitter: `https://twitter.com/yourkennel`

#### Logo Upload

**Preparing Your Logo**

- File format: JPG, PNG, or WebP
- Recommended size: 500x500 pixels
- Maximum file size: 5MB
- Best: Square image with transparent background

**Upload Process**

1. Click "Upload Logo" button
2. Browse to select your logo file
3. Image cropping tool appears
4. Adjust crop area if needed
5. Click "Save"
6. Logo appears in profile

**Logo Usage**

- Shows on your public website
- Appears on generated documents
- Displays in breeder connections

### Saving Your Profile

**Important: Always Save!**

1. Scroll to bottom of Settings page
2. Click "Save Profile" button
3. Wait for confirmation message
4. "Profile updated successfully" appears

### Practice Exercise

Complete your breeder profile:

- â˜ Fill in kennel name
- â˜ Write description (2-3 sentences)
- â˜ Add location information
- â˜ Enter contact details
- â˜ Upload logo
- â˜ Add at least one social media link
- â˜ Save profile

### Knowledge Check

- â˜ My profile is complete
- â˜ I uploaded a logo
- â˜ I know what information is public
- â˜ I saved my changes

## Lesson 3: Understanding the Dashboard

### Learning Objectives

- Navigate the dashboard
- Understand key metrics
- Interpret statistics cards
- Use quick actions

### Dashboard Overview

The Dashboard is your command center. It provides:

- At-a-glance statistics
- Quick access to important information
- Upcoming events and reminders
- Recent activity

### Dashboard Sections

#### 1. Statistics Cards (Top Row)

**Total Dogs**

- Shows: Number of active dogs in your program
- Excludes: Deceased/retired dogs
- Click: Opens Dogs page with all dogs

**Active Dams**

- Shows: Breeding-age female dogs
- Includes: Only active, not retired
- Click: Opens Dogs page filtered to females

**Active Sires**

- Shows: Breeding-age male dogs
- Includes: Only active males
- Click: Opens Dogs page filtered to males

**Puppies Available**

- Shows: Puppies currently for sale
- Status: Only "Available" puppies
- Click: Opens Litters page with available puppies

**This Year's Income**

- Shows: Total sales revenue this calendar year
- Includes: Completed puppy sales only
- Updates: Real-time as sales are recorded

#### 2. Upcoming Heats (Middle Section)

**What It Shows**

- Female dogs with predicted upcoming heat cycles
- Days until expected heat
- Last heat cycle date

**How Predictions Work**

- Based on previous heat cycle dates
- Uses average cycle length (typically 6-7 months)
- Accuracy improves with more data

**Using This Information**

- Plan breeding schedules
- Prepare for heats
- Contact stud owners in advance

**Color Coding**

- Green: More than 30 days away
- Orange: Within 30 days
- Red: Within 7 days

#### 3. Quick Actions (Right Side)

**Add Dog**

- Click: Opens dog creation form
- Shortcut: No need to navigate to Dogs page

**Add Litter**

- Click: Opens litter creation form
- Shortcut: Start litter records immediately

**View All**

- Links to full pages
- See complete lists

#### 4. Recent Activity

**What Appears Here**

- New inquiries
- Upcoming pickups
- Recent puppy births
- Important reminders

**Activity Items**

- Shows date/time
- Brief description
- Click to view details

### Refreshing Data

**Automatic Refresh**

- Dashboard updates in real-time
- New data appears automatically
- No need to reload page

**Manual Refresh**

- Click browser refresh (F5)
- Use Ctrl+R (Windows) or Cmd+R (Mac)
- Ensures latest data

### Practice Exercise

Explore your dashboard:

1. Click on each statistics card
2. Note what page opens
3. Return to dashboard each time
4. Try the quick action buttons
5. Observe the layout and information

### Knowledge Check

- â˜ I understand each statistics card
- â˜ I can use quick actions
- â˜ I know how to interpret heat predictions
- â˜ I can navigate from dashboard efficiently

---

## Lesson 4: Navigation and Interface

### Learning Objectives

- Master sidebar navigation
- Use search functionality
- Understand page layouts
- Access help resources

### Sidebar Navigation

#### Navigation Structure

**Top Section: Management**

- Dashboard: Home view with statistics
- Dogs: All dog records
- Litters: All litter records
- Calendar: Date-based events
- Reminders: Alerts and notifications

**Middle Section: Records**

- Health Records: Health tracking across all dogs
- Pedigrees: Family tree views

**Bottom Section: Business**

- Customers: CRM and contact management
- Waitlist: Application management
- Inquiries: Lead tracking
- Connections: Breeder networking
- Analytics: Reports and insights
- Website: Public website settings
- Settings: App configuration
- Help: This training and support

#### Sidebar Features

**Collapsible Sidebar**

- Click arrow icon to collapse
- Saves screen space
- Icons remain visible
- Click arrow to expand

**Pin Sidebar**

- Click pin icon to keep open
- Stays open as you navigate
- Useful for frequent navigation
- Click again to unpin

**Active Page Highlighting**

- Current page is highlighted
- Visual indicator of location
- Makes orientation easy

### Search Functionality

**Global Search Bar**

- Located at top of screen
- Searches across all records
- Type to see results instantly

**What You Can Search**

- Dog names
- Customer names
- Litter names
- Registration numbers
- Microchip numbers
- Phone numbers
- Email addresses

**Search Tips**

- Type partial names (e.g., "Max" finds "Maximus")
- Search is not case-sensitive
- Use full registration numbers for exact match
- Recent searches may appear

### Page Layouts

#### Common Elements

**Page Header**

- Page title
- Brief description
- Action buttons (e.g., "+ Add Dog")

**Filters and Sorting**

- Filter dropdowns
- Sort options
- Search within page

**Data Tables**

- Sortable columns
- Clickable rows
- Action buttons per row

**Detail Views**

- Tabs for different sections
- Edit buttons
- Related records

### Getting Help

#### In-App Help

1. Click "Help" in sidebar
2. Search for topics
3. Browse categories
4. Read step-by-step guides

#### Contextual Help

- Look for (?) icons
- Hover for tooltips
- Click for detailed explanation

#### External Resources

- User manual (this document)
- Quick start guide
- Video tutorials (coming soon)

### Practice Exercise

Navigation challenge:

1. Start at Dashboard
2. Navigate to Dogs
3. Open a dog profile
4. Use breadcrumbs to go back
5. Try collapsing sidebar
6. Search for a dog by name
7. Access Help section
8. Return to Dashboard

### Knowledge Check

- â˜ I can navigate using the sidebar
- â˜ I can search for records
- â˜ I understand page layouts
- â˜ I know where to find help

# Module 2: Dog Management

## Lesson 5: Adding and Managing Dogs

### Learning Objectives

- Add new dogs to the system
- Edit existing dog information
- Upload and manage photos
- Set program status
- Delete dogs (when necessary)

### Adding Your First Dog

#### Opening the Add Dog Form

**Method 1: From Dogs Page**

1. Click "Dogs" in sidebar
2. Click "+ Add Dog" button (top right)

**Method 2: From Dashboard**

1. Look for "Quick Actions" section
2. Click "Add Dog" button

**Method 3: Using Keyboard**

1. Press Ctrl+K (Windows) or Cmd+K (Mac)
2. Type "Add Dog"
3. Press Enter

#### Required Information

**Name**

- Dog's registered or call name
- Examples: "Champion's Golden Star" or "Buddy"
- Tip: Use the name that appears on registration

**Breed**

- Start typing breed name
- Select from dropdown (280+ breeds)
- Examples: "Golden Retriever", "Labrador Retriever"
- Note: Searchable and auto-complete

**Sex**

- Select: Male or Female
- Important for breeding records
- Affects heat cycle tracking

**Date of Birth**

- Click calendar icon
- Select or type date
- Format: MM/DD/YYYY
- Tip: Exact date helps with age calculations

#### Recommended Information

**Color**

- Primary coat color
- Examples: "Golden", "Black", "Chocolate"
- Free text field

**Markings**

- Distinctive markings
- Examples: "White chest patch", "Black mask"
- Helps identification

**Weight**

- Current weight in pounds
- Can be updated anytime
- Used for health tracking

#### Advanced Information

**Registration**

- Registration Number: AKC/CKC number
- Registration Status:
  - Registered
  - Pending
  - Not Registered

**Program Status**

- Breeding Dog: Active in program
- Guardian Home: Lives with family
- External Stud: Breeding services only
- Retired: No longer breeding

**Parents**

- Sire: Father's name (select from your dogs)
- Dam: Mother's name (select from your dogs)
- Note: Needed for pedigrees

**Additional Details**

- Microchip Number
- Titles and Achievements
- Special Notes

### Photo Management

#### Uploading Photos

**Drag and Drop**

1. Drag photo from computer
2. Drop onto upload area
3. Wait for upload to complete

**Click to Browse**

1. Click "Upload Photo" button
2. Browse your computer
3. Select photo file
4. Click "Open"

**Photo Requirements**

- Format: JPG, PNG, WebP
- Max size: 5MB per photo
- Recommended: 1000x1000 pixels or larger
- Orientation: Any (will be adjusted)

#### Managing Multiple Photos

**Adding More Photos**

- Click "+ Add Another Photo"
- Upload additional images
- First photo is the featured image

**Reordering Photos**

- Drag photos to reorder
- First photo shows in lists
- Order affects display

**Deleting Photos**

- Hover over photo
- Click "X" or trash icon
- Confirm deletion

### Editing Dogs

#### Opening Edit Mode

**From Dogs List**

1. Find dog in list
2. Click "Edit" button
3. Edit form opens

**From Dog Profile**

1. Open dog's profile page
2. Click "Edit" button (top right)
3. Make changes

#### What You Can Edit

- âœ… All basic information
- âœ… Photos (add, remove, reorder)
- âœ… Registration details
- âœ… Program status
- âœ… Parents (sire/dam)
- âœ… Notes and details

#### What You Cannot Edit

- âŒ System-generated ID
- âŒ Creation date
- âŒ Historical records (but can add notes)

#### Saving Changes

1. Make your edits
2. Scroll to bottom
3. Click "Save Changes"
4. Wait for confirmation

### Marking Dogs as Retired/Deceased

#### Retiring a Dog

**Why Retire?**

- No longer breeding
- Keep in system for pedigrees
- Maintain historical records

**How to Retire**

1. Edit dog
2. Change Program Status to "Retired"
3. Add note with retirement date
4. Save changes

**What Happens**

- Removed from active breeding counts
- Still appears in pedigrees
- Historical litters remain linked

#### Marking as Deceased

**When to Use**

- Dog has passed away
- Want to keep records
- Maintain pedigree completeness

**How to Mark Deceased**

1. Edit dog
2. Check "Deceased" checkbox
3. Enter date of death
4. Add optional notes/memorial
5. Save changes

**What Happens**

- Removed from all active counts
- Pedigrees still show the dog
- Records preserved
- Memorial note saved

### Deleting Dogs

âš ï¸ **Warning: Deletion is Permanent**

**When to Delete**

- Duplicate entry by mistake
- Test data to remove
- Dog never in your program

**What Gets Deleted**

- Dog record completely removed
- Photos deleted
- Health records removed
- Pedigree connections broken

**What's Preserved**

- Litter records (but sire/dam link broken)
- Historical data references

**How to Delete**

1. Go to dog profile or list
2. Click "Delete" button
3. Confirm deletion (type name)
4. Dog permanently removed

**Better Alternative: Mark Deceased**

- Preserves historical data
- Maintains pedigree integrity
- Keeps litter connections

### Practice Exercises

**Exercise 1: Add a Dog**

1. Click "Dogs" â†’ "+ Add Dog"
2. Enter all required information
3. Upload a photo
4. Set program status
5. Save the dog

**Exercise 2: Edit a Dog**

1. Open the dog you just created
2. Click "Edit"
3. Add weight
4. Upload another photo
5. Save changes

**Exercise 3: Photo Management**

1. Upload 3 photos to a dog
2. Reorder them
3. Make the best one first
4. Delete one photo
5. Save

### Knowledge Check

- â˜ I can add a new dog with all details
- â˜ I can upload and manage photos
- â˜ I can edit existing dogs
- â˜ I understand program status options
- â˜ I know when to retire vs. delete dogs

## Lesson 6: Health Records and DNA Profiles

### Learning Objectives

- Record vaccinations
- Track vet visits
- Store DNA test results
- Monitor health events
- View health history

### Health Tracking Overview

The health tracking system helps you:

- Maintain complete medical records
- Track vaccination schedules
- Store genetic test results
- Monitor health trends
- Generate health reports for buyers

### Vaccinations

#### Recording Vaccinations

**Access Vaccination Records**

1. Open dog profile
2. Click "Health" tab
3. Find "Vaccinations" section
4. Click "Add Vaccination"

**Vaccination Information**

- **Date**: When vaccine was administered
- **Type**: Vaccine name (e.g., "Rabies", "DHPP", "Bordetella")
- **Veterinarian**: Vet's name or clinic
- **Next Due**: When next dose is due (optional)
- **Notes**: Reactions, lot number, etc.

**Common Vaccines**

- Rabies
- DHPP (Distemper, Hepatitis, Parvovirus, Parainfluenza)
- Bordetella (Kennel Cough)
- Leptospirosis
- Lyme Disease
- Canine Influenza

#### Vaccination Schedule

**Puppy Series (6-16 weeks)**

- 6-8 weeks: DHPP #1
- 10-12 weeks: DHPP #2
- 14-16 weeks: DHPP #3, Rabies

**Adult Boosters**

- Rabies: Every 1-3 years
- DHPP: Annually or every 3 years
- Bordetella: Every 6-12 months

**Reminders**

- System alerts before vaccines due
- Shows overdue vaccines
- Tracks series completion

### Vet Visits

#### Recording Vet Visits

**Add Vet Visit**

1. Health tab â†’ "Vet Visits"
2. Click "Add Vet Visit"
3. Enter information:
   - Date of visit
   - Reason (checkup, illness, injury, etc.)
   - Veterinarian name
   - Diagnosis/findings
   - Treatment provided
   - Follow-up needed
   - Cost (optional)
   - Notes

**Visit Types**

- Routine checkup
- Illness/injury
- Pre-breeding exam
- Pregnancy check
- Surgery
- Emergency
- Follow-up

**Attaching Documents**

- Upload vet reports
- Store test results
- Keep prescriptions
- Save X-rays/images

### DNA Profiles

#### What is a DNA Profile?

DNA testing reveals:

- Genetic health markers
- Coat color genetics
- Physical trait genetics
- Breed verification
- Parentage verification

#### Adding DNA Test Results

**Access DNA Section**

1. Dog profile â†’ Health tab
2. Find "DNA Profile" section
3. Click "Add/Edit DNA Profile"

**Health Markers**

- Disease carrier status
- Health conditions tested
- Clear/Carrier/Affected results
- Test date and lab

**Coat Color Genetics**

- Base color (E locus, B locus)
- Dilution (D locus)
- Patterns (K locus, A locus)
- White spotting (S locus)
- Furnishings (F locus)

**Physical Traits**

- Size predictions
- Tail length genetics
- Ear type
- Muzzle length
- Leg length

**Inputting Results**

1. Select test provider (Embark, Wisdom Panel, etc.)
2. Enter test date
3. Record results for each marker
4. Upload PDF report (optional)
5. Save profile

#### Using DNA Information

**For Breeding Decisions**

- Avoid pairing two carriers
- Predict puppy colors
- Plan for specific traits

**For Buyers**

- Provide genetic health clearances
- Show color predictions
- Demonstrate testing commitment

**For Pedigrees**

- Include in pedigree exports
- Show genetic diversity
- Track hereditary health

### Health Events

#### Recording Health Events

**What to Record**

- Injuries
- Illnesses
- Surgeries
- Reactions
- Unusual symptoms
- Chronic conditions

**Event Details**

- Date of occurrence
- Description of event
- Severity (mild, moderate, severe)
- Treatment provided
- Outcome
- Recovery time
- Follow-up needed

**Why Track Events**

- Complete medical history
- Pattern identification
- Breeding decisions
- Puppy buyer disclosure

### Weight Tracking

#### Recording Weights

**Add Weight Entry**

1. Health tab â†’ "Weight Tracking"
2. Click "Add Weight"
3. Enter:
   - Date
   - Weight (pounds)
   - Body condition (optional)
   - Notes

**Weight Chart**

- Visual graph of weight over time
- Identify trends
- Compare to breed standards
- Monitor health

**Ideal Weight Ranges**

- Compare to breed standards
- Track individual trends
- Flag unusual changes

### Health Reports

#### Generating Health Reports

**For Puppy Buyers**

1. Go to dog profile
2. Health tab
3. Click "Generate Health Report"
4. Select information to include:
   - Vaccinations
   - Vet visits
   - DNA results
   - Health clearances
5. Export as PDF

**Report Uses**

- Provide to buyers
- Show at health exams
- Submit for registrations
- Share with vets

### Practice Exercises

**Exercise 1: Add Vaccination Record**

1. Select a dog
2. Go to Health tab
3. Add today's date rabies vaccine
4. Add your vet's name
5. Set next due date (1 year)
6. Save

1. Add a vet visit for annual checkup
2. Enter today's date
3. Write "Annual wellness exam - healthy"
4. Add vet name
5. Record cost (e.g., $150)
6. Save

**Exercise 3: Start DNA Profile**

1. Open DNA Profile section
2. Select a test provider
3. Enter test date
4. Add at least one health marker result
5. Add coat color results
6. Save profile

## Lesson 7: Heat Cycle Tracking

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Record heat cycle dates
- Track cycle patterns
- Predict upcoming heats
- Plan breeding schedules
- Set heat cycle reminders

### Why Track Heat Cycles?

Heat cycle tracking is essential for:

- **Breeding Planning**: Know when females are fertile
- **Health Monitoring**: Identify irregularities
- **Schedule Coordination**: Plan for optimal breeding times
- **Stud Booking**: Reserve stud services in advance
- **Litter Spacing**: Maintain healthy intervals between litters

> ðŸ’¡ **Tip**: Most dogs cycle every 6-7 months, but this varies by breed and individual dog.

### Understanding Heat Cycles

#### The Four Stages

**1. Proestrus (7-10 days)**

- Vulva swelling begins
- Bloody discharge
- Attracts males but won't breed
- Not fertile yet

**2. Estrus (5-9 days)**

- Standing heat - receptive to males
- Discharge lightens (straw-colored)
- Ovulation occurs
- **FERTILE PERIOD** ðŸ”´

**3. Diestrus (60-90 days)**

- Heat signs end
- May have false pregnancy
- Not fertile

**4. Anestrus (4-5 months)**

- Normal period between heats
- Reproductive rest

### Recording a Heat Cycle

![Screenshot: Dog profile with Heat Cycles tab highlighted]

#### Step-by-Step Process

**1. Access Heat Cycle Tracking**

1. Navigate to **Dogs** page
2. Click on a female dog's profile
3. Select **"Heat Cycles"** tab
4. Click **"+ Add Heat Cycle"** button

**2. Enter Start Date**

- **First Day of Heat**: Date when you first notice signs
- Use calendar picker
- Format: MM/DD/YYYY
- Most accurate if recorded on day 1

> ðŸ’¡ **Tip**: Set a reminder to check your females regularly so you catch day 1

**3. Record Key Information**

**Start Date** (Required)

- First day of bleeding/swelling
- Example: 03/15/2025

**End Date** (Optional)

- Last day of discharge
- Usually 14-21 days after start
- Can add later if unsure

**Breeding Window**

- Days 10-14 typically
- Can vary by individual
- Mark best breeding days

**Notes Field**

- Behavioral changes observed
- Intensity of heat
- Any complications
- Stud used (if bred)
- Example: "Strong heat, bred on day 12 with Max"

**4. Save the Record**

- Click **"Save"**
- Heat cycle appears in timeline
- Next heat prediction calculated

### Viewing Heat Cycle History

#### Heat Cycle Timeline

![Screenshot: Heat cycle timeline showing multiple cycles]

**What You See:**

- Chronological list of all heats
- Start and end dates
- Days between cycles
- Notes for each cycle
- Breeding records linked

**Color Coding:**

- ðŸ”µ Blue = Past heats
- ðŸŸ¡ Yellow = Current heat
- ðŸŸ¢ Green = Predicted upcoming heat

#### Heat Cycle Statistics

**Average Cycle Length**

- Calculated from your data
- Updates with each new cycle
- Individual to each dog
- More accurate over time

**Example:**

```
Average Cycle: 6.5 months
Last Heat: 03/15/2025
Next Predicted: 09/30/2025
Confidence: High (based on 5 previous cycles)
```

### Predicting Upcoming Heats

#### How Predictions Work

**Algorithm Factors:**

1. Average cycle length from past heats
2. Recent cycle pattern trends
3. Dog's age and maturity
4. Seasonal variations (if applicable)

**Prediction Accuracy:**

- **High**: 4+ recorded cycles, regular pattern
- **Medium**: 2-3 recorded cycles
- **Low**: 0-1 recorded cycles

> âš ï¸ **Note**: Predictions are estimates. Always watch for actual heat signs.

#### Dashboard Heat Predictions

![Screenshot: Dashboard showing upcoming heats widget]

**From Dashboard:**

- See all females' predicted heats
- Days until next heat
- Sorted by date
- Color-coded urgency:
  - ðŸ”´ Red: Within 7 days
  - ðŸŸ¡ Orange: Within 30 days
  - ðŸŸ¢ Green: 30+ days away

### Setting Heat Cycle Reminders

#### Automatic Reminders

**System Sends Alerts:**

- 30 days before predicted heat
- 7 days before predicted heat
- When heat is predicted to start

**Notification Channels:**

- Email notifications
- In-app notifications
- Calendar integration (optional)

#### Manual Reminders

**Create Custom Reminders:**

1. Open dog profile
2. Go to Calendar/Reminders
3. Click "Add Reminder"
4. Select "Heat Cycle Check"
5. Set date
6. Add notes
7. Save

**Good Reminder Times:**

- Monthly checks for signs
- Pre-breeding health checks
- Stud service booking dates

### Breeding Planning with Heat Cycles

#### Optimal Breeding Times

**General Guidelines:**

- Day 10-14 of heat cycle
- When discharge lightens
- Female stands for male
- Progesterone testing confirms

**Planning Steps:**

1. Review heat cycle history
2. Note predicted heat date
3. Book stud service in advance
4. Schedule progesterone tests
5. Set reminders for breeding window

#### Tracking Breeding Attempts

**Record Breeding:**

1. During heat cycle, note breeding date
2. Add to heat cycle notes
3. Link to breeding record
4. Calculate expected due date (63 days)
5. Create litter record

![Screenshot: Heat cycle with breeding information linked]

### Managing Irregular Cycles

#### Identifying Issues

**Red Flags:**

- Cycles less than 4 months apart
- Cycles more than 12 months apart
- Split heats (heat stops and restarts)
- Very short heats (less than 5 days)
- No heats by age 24 months

**What to Do:**

1. Document all observations
2. Record in notes
3. Consult veterinarian
4. Consider hormone testing
5. Update dog's health records

#### Silent Heats

**What Are Silent Heats?**

- Ovulation occurs
- No visible signs
- Can still conceive
- More common in some breeds

**How to Track:**

- Regular progesterone testing
- Veterinary monitoring
- Blood tests every 2-3 months
- Note in dog's profile

### Heat Cycle and Health

#### Normal vs. Concerning

**Normal Heat Cycle:**

- Clear to bloody discharge
- Mild to moderate swelling
- Normal appetite and energy
- Attracts male dogs
- Lasts 2-3 weeks total

**Concerning Signs:**

- Foul-smelling discharge
- Excessive bleeding
- Lethargy or fever
- Loss of appetite
- Prolonged heat (4+ weeks)

**Action Required:**

- Contact veterinarian
- Record symptoms in health tracking
- Don't breed if abnormal
- Follow vet recommendations

### Age-Related Considerations

#### First Heat

**Typical Age:**

- Small breeds: 6-12 months
- Medium breeds: 8-14 months
- Large breeds: 10-18 months
- Giant breeds: 18-24 months

**Best Practices:**

- Record first heat date
- Note dog's age at first heat
- Don't breed on first heat
- Wait until physical maturity

#### Senior Dogs

**Aging Considerations:**

- Dogs don't go through menopause
- Cycles may become irregular
- Longer intervals between heats
- Retirement recommendations:
  - Small breeds: 7-8 years
  - Large breeds: 5-6 years

### Practice Exercises

**Exercise 1: Add First Heat Cycle**

1. Select a female dog
2. Go to Heat Cycles tab
3. Click "+ Add Heat Cycle"
4. Enter start date (use past date)
5. Add notes about heat intensity
6. Save record

**Exercise 2: Add Multiple Historical Heats**

1. Same dog as Exercise 1
2. Add heat cycle from 6 months before first
3. Add another from 6 months before that
4. Check predicted next heat date
5. Note the average cycle length calculated

**Exercise 3: Explore Dashboard Predictions**

1. Return to Dashboard
2. Find "Upcoming Heats" widget
3. Identify which dogs are due soon
4. Click on a dog to view details
5. Review heat cycle history

**Exercise 4: Link Breeding to Heat Cycle**

1. Open a heat cycle record
2. Add breeding information in notes
3. Record stud used
4. Note optimal breeding days
5. Save with breeding details

### Tooltips and Quick Help

> ðŸ“Œ **Quick Access**: Click the ðŸ”´ icon next to any female dog's name to quickly add a heat cycle

> ðŸ“Š **Data Insights**: The more heats you track, the more accurate predictions become

> ðŸ”” **Smart Reminders**: Enable email notifications in Settings to never miss a heat cycle

> ðŸ“± **Mobile Tip**: Take photos of your heat tracking calendar and upload to notes

### Knowledge Check

- â˜ I can record a heat cycle with start date
- â˜ I understand the four stages of heat
- â˜ I can view heat cycle predictions
- â˜ I know how to link breeding to heat cycles
- â˜ I can identify irregular cycle patterns
- â˜ I understand when to breed and when not to

## Lesson 8: Pedigree Trees

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- View interactive pedigree trees
- Navigate multi-generation pedigrees
- Export pedigree documents
- Add parents to dogs
- Build complete family trees
- Share pedigrees with buyers

### Understanding Pedigrees

#### What is a Pedigree?

A pedigree is a family tree showing:

- **Ancestors**: Parents, grandparents, great-grandparents
- **Lineage**: Bloodlines and breeding history
- **Titles**: Championships and achievements
- **Health**: Genetic testing results
- **Registration**: Official registration numbers

**Standard Pedigree Levels:**

- **3-Generation**: Dog, parents, grandparents
- **4-Generation**: Adds great-grandparents
- **5-Generation**: Adds great-great-grandparents

> ðŸ’¡ **Why Pedigrees Matter**: Buyers want to see quality bloodlines, health clearances, and titled ancestors

### Viewing Pedigrees

![Screenshot: Pedigree page showing navigation]

#### Accessing Pedigrees

**Method 1: From Pedigrees Page**

1. Click **"Pedigrees"** in sidebar
2. See all dogs with pedigrees
3. Click any dog to view their pedigree
4. Interactive tree displays

**Method 2: From Dog Profile**

1. Open any dog's profile
2. Click **"Pedigree"** tab
3. Pedigree tree appears
4. Navigate from there

**Method 3: Quick View**

1. From Dogs list
2. Click ðŸ“Š pedigree icon next to dog name
3. Pedigree opens in modal
4. Full screen option available

### Interactive Pedigree Features

![Screenshot: Interactive pedigree tree with clickable cards]

#### Pedigree Card Layout

**Each Dog Card Shows:**

- Name (top)
- Sex indicator (color: ðŸ’™ male, ðŸ’– female)
- Registration number
- Color/markings
- Titles (if any)
- Photo thumbnail
- Click to expand details

**Color Coding:**

- **Blue cards**: Male dogs
- **Pink cards**: Female dogs
- **Gray cards**: Unknown/missing information
- **Gold border**: Titled dogs

#### Navigation Features

**Clicking a Dog Card:**

- Opens detailed profile
- Shows full information
- Links to that dog's page
- View their pedigree
- See offspring

**Zoom Controls:**

- ðŸ” Zoom in: See details closer
- ðŸ” Zoom out: See full tree
- â†”ï¸ Fit to screen: Optimal view
- ðŸ–±ï¸ Drag to pan: Move around large pedigrees

**Generation Toggle:**

- Switch between 3, 4, 5 generations
- More generations = more ancestors
- Scroll horizontally for wide trees

### Building Pedigrees

#### Adding Parent Information

**Setting Sire (Father):**

1. Edit dog profile
2. Find "Sire" field
3. Click dropdown
4. Select from your dogs OR
5. Click "Add External Dog"
6. Enter sire's information
7. Save

**Setting Dam (Mother):**

1. Same process as sire
2. Find "Dam" field
3. Select from your dogs OR
4. Add external dam
5. Enter information
6. Save

> ðŸ’¡ **Tip**: You can add dogs you don't own (external dogs) to complete pedigrees

#### External Dogs

**When to Use External Dogs:**

- Stud services from other breeders
- Dogs you used but don't own
- Historical pedigree information
- Import from registries

**Adding External Dog:**

1. Click "Add External Dog" in parent field
2. Enter full information:
   - Name (required)
   - Registration number
   - Breed
   - Sex
   - Color
   - Titles
   - Owner/breeder name (optional)
   - Health clearances (optional)
3. Save
4. Links to your dog's pedigree

**External Dog Properties:**

- Marked as "External"
- Shows in pedigrees
- Cannot be edited like your dogs
- No offspring tracking
- Pedigree view only

### Pedigree Information Details

![Screenshot: Expanded pedigree card showing all details]

#### Essential Information

**Registration Numbers**

- AKC/CKC numbers
- Other registry numbers
- Import registration
- Display in standard format

**Titles and Achievements**

- Champion (Ch.)
- Grand Champion (GCh.)
- Obedience titles
- Working titles
- International titles
- Custom titles

**Health Clearances**

- OFA Hip/Elbow ratings
- Eye clearances (CERF)
- Heart clearances
- DNA test results
- Display as icons/badges

**Color Genetics**

- Coat color
- Pattern information
- Genetic code (if known)
- Helps predict puppy colors

### Exporting Pedigrees

#### Export Options

![Screenshot: Export pedigree dialog with options]

**Export Button Location:**

1. Open any pedigree view
2. Click **"Export"** button (top right)
3. Select format
4. Choose options
5. Download

**Available Formats:**

**1. PDF Document**

- Professional layout
- Printable quality
- Include photos option
- Include health clearances
- Custom header/footer
- Breeder logo
- Use cases: Buyer packets, printed records

**2. Image (PNG)**

- High resolution
- Transparent background option
- Social media ready
- Website display
- Use cases: Online sharing, graphics

**3. Text Format**

- Simple text list
- Registration numbers included
- Easy to copy/paste
- Email friendly
- Use cases: Quick sharing, records

#### Customizing Exports

**Include Options:**

- â˜‘ Photos (adds dog images)
- â˜‘ Registration numbers
- â˜‘ Titles and achievements
- â˜‘ Health clearances
- â˜‘ DNA test results
- â˜‘ Breeder information
- â˜‘ Color genetics
- â˜‘ Date generated

**Layout Options:**

- Portrait or landscape
- Number of generations (3-5)
- Card size (small, medium, large)
- Color scheme
- Font style

**Branding:**

- Add kennel logo
- Custom header text
- Footer information
- Watermark (optional)

### Sharing Pedigrees

#### With Puppy Buyers

**Best Practices:**

1. Export as PDF with all details
2. Include in puppy packet
3. Highlight titled ancestors
4. Show health clearances
5. Explain significant ancestors

**What Buyers Look For:**

- Champion bloodlines
- Health testing
- Breed type consistency
- Genetic diversity
- Notable achievements

#### Public Sharing

**Share Link Feature:**

1. Open pedigree
2. Click "Share" button
3. Toggle "Make Public"
4. Copy share link
5. Post anywhere

**Public Pedigree Settings:**

- Choose visibility level
- Include/exclude contact info
- Watermark option
- Expiration date (optional)
- View count tracking

> âš ï¸ **Privacy**: Only share pedigrees you have permission to share

### Advanced Pedigree Features

#### Coefficient of Inbreeding (COI)

**What is COI?**

- Measures genetic similarity
- Shows inbreeding level
- Percentage format (0-100%)
- Lower is more diverse

**COI Ranges:**

- 0-5%: Diverse, low inbreeding
- 5-10%: Moderate
- 10-15%: Higher (some breeds acceptable)
- 15%+: High inbreeding, caution

**How It's Calculated:**

- Analyzes common ancestors
- Looks back 5+ generations
- Automatic calculation
- Updates as you add ancestors

![Screenshot: COI display in pedigree]

#### Ancestor Analysis

**Common Ancestors Highlighted:**

- Shows where dogs appear multiple times
- Indicates linebreeding
- Helps understand genetics
- Plan future breedings

**Pedigree Statistics:**

- Unique dogs count
- Common ancestors
- Generation completeness
- Title percentage
- Health clearance percentage

### Searching Pedigrees

#### Find Specific Dogs

**Pedigree Search:**

1. Go to Pedigrees page
2. Use search bar
3. Enter dog name, registration, or keyword
4. Results show all matches
5. Click to view pedigree

**Filter Options:**

- By breed
- By registry
- Titled dogs only
- Health cleared only
- Your dogs vs external
- Date range

### Pedigree Maintenance

#### Keeping Pedigrees Current

**Regular Updates:**

- Add new titles as earned
- Update health clearances
- Correct registration numbers
- Add missing ancestors
- Update photos

**Data Quality:**

- Verify spelling
- Check registration numbers
- Confirm parentage
- Validate titles
- Cross-reference registries

#### Importing Pedigree Data

**From Registries:**

- Some registries allow export
- Import CSV or text format
- Bulk add ancestors
- Auto-populate information
- Verify after import

**From Other Software:**

- Export from previous system
- Match data format
- Import process available
- Technical support for large imports

### Practice Exercises

**Exercise 1: View a Complete Pedigree**

1. Go to Pedigrees page
2. Select a dog with parents entered
3. View 3-generation pedigree
4. Switch to 4-generation view
5. Click on each ancestor card
6. Note missing information

**Exercise 2: Add Parent Information**

1. Choose a dog without parents
2. Edit dog profile
3. Add sire information (create external if needed)
4. Add dam information
5. Save and view updated pedigree
6. See 2 generations now

**Exercise 3: Export a Pedigree**

1. Open a dog's pedigree
2. Click "Export" button
3. Select PDF format
4. Enable all options (photos, health, etc.)
5. Generate and download
6. Review PDF quality

**Exercise 4: Build 5-Generation Pedigree**

1. Start with one dog
2. Add parents (generation 2)
3. Add grandparents (generation 3)
4. Add great-grandparents (generation 4)
5. Add great-great-grandparents (generation 5)
6. View complete 5-generation tree

**Exercise 5: Calculate COI**

1. Find a dog with 4+ generation pedigree
2. View pedigree
3. Look for COI calculation
4. Note any common ancestors
5. Understand inbreeding level

### Tooltips and Quick Help

> ðŸŽ¨ **Visual Tip**: Gold borders indicate titled dogs - hover to see titles

> ðŸ§¬ **Genetics**: Click DNA icon on any card to see genetic test results

> ðŸ“¸ **Photos**: Drag and drop photos onto pedigree cards to update images

> ðŸ”— **Linking**: External dogs can be converted to owned dogs later

> ðŸ“Š **Analysis**: Use pedigree reports to identify valuable bloodlines

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Pedigree shows incomplete**

- Solution: Add missing parent information to fill gaps

**Problem: Can't find external dog**

- Solution: Check spelling, try alternate names, check registration number

**Problem: Export PDF is blank**

- Solution: Ensure dog has parents, try different browser, clear cache

**Problem: COI not calculating**

- Solution: Need at least 3 complete generations for accurate COI

### Knowledge Check

- â˜ I can view and navigate pedigree trees
- â˜ I know how to add parent information
- â˜ I can create external dogs for pedigrees
- â˜ I can export pedigrees in multiple formats
- â˜ I understand COI and what it means
- â˜ I can share pedigrees with buyers
- â˜ I know how to interpret pedigree information

# Module 3: Litter Management

## Lesson 9: Creating and Managing Litters

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Create new litter records
- Set breeding and whelping dates
- Manage litter status through lifecycle
- Track litter milestones
- Link sire and dam
- Update litter information
- Archive completed litters

### Understanding Litter Management

#### Why Track Litters?

Comprehensive litter management helps you:

- **Organize Information**: All puppy data in one place
- **Track Progress**: From breeding to placement
- **Maintain Records**: Complete breeding history
- **Buyer Communication**: Share litter updates
- **Financial Tracking**: Sales and expenses per litter
- **Health Monitoring**: Group health tracking
- **Planning**: Schedule care and appointments

> ðŸ’¡ **Best Practice**: Create litter record immediately after successful breeding confirmation

### Creating a New Litter

![Screenshot: Add Litter button on Litters page]

#### Accessing Litter Creation

**Method 1: From Litters Page**

1. Click **"Litters"** in sidebar
2. Click **"+ Add Litter"** button (top right)
3. Litter creation form opens

**Method 2: From Dashboard**

1. Find "Quick Actions" widget
2. Click **"Add Litter"**
3. Form opens directly

**Method 3: From Dog Profile**

1. Open female dog's profile
2. Go to **"Litters"** tab
3. Click **"+ New Litter"**
4. Dam pre-selected

### Litter Creation Form

![Screenshot: New litter creation form with all fields]

#### Essential Information

**1. Litter Name** (Required)

- Unique identifier for this litter
- Common formats:
  - Seasonal: "Summer 2025 Litter"
  - Sequential: "Bella's 3rd Litter"
  - Themed: "Rainbow Litter"
  - Date-based: "March 2025 Golden Litter"
- Make it memorable and descriptive
- Will appear in all records

> ðŸ’¡ **Naming Tip**: Include dam's name or season for easy identification

**2. Dam (Mother)** (Required)

- Select from your female dogs
- Dropdown shows all active dams
- Shows dog's name and age
- Must have valid dog record first

**Search Feature:**

- Type to filter list
- Shows recent selections first
- Can't proceed without selecting

**3. Sire (Father)** (Required)

- Select from your dogs OR
- Choose external stud
- Shows name and registration
- Links to dog profile if owned

**External Stud:**

- Check "External Stud" box
- Enter stud's information:
  - Name
  - Registration number
  - Owner/breeder contact
  - Stud fee amount
  - Health clearances
- Saved for future use

**4. Breeding Date** (Required)

- Date of successful breeding
- Use calendar picker
- Format: MM/DD/YYYY
- Can enter multiple breeding dates if applicable

> ðŸ“… **Calculation**: System automatically calculates due date (breeding date + 63 days)

**5. Expected Due Date**

- Auto-calculated from breeding date
- Editable if needed
- Average gestation: 63 days (range: 58-68)
- Used for reminders and planning

**6. Date of Birth** (Optional initially)

- Add when puppies are born
- Updates litter status
- Triggers milestone tracking
- Required for puppy records

#### Additional Information

**Litter Status**

- **Planned**: Breeding scheduled or just occurred
- **Expected**: Pregnancy confirmed
- **Born**: Puppies delivered
- **Weaned**: Puppies weaned from mother
- **Ready**: Available for pickup
- **Placed**: All puppies in homes
- **Archived**: Historical record

> ðŸ”„ **Status Flow**: Plan â†’ Expected â†’ Born â†’ Weaned â†’ Ready â†’ Placed â†’ Archived

**Number of Puppies**

- Total born (including deceased)
- Living puppies count
- Updates as puppies added
- Shows in litter overview

**Expected/Actual Count:**

- Expected: Estimated from ultrasound/x-ray
- Actual: Count after birth
- Difference tracked for records

**Pickup Ready Date**

- When puppies available for homes
- Usually 8-12 weeks from birth
- Used for buyer communication
- Triggers ready notifications

**Litter Photos**

- Upload multiple photos
- Show litter together
- Update throughout growth
- Display on public pages
- Drag to reorder

**Photo Tips:**

- First photo is featured image
- Include group shots
- Add weekly progression photos
- Name photos with dates
- Max 20 photos per litter

**Notes Section**

- Breeding details
- Whelping notes
- Special considerations
- Health observations
- Buyer inquiries
- Any relevant information

**Example Notes:**

```
Breeding: Natural tie, 15 minutes
Progesterone: 8.2 ng/ml on 11/15
Ultrasound confirmed 6 puppies on 12/10
Whelping: Natural delivery, no complications
All puppies nursing well
```

### Saving the Litter

**Before Saving Checklist:**

- â˜ Unique litter name entered
- â˜ Dam selected
- â˜ Sire selected
- â˜ Breeding date entered
- â˜ Expected due date confirmed
- â˜ Status appropriate
- â˜ Photos uploaded (optional but recommended)

**Save Process:**

1. Review all information
2. Scroll to bottom
3. Click **"Create Litter"** button
4. Confirmation message appears
5. Redirects to litter details page

### Litter Details Page

![Screenshot: Complete litter details page layout]

#### Overview Section

**Top Card Information:**

- Litter name prominently displayed
- Featured photo
- Current status badge
- Key dates at a glance:
  - Breeding date
  - Due date
  - Birth date (if born)
  - Pickup ready date

**Quick Stats:**

- ðŸ‘¶ Total puppies
- âœ… Available puppies
- ðŸ  Placed puppies
- â° Age (weeks and days)

**Action Buttons:**

- âœï¸ Edit Litter
- ðŸ• Add Puppy
- ðŸ“„ Generate Documents
- ðŸ”— Share Public Page
- ðŸ“Š View Reports
- ðŸ—‘ï¸ Archive/Delete

#### Parents Section

**Dam (Mother) Card:**

- Photo and name
- Age at breeding
- Registration number
- Click to view full profile
- Shows litter count
- Health clearances

**Sire (Father) Card:**

- Same information as dam
- External stud marked if applicable
- Stud fee information
- Contact owner (if external)

**Genetics Preview:**

- Expected colors
- Size predictions
- Coat type
- Based on parent genetics

### Managing Litter Status

![Screenshot: Status progression timeline]

#### Status Updates

**Changing Status:**

1. Click **"Edit Litter"** button
2. Update **Status** dropdown
3. Adjust dates as needed
4. Add notes about change
5. Save

**Status Triggers:**

**Planned â†’ Expected:**

- Breeding occurred
- Waiting for confirmation
- Trigger: Breeding date entered

**Expected â†’ Born:**

- Pregnancy confirmed
- Puppies expected soon
- Trigger: Update status manually after confirmation

**Born â†’ Weaned:**

- Puppies delivered
- Beginning care schedule
- Trigger: Birth date entered

**Weaned â†’ Ready:**

- Puppies eating independently
- Usually 4-6 weeks old
- Trigger: Manual update

**Ready â†’ Placed:**

- Puppies available for pickup
- Taking deposits/applications
- Trigger: Pickup ready date

**Placed â†’ Archived:**

- All puppies in homes
- Litter complete
- Trigger: All puppies marked as placed

#### Status-Based Features

**Automatic Actions:**

**When Status = Born:**

- âœ… Puppy adding enabled
- âœ… Weight tracking activated
- âœ… Care schedule starts
- âœ… Milestone tracking begins
- âœ… Buyer notifications sent

**When Status = Ready:**

- âœ… Public page goes live
- âœ… Waitlist notified
- âœ… Contracts generated
- âœ… Pickup scheduling enabled

**When Status = Placed:**

- âœ… Sales finalized
- âœ… Documents issued
- âœ… Follow-up reminders created
- âœ… Statistics updated

### Editing Litter Information

#### What You Can Edit

**Always Editable:**

- Litter name
- Status
- Notes
- Photos (add, remove, reorder)
- Pickup ready date
- Contact preferences

**Carefully Edit:**

- Breeding date (affects due date)
- Due date
- Birth date (affects puppy ages)
- Sire/Dam (breaks existing links)

**Cannot Edit:**

- System-generated ID
- Creation date
- Historical puppy records

> âš ï¸ **Warning**: Changing birth date affects all puppy ages and milestone tracking

#### Edit Process

1. Open litter details page
2. Click **"Edit Litter"** button
3. Form opens with current data
4. Make changes
5. Review carefully
6. Click **"Save Changes"**
7. Confirmation appears

### Litter Timeline

![Screenshot: Interactive litter timeline]

#### Milestone Tracking

**Automatic Milestones:**

- Breeding date
- Due date
- Birth date
- Eyes open (10-14 days)
- Ears open (2-3 weeks)
- First solid food (3-4 weeks)
- Weaning complete (6-8 weeks)
- First vaccinations (6-8 weeks)
- Ready for homes (8-12 weeks)

**Custom Milestones:**

- Add your own events
- Vet visits
- Microchipping
- Evaluation dates
- Special achievements
- Photos/videos

**Timeline View:**

- Chronological event list
- Past, present, future
- Photo attachments
- Notes on each milestone
- Shareable with buyers

### Litter Care Schedule

#### Setting Up Care Routines

**Access Care Schedule:**

1. Litter details page
2. Click **"Care Schedule"** tab
3. Select template OR create custom
4. Customize for this litter
5. Save and activate

**Template Options:**

- Newborn puppies (0-2 weeks)
- Transitional period (2-4 weeks)
- Socialization period (4-8 weeks)
- Pre-placement (8-12 weeks)
- Custom schedule

**Schedule Includes:**

- Feeding times and amounts
- Weight check frequency
- Cleaning tasks
- Temperature monitoring
- Socialization activities
- Training exercises
- Health checks

> See Lesson 12 for detailed care schedule management

### Multiple Litters

#### Managing Multiple Active Litters

**Overview Dashboard:**

- See all active litters
- Filter by status
- Sort by due date or age
- Quick status updates

**Comparison View:**

- Side-by-side litter stats
- Age comparisons
- Available puppy counts
- Financial summaries

**Best Practices:**

- Unique naming conventions
- Color-code by season
- Separate care schedules
- Clear photo organization
- Regular status updates

### Archiving Litters

#### When to Archive

**Archive When:**

- All puppies placed
- Follow-up complete
- No pending actions
- Records finalized
- Financial settled

**What Archiving Does:**

- Removes from active list
- Keeps all data
- Maintains searchability
- Preserves history
- Doesn't delete anything

#### Archive Process

1. Open litter details
2. All puppies must be placed
3. Click **"Archive Litter"** button
4. Confirm archiving
5. Moved to archived section

**Accessing Archived Litters:**

- Go to Litters page
- Toggle "Show Archived"
- View all historical litters
- Can unarchive if needed

### Practice Exercises

**Exercise 1: Create Your First Litter**

1. Go to Litters page

5. Select any sire

6. Complete litter creation
7. View sire information

2. Click "Edit Litter"
3. Upload 3 different photos
4. Drag to reorder them
5. Make best photo first
6. Save and view featured image

1. Create test litter with past dates
2. Set breeding date: 70 days ago
3. Update status to "Born"
4. Enter birth date: 7 days ago
5. View how dates affect status
6. Check milestone timeline

### Tooltips and Quick Help

> ðŸ“… **Due Date Calculator**: System uses 63-day average, but normal range is 58-68 days

> ðŸ”” **Reminders**: Automatic reminders sent at 7 days and 1 day before due date

> ðŸ“¸ **Photo Tip**: Take weekly group photos to track growth progression

> ðŸ’° **Financial**: Link expenses to litters for accurate per-litter cost tracking

> ðŸŒ **Public Page**: Each litter gets unique public URL for buyer viewing

> ðŸ“‹ **Templates**: Save frequently used litter setups as templates

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Can't select dam or sire**

- Solution: Must add dog to system first, then create litter

**Problem: Due date wrong**

- Solution: Edit breeding date or manually adjust due date

**Problem: Can't add puppies**

- Solution: Must enter birth date and change status to "Born" first

**Problem: Litter not showing on dashboard**

- Solution: Check status filter, ensure litter not archived

**Problem: Lost litter data**

- Solution: Check archived litters, use search function

## Lesson 10: Puppy Tracking

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Add individual puppies to litters
- Assign identification methods
- Track puppy growth and development
- Record puppy-specific health information
- Assign puppies to buyers
- Manage puppy availability status
- Export puppy information

### Understanding Puppy Records

#### Why Track Individual Puppies?

Individual puppy tracking enables:

- **Unique Identification**: Distinguish each puppy
- **Growth Monitoring**: Track weight and development
- **Health Records**: Individual medical history
- **Buyer Assignment**: Match puppies to families
- **Sales Tracking**: Monitor deposits and payments
- **Documentation**: Generate puppy-specific papers
- **Follow-up**: Post-placement communication

> ðŸ’¡ **Key Point**: Each puppy is a complete record linked to their litter

### Adding Puppies to a Litter

![Screenshot: Add Puppy button in litter details]

#### Prerequisites

**Before Adding Puppies:**

- â˜ Litter must exist
- â˜ Birth date must be entered
- â˜ Status should be "Born" or later
- â˜ Have identification system ready

#### Access Puppy Creation

**Method 1: From Litter Details**

1. Open litter details page
2. Scroll to "Puppies" section
3. Click **"+ Add Puppy"** button
4. Puppy form opens

**Method 2: Quick Add**

1. From Litters list
2. Click âž• icon on litter row
3. Quick add form appears
4. Streamlined puppy creation

**Method 3: Bulk Add**

1. Open litter details
2. Click **"Add Multiple Puppies"**
3. Enter total count
4. Creates placeholder records
5. Edit individual details later

### Puppy Information Form

![Screenshot: Complete puppy creation form]

#### Essential Information

**1. Puppy Name** (Required)

- Temporary or permanent name
- Common temporary names:
  - Colors: "Blue", "Yellow", "Pink"
  - Physical: "Big Boy", "Tiny", "Floof"
  - Collar: "Blue Collar", "Green Girl"
  - Registration: Will add later

**Naming Tips:**

- Use identifying features initially
- Update when buyer names puppy
- Keep track of multiple similar puppies
- Registration name different from call name

**2. Sex** (Required)

- Male or Female
- Determined at birth
- Cannot change after setting
- Affects some tracking features

**3. Identification** (Important)

- **Collar Color**: Primary ID method
  - Select from color list
  - Match to physical collar
  - Photo with collar recommended
- **Markings**: Unique identifiers

  - White chest patch
  - Facial markings
  - Tail tip color
  - Paw patterns
  - Detailed description helps

- **Temporary Mark**: Short-term ID
  - Nail polish on nail
  - Ribbon color
  - Washable marker
  - Until collars fit

> ðŸ’¡ **Best Practice**: Use multiple ID methods - collar + markings description + photo

**4. Birth Weight** (Recommended)

- Measured at or shortly after birth
- In ounces or grams
- Baseline for growth tracking
- Helps identify concerns early

**Typical Birth Weights by Breed:**

- Small breeds: 3-5 oz
- Medium breeds: 8-16 oz
- Large breeds: 1-2 lbs
- Giant breeds: 1.5-2.5 lbs

**5. Color** (Required)

- Coat color at birth
- May change as puppy grows
- Use breed-standard terms
- Examples: Black, Chocolate, Red, Cream, Parti-color

**6. Availability Status** (Required)

- **Available**: Ready for reservation
- **Reserved**: Deposit received
- **Placed**: Puppy in new home
- **Kept**: Staying with you
- **Pending**: Awaiting decision
- **Unavailable**: Not for sale

**Status Affects:**

- Public website display
- Waitlist notifications
- Buyer communications
- Financial tracking

#### Additional Information

**Microchip Number**

- Enter after microchipping (usually 6-8 weeks)
- 15-digit number
- Links to registry
- Required for travel in many areas
- Searchable in system

**Registration Information**

- Registration number (AKC, CKC, etc.)
- Application number
- Registration name
- Registration date
- Papers issued date

**Price**

- Base price for this puppy
- Can differ by:
  - Sex (males often more)
  - Color (rare colors premium)
  - Markings (desirable patterns)
  - Quality (show vs pet)
  - Breeding rights
- Displays on buyer documents

**Special Notes**

- Whelping notes (first born, breech, etc.)
- Personality traits
- Development observations
- Health notes
- Buyer preferences
- Anything unique about this puppy

**Example Notes:**

```
First born, strong nurser
Extra white on chest
Most vocal of litter
Potential show prospect - excellent structure
Reserved for working home
```

### Puppy Photos

![Screenshot: Puppy photo gallery with upload interface]

#### Photo Management

**Uploading Photos:**

1. In puppy form, find "Photos" section
2. Click "Upload Photo" or drag files
3. Select multiple photos
4. Photos appear in gallery
5. Reorder by dragging
6. First photo is featured image

**Photo Recommendations:**

- Weekly progression photos
- Multiple angles (front, side, rear)
- Standing pose
- With collar visible
- Comparison with littermates
- Action shots for personality
- With size reference

**Photo Organization:**

- Date photos in filename
- Name format: "PuppyName_Week3_Front.jpg"
- Keep originals backed up
- Add captions in photo description
- Maximum 50 photos per puppy

### Saving Puppy Record

**Completion Checklist:**

- â˜ Name entered
- â˜ Sex selected
- â˜ Identification method assigned
- â˜ Birth weight recorded
- â˜ Color entered
- â˜ Availability status set
- â˜ At least one photo uploaded

**Save Process:**

1. Review all information
2. Click **"Add Puppy"** button
3. Puppy added to litter
4. Returns to litter details
5. Puppy appears in list

### Puppy List View

![Screenshot: Litter puppy list with cards]

#### Puppy Card Layout

**Each Puppy Card Shows:**

- Featured photo
- Name prominently

- âœï¸ Edit puppy details

- ðŸ—‘ï¸ Remove puppy

- By sex (male/female)
- By availability

- By collar color
- Sort by weight, name, or birth order

### Editing Puppy Information

#### What to Update

**Regular Updates:**

- Weight (weekly or more often)
- Photos (new ones frequently)
- Availability status (as reserved)
- Buyer assignment (when selected)
- Registration info (when received)
- Notes (ongoing observations)

**Occasional Updates:**

- Microchip number (when chipped)
- Name (if buyer renames)
- Price (adjustments)
- Color (if changes with age)

#### Edit Process

1. Click puppy card or name
2. Opens puppy detail view
3. Click **"Edit"** button
4. Update information
5. Save changes
6. View updated puppy profile

### Puppy Development Tracking

![Screenshot: Puppy development timeline]

#### Growth Milestones

**Automatic Tracking:**

- Birth (day 0)
- Eyes open (10-14 days)
- Ears open (14-18 days)
- First steps (2-3 weeks)
- Teeth eruption (3-4 weeks)
- Weaning start (4-5 weeks)
- Ready for homes (8-10 weeks)

**Recording Milestones:**

1. Puppy detail page
2. Go to **"Milestones"** tab
3. Check off when reached
4. Add date and notes
5. Photos optional
6. Automatically tracked

**Individual vs. Litter:**

- Some milestones litter-wide
- Some individual (first teeth, etc.)
- Both types tracked
- Helps identify delays

#### Development Notes

**What to Record:**

- Personality emerging
- Social behaviors
- Activity level
- Vocalizations
- Play style
- Food preferences
- Reactions to new things

**Uses for Notes:**

- Match puppy to buyer
- Identify potential issues
- Track socialization progress
- Share with buyers
- Support puppy placement decisions

### Puppy Health Tracking

#### Individual Health Records

**Access Health Tab:**

1. Open puppy detail page
2. Click **"Health"** tab
3. All health records appear
4. Add new records

**Health Record Types:**

**Vaccinations**

- Track puppy vaccine series
- Due dates calculated
- Multiple vaccines per visit
- Certificate generation
- Share with buyers

**Deworming**

- Schedule: 2, 4, 6, 8 weeks
- Product used
- Dosage by weight
- Administrator
- Next due date

**Vet Checks**

- Health examinations
- Any treatments
- Medications
- Concerns addressed
- Vet notes

**Health Issues**

- Any problems
- Symptoms
- Diagnosis
- Treatment
- Resolution
- Prevention notes

> See Lesson 11 for detailed health monitoring

### Assigning Puppies to Buyers

![Screenshot: Assign buyer dialog]

#### Buyer Assignment Process

**Prerequisites:**

- Buyer record exists in Customers
- Puppy status is Available
- Deposit received (recommended)

**Assignment Steps:**

1. Open puppy details
2. Click **"Assign to Buyer"** button
3. Search for customer
4. Select buyer
5. Enter deposit amount
6. Set pickup date
7. Add contract details
8. Save assignment

**What Changes:**

- Puppy status â†’ "Reserved"
- Buyer name shows on card
- Contract generation available
- Financial tracking updated
- Buyer notifications sent
- Public listing updated

**Reassigning Puppies:**

- If buyer backs out
- Click "Unassign" or "Reassign"
- Refund deposit (track separately)
- Return status to "Available"
- Notify waitlist

### Puppy Availability Management

#### Status Definitions

**Available**

- Not yet spoken for
- Accepting applications
- Shows on public page
- Waitlist can view
- Full details visible

**Reserved**

- Deposit received
- Buyer assigned
- Removed from public listing
- Still visible to assigned buyer
- Awaiting final payment

**Placed**

- Puppy has gone home
- Full payment received
- Contract signed
- Ownership transferred
- Follow-up phase begins

**Kept**

- Remaining with breeder
- Not for sale
- Potential breeding prospect
- Guardian home possibility
- May change later

**Pending**

- Decision in progress
- Evaluating for show/breeding
- Awaiting buyer approval
- Temporary status
- Should resolve within days

**Unavailable**

- Not available for any reason
- Health concerns
- Already committed
- Other circumstances
- Not displayed publicly

#### Bulk Status Updates

**Update Multiple Puppies:**

1. Litter details page
2. Select multiple puppies (checkboxes)
3. Click "Bulk Actions"
4. Select "Update Status"
5. Choose new status
6. Apply to selected
7. All update simultaneously

**Use Cases:**

- Mark all available at once
- Update when litter ready
- Quick status changes
- Efficient management

### Generating Puppy Documents

![Screenshot: Document generation menu]

#### Available Documents

**Puppy Information Sheet**

- Photo and details
- Parents information
- Health records
- Care instructions
- Feeding schedule
- Buyer welcome packet

**Health Certificate**

- Vaccination records
- Deworming schedule
- Vet check information
- Health guarantee
- Official format

**Registration Application**

- Pre-filled with puppy info
- Parents details
- Breeder information
- AKC/CKC formats
- Ready to submit

**Sales Contract**

- Customized per puppy
- Buyer information
- Price and payment
- Health guarantee
- Breeding rights clauses
- Co-ownership terms

> See Lesson 18 for detailed contract generation

1. Open puppy details

   - PDF summary
   - Data spreadsheet
   - Photo gallery ZIP
4. Download

**Litter Puppy Export:**

1. Litter details page
2. Click "Export All Puppies"
3. Options:
   - Spreadsheet (all data)
   - PDF booklet (all puppies)
   - Photo package (all photos)
   - Summary report
4. Generate and download

**Uses:**

- Backup records
- Share with co-breeder
- Provide to buyers
- Print for files
- Submit to registry

### Practice Exercises

**Exercise 1: Add Single Puppy**

   - Red Collar (Female, 11 oz, Golden, Available)
   - Green Collar (Male, 13 oz, Dark Golden, Reserved)
   - Pink Collar (Female, 10 oz, Light Golden, Available)
3. Use different collar colors
4. Upload photos for each
5. Save all

**Exercise 3: Track Puppy Weight**

1. Select Blue Collar puppy
2. Go to Health tab
3. Click "Add Weight"
4. Enter today's date
5. Enter weight: 24 oz (if 1 week old)
6. Add note: "Good weight gain"
7. Save

**Exercise 4: Assign Puppy to Buyer**

5. Add note: "Both eyes fully open, no issues"
6. Add photo (optional)

### Tooltips and Quick Help

> ðŸŽ¨ **Color Coding**: Use consistent collar colors across litters for easier tracking

> âš–ï¸ **Weight Tracking**: Weigh puppies daily for first 2 weeks, then weekly

> ðŸ“¸ **Photo Schedule**: Take photos at 1, 2, 4, 6, 8 weeks minimum

> ðŸ’° **Pricing**: Set base price but can adjust per puppy for quality, color, etc.

> ðŸ“‹ **Identification**: Combination of collar + markings + photos is most reliable

> ðŸ”” **Notifications**: System alerts when puppies reach vaccination milestones

> ðŸ“Š **Charts**: Weight charts automatically generated from weight entries

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Can't add puppies to litter**

- Solution: Ensure litter has birth date entered and status is "Born" or later

**Problem: Puppies all look the same**

- Solution: Use unique collar colors and take detailed marking photos

**Problem: Lost track of which puppy is which**

- Solution: Review marking notes and photos, use process of elimination

**Problem: Puppy weight chart not showing**

- Solution: Need at least 2 weight entries to generate chart

**Problem: Can't assign puppy to buyer**

- Solution: Buyer must exist in Customers, create customer first

**Problem: Wrong sex entered**

- Solution: Contact support - sex changes require admin to prevent errors

### Advanced Tips

**Batch Operations:**

- Use bulk add for large litters
- Update all photos at once
- Export all puppy data together
- Generate all contracts simultaneously

**Organization:**

- Name puppies systematically
- Keep photos organized by week
- Update weights on same schedule
- Review all puppies weekly

**Communication:**

- Share puppy pages with buyers
- Send weekly photo updates
- Update milestones promptly
- Keep notes current for buyer matching

- â˜ I can add individual puppies to a litter
