## Lesson 11: Weight and Health Monitoring

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Record daily/weekly puppy weights
- Interpret weight gain charts
- Identify concerning weight patterns
- Track litter-wide health trends
- Record individual health events
- Monitor developmental milestones
- Generate health reports for buyers
- Set up health monitoring alerts

### Why Monitor Weight and Health?

Consistent monitoring helps you:

- **Early Detection**: Spot problems before they become serious
- **Growth Verification**: Ensure proper development
- **Buyer Confidence**: Show commitment to puppy health
- **Record Keeping**: Complete medical history
- **Comparative Analysis**: Compare to littermates and breed standards
- **Intervention Timing**: Know when vet care needed

> ðŸ’¡ **Critical Period**: First 2 weeks are crucial - daily weight monitoring can save lives

### Puppy Weight Tracking

![Screenshot: Weight tracking interface with chart]

#### Understanding Puppy Growth

**Normal Growth Patterns:**

**Week 1:**

- Should gain weight daily
- Double birth weight by day 10-14
- 5-10% gain per day typical
- Any weight loss concerning

**Weeks 2-4:**

- Rapid growth phase
- Weight triples or quadruples
- 10-15% gain per week
- Eyes and ears open

**Weeks 4-8:**

- Continued steady growth
- Transition to solid food
- Growth rate may slow slightly
- Individual variations appear

**Weeks 8-12:**

- Growth continues
- Weaning complete
- Moving to new homes
- Growth spurts common

**Breed Size Variations:**

- Small breeds: Faster early growth, mature sooner
- Medium breeds: Moderate, steady growth
- Large breeds: Slower growth, longer development
- Giant breeds: Extended growth period (18-24 months)

#### Recording Puppy Weights

![Screenshot: Add weight entry form]

**Access Weight Tracking:**

**Method 1: Individual Puppy**

1. Open puppy detail page
2. Click **"Weight"** tab
3. Click **"Add Weight"** button
4. Enter information
5. Save

**Method 2: Batch Entry (Recommended)**

1. Open litter details page
2. Click **"Record Weights"** button
3. See all puppies in list
4. Enter weight for each
5. Save all at once

**Method 3: Mobile Quick Entry**

1. Use mobile device at scale
2. Quick add weights
3. Minimal taps
4. Syncs automatically

#### Weight Entry Form

**Required Information:**

- **Date**: When weighed
- **Weight**: Amount in oz or grams
- **Puppy**: Which puppy (auto-filled if from puppy page)

**Optional Information:**

- **Time of Day**: Morning, afternoon, evening
- **Before/After Feeding**: Can affect measurement
- **Notes**: Any observations
- **Body Condition Score**: Visual assessment (1-5 scale)

**Unit Selection:**

- Ounces (oz): Common for small puppies
- Grams (g): More precise
- Pounds (lbs): For larger/older puppies
- System converts automatically

> ðŸ’¡ **Consistency Tip**: Use same scale, same time of day, and same conditions for accurate tracking

#### Best Practices for Weighing

**Daily Weighing (Birth - 2 Weeks):**

- Same time each day
- Before feeding for consistency
- Use gram scale for accuracy
- Record immediately
- Note any concerns

**Weekly Weighing (2 Weeks - Placement):**

- Same day each week
- Keep puppy calm
- Weigh multiple times if active
- Average if needed
- Take photos at weigh-in

**Equipment:**

- Digital scale required
- 0.1 oz or 1g precision
- Tare function helpful
- Place bowl/container for small puppies
- Calibrate regularly

**Recording Tips:**

- Keep scale near whelping area
- Use voice notes if needed
- Enter data within 24 hours
- Don't skip days in early weeks
- Note unusual circumstances

### Weight Charts and Analysis

![Screenshot: Interactive weight chart with trend lines]

#### Understanding Weight Charts

**Chart Features:**

**Growth Curve:**

- Line graph showing weight over time
- Each puppy has unique color
- Expected range shown as shaded area
- Trend line indicates direction

**Data Points:**

- Each weight entry is a point
- Hover to see exact values
- Click to view entry details
- Add notes to specific points

**Comparison View:**

- Overlay all littermates
- See relative sizes
- Identify outliers
- Compare to breed standard

**Zoom and Filter:**

- Focus on specific date range
- View individual or group
- Daily, weekly, or monthly view
- Export chart as image

#### Interpreting Growth Patterns

**Healthy Growth Indicators:**

- âœ… Steady upward trend
- âœ… Following expected curve
- âœ… Consistent daily/weekly gains
- âœ… Active and alert puppy
- âœ… Good nursing behavior

**Warning Signs:**

- âš ï¸ Flat or declining weight
- âš ï¸ Sudden drops
- âš ï¸ Falling behind littermates
- âš ï¸ Very slow gain
- âš ï¸ Erratic pattern

**Red Flags - Immediate Action:**

- ðŸ”´ Weight loss in first week
- ðŸ”´ No gain for 24+ hours (newborns)
- ðŸ”´ Dropping below birth weight
- ðŸ”´ Lethargic puppy
- ðŸ”´ Not nursing

#### Failure to Thrive

**Identifying FTT:**

- Not gaining weight appropriately
- Significantly smaller than littermates
- Weak or inactive
- Poor nursing reflex
- Cool to touch

**Common Causes:**

- Insufficient milk production
- Competition from larger siblings
- Congenital defects
- Infections
- Parasites
- Hypothermia

**Intervention Steps:**

1. Isolate from competition
2. Supplement feed if needed
3. Keep warm (90-95Â°F first week)
4. Weigh every 4-6 hours
5. Contact veterinarian
6. Document everything

**Supplemental Feeding:**

- Commercial puppy formula
- Feed every 2-3 hours
- Use puppy bottle or tube (if trained)
- Warm formula to body temperature
- Calculate amount by weight
- Continue monitoring

> âš ï¸ **Emergency**: If puppy loses more than 10% body weight, contact vet immediately

### Litter-Wide Health Monitoring

![Screenshot: Litter health dashboard]

#### Health Overview Dashboard

**Access Litter Health:**

1. Open litter details
2. Click **"Health"** tab
3. Overview appears
4. Individual tracking available

**Dashboard Displays:**

**Weight Statistics:**

- Average litter weight
- Smallest puppy
- Largest puppy
- Weight range
- Average daily gain
- Trends (improving/declining)

**Health Status:**

- All healthy (green)
- Some concerns (yellow)
- Issues present (red)
- Recent vet visits
- Upcoming vaccinations

**Development Milestones:**

- Eyes opened (all/some/none)
- Ears opened
- First teeth
- Walking
- Eating solid food
- Vaccination status

**Alerts and Reminders:**

- Puppies due for weigh-in
- Vaccinations due
- Deworming schedule
- Health checks needed
- Unusual patterns detected

#### Tracking Common Health Events

**Deworming Schedule:**

**Standard Protocol:**

- Week 2: First deworming
- Week 4: Second dose
- Week 6: Third dose
- Week 8: Fourth dose
- Additional as needed

**Recording Deworming:**

1. Litter health tab
2. Click "Add Deworming"
3. Select all puppies OR individual
4. Enter date
5. Product used
6. Dosage (calculated by weight)
7. Administrator
8. Next due date auto-calculated
9. Save

**What to Track:**

- Product name (Pyrantel, Panacur, etc.)
- Dosage per puppy
- Any reactions
- Effectiveness
- Next treatment date

**Vaccination Tracking:**

**Puppy Vaccine Schedule:**

- 6 weeks: DHPP #1 (optional)
- 8 weeks: DHPP #1 or #2
- 12 weeks: DHPP #2 or #3
- 16 weeks: DHPP #3 or #4, Rabies

**Recording Vaccinations:**

1. Health tab â†’ Vaccinations
2. Click "Add Vaccination Event"
3. Select puppies (can multi-select)
4. Choose vaccine type
5. Enter date and vet info
6. Lot number (important!)
7. Next due date
8. Save for all selected

**Batch Vaccination Benefits:**

- Enter once for whole litter
- Consistent records
- Certificate generation
- Reminder automation
- Buyer documentation

> ðŸ’¡ **Tip**: Take photos of vaccine certificates for digital backup

### Individual Puppy Health Issues

![Screenshot: Individual puppy health record]

#### Recording Health Events

**Common Puppy Health Issues:**

**Umbilical Hernias:**

- Very common, usually minor
- Note size and location
- Monitor for changes
- Disclose to buyers
- May resolve or need surgery

**Cleft Palates:**

- Identified at birth
- Cannot nurse properly
- Often euthanized humanely
- Record in notes
- Genetic consideration

**Swimmer Puppy:**

- Legs splay out
- Can't walk properly
- Treatable if caught early
- Physical therapy
- Taping/hobbles
- Usually resolves

**Hypoglycemia:**

- Low blood sugar
- More common in toys
- Weakness, trembling
- Emergency treatment
- Frequent feeding
- Monitor closely

**Fading Puppy Syndrome:**

- Rapid decline
- Often in first 2 weeks
- Many possible causes
- Intensive care needed
- High mortality
- Document thoroughly

#### Health Event Documentation

**Recording Process:**

1. Puppy detail page
2. Health tab
3. Click "Add Health Event"
4. Enter comprehensive information
5. Save and monitor

**Information to Record:**

**Event Details:**

- Date/time noticed
- Symptoms observed
- Severity (mild/moderate/severe)
- Puppy's behavior
- Temperature if taken
- Other affected puppies?

**Actions Taken:**

- First aid provided
- Medications given
- Vet consulted (when)
- Treatment prescribed
- Response to treatment
- Follow-up needed

**Outcome:**

- Resolved fully
- Ongoing monitoring
- Chronic condition
- Surgical intervention
- Euthanasia (if necessary)
- Prevention steps

**Photos/Videos:**

- Upload documentation
- Before/after treatment
- Wound progression
- Movement issues
- Share with vet remotely

### Body Condition Scoring

![Screenshot: Body condition score chart with examples]

#### BCS Scale (1-5)

**1 - Emaciated:**

- Ribs, spine, bones prominent
- No body fat
- Severe muscle wasting
- Emergency situation

**2 - Thin:**

- Ribs easily felt
- Minimal fat
- Visible waist and tuck
- Below ideal

**3 - Ideal:**

- Ribs felt with slight pressure
- Visible waist from above
- Slight tuck from side
- Healthy weight

**4 - Overweight:**

- Ribs hard to feel
- No waist definition
- Some fat deposits
- Reduce food slightly

**5 - Obese:**

- Cannot feel ribs
- Heavy fat deposits
- No waist or tuck
- Health concerns

> ðŸ’¡ **Puppy BCS**: Young puppies (under 8 weeks) should be slightly pudgy (BCS 3-4)

#### Recording BCS

**When to Score:**

- Weekly with weight
- Before vet visits
- When buyer viewing
- With progress photos

**How to Record:**

1. During weight entry
2. Select BCS (1-5)
3. Add notes if needed
4. Save with weight
5. Tracks over time

**Using BCS Data:**

- Adjust feeding amounts
- Identify over/underfeeding
- Compare to weight gain
- Share with buyers
- Vet visit information

### Health Alerts and Notifications

#### Automated Alerts

**System Monitors:**

- Weight gain patterns
- Missed weigh-ins
- Vaccination due dates
- Deworming schedule
- Milestone delays
- Unusual health events

**Alert Types:**

**Critical Alerts (Immediate):**

- ðŸ”´ Weight loss detected
- ðŸ”´ No weight gain in 24 hours (newborn)
- ðŸ”´ Vaccination overdue
- ðŸ”´ Health event marked severe

**Warning Alerts (Review Soon):**

- ðŸŸ¡ Slow weight gain
- ðŸŸ¡ Missed scheduled weigh-in
- ðŸŸ¡ Deworming due soon
- ðŸŸ¡ Milestone delayed

**Information Alerts:**

- ðŸ”µ Time for weekly weigh-in
- ðŸ”µ Vaccination available
- ðŸ”µ Photo update suggested
- ðŸ”µ Buyer check-in due

#### Configuring Alerts

**Settings Access:**

1. Settings â†’ Notifications
2. Find "Health Monitoring" section
3. Configure preferences
4. Save settings

**Notification Channels:**

- â˜‘ Email notifications
- â˜‘ In-app notifications
- â˜‘ SMS alerts (critical only)
- â˜‘ Push notifications (mobile)

**Customization:**

- Set alert thresholds
- Choose notification methods
- Quiet hours
- Frequency limits
- Puppy-specific overrides

### Tooltips and Quick Help

> âš–ï¸ **Weighing Tip**: Place bowl on scale, tare to zero, add puppy - easier than holding

> ðŸ“Š **Chart Colors**: Each puppy has unique color on chart for easy identification

> ðŸ”” **Smart Alerts**: System learns your patterns and suggests optimal weigh-in times

> ðŸ“¸ **Photo Weights**: Take photo with scale display visible as backup documentation

> ðŸŽ¯ **Target Weight**: Set expected weight goals and track progress automatically

> ðŸ’Š **Dosage Calculator**: System calculates medication doses based on current weight

> ðŸ“± **Mobile App**: Use phone camera to scan and record scale readings

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Weight chart shows strange spikes**

- Solution: Check for data entry errors, verify units (oz vs lbs), remove outliers if mistake

**Problem: Can't see all puppies on chart**

- Solution: Use filter to select specific puppies, or zoom out to fit all

**Problem: Missed several days of weighing**

- Solution: Can't backfill exact data, resume daily tracking, note gap in records

**Problem: Weight seems stuck/not changing**

- Solution: Check scale batteries, verify scale accuracy, try different scale

**Problem: Alert not received for concerning weight**

- Solution: Check notification settings, verify email correct, check spam folder

**Problem: Can't generate health report**

- Solution: Ensure minimum data present (at least 2 weights, 1 health record)

### Advanced Features

**Growth Predictions:**

- Based on current weight and age
- Estimates adult weight
- Breed-specific algorithms
- Helps buyer planning
- Updates as puppy grows

**Comparative Analytics:**

- Compare to previous litters
- Same parents comparison
- Breed averages
- Identify trends
- Improve breeding program

**Integration with Vet Records:**

- Import vet visit data
- Sync vaccination schedules
- Share records securely
- Request vet reviews
- Collaborative care

**Export Options:**

- CSV for spreadsheet analysis
- JSON for data backup
- PDF for printing
- Image charts for social media
- Vet-compatible formats

## Lesson 12: Care Schedules and Templates

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Create daily care schedules for litters
- Use pre-built care templates
- Customize schedules by age
- Track task completion
- Set up recurring reminders
- Manage multiple litter schedules
- Share schedules with helpers
- Create reusable templates

### Understanding Care Schedules

#### Why Use Care Schedules?

Structured care schedules provide:

- **Consistency**: Same care every day
- **Organization**: Nothing gets forgotten
- **Delegation**: Easy to assign tasks to helpers
- **Time Management**: Plan your day efficiently
- **Record Keeping**: Track what's been done
- **Compliance**: Meet legal/ethical standards
- **Peace of Mind**: Confidence in complete care

> ðŸ’¡ **Professional Standard**: Detailed care schedules demonstrate commitment to puppy welfare

### Care Schedule Basics

![Screenshot: Care schedule overview page]

#### Schedule Components

**Daily Tasks:**

- Feeding times and amounts
- Weight checks
- Temperature monitoring
- Cleaning whelping box
- Health observations
- Socialization activities
- Training exercises
- Play sessions

**Weekly Tasks:**

- Nail trimming
- Bathing
- Deworming
- Weigh-ins
- Photos
- Area deep cleaning
- Supply restocking

**Milestone Tasks:**

- Vaccinations
- Microchipping
- Vet checkups
- Evaluations
- Buyer visits
- Go-home preparations

#### Age-Based Schedules

**Week 0-2 (Neonatal):**

- Focus: Warmth, nutrition, weight gain
- Every 2-4 hours around the clock
- Constant temperature monitoring
- Minimal handling
- Mom care primary
- Supplement if needed

**Week 2-4 (Transitional):**

- Focus: Eyes/ears opening, beginning mobility
- Every 4-6 hours
- Starting environmental exposure
- Gentle socialization begins
- Littermate interaction
- Mom still primary care

**Week 4-7 (Socialization Critical Period):**

- Focus: Weaning, social skills, exploration
- Scheduled feeding times (4x daily)
- Heavy socialization
- Exposure to sounds, surfaces, people
- Potty training introduction
- Crate training begins

**Week 7-12 (Juvenile):**

- Focus: Independence, training, placement prep
- Feeding 3-4x daily
- Advanced socialization
- Basic training (sit, come)
- Individual personalities emerge
- Buyer meetings
- Go-home preparation

### Accessing Care Schedules

![Screenshot: Navigation to care schedules]

#### Finding Care Schedules

**Method 1: From Litter Page**

1. Open litter details
2. Click **"Care Schedule"** tab
3. View/edit schedule
4. Mark tasks complete

**Method 2: From Dashboard**

1. Dashboard â†’ Today's Tasks widget
2. Shows all litter tasks due today
3. Click to mark complete
4. View detailed schedule

**Method 3: From Calendar**

1. Calendar view
2. Filter by "Care Tasks"
3. See all litter care scheduled
4. Click task to complete or edit

### Creating a New Care Schedule

![Screenshot: Create schedule wizard]

#### Using Templates

**Access Templates:**

1. Litter details â†’ Care Schedule tab
2. Click **"Create Schedule"**
3. Select **"Use Template"**
4. Browse available templates
5. Choose appropriate for age
6. Customize if needed
7. Activate schedule

**Pre-Built Templates:**

**Newborn Template (0-2 weeks):**

- Every 2 hours: Check puppies breathing, warm, nursing
- Every 4 hours: Weight all puppies
- Every 6 hours: Check mom, provide water/food
- Every 12 hours: Clean whelping box
- Daily: Temperature check, visual health exam

**Transitional Template (2-4 weeks):**

- 4x daily: Weight check (reduce to weekly after 3 weeks)
- 4x daily: Check food/water for mom
- 3x daily: Whelping box spot clean
- 2x daily: Handle each puppy 5-10 minutes
- Daily: Introduce new sounds/textures
- Weekly: Full whelping area clean, nail trim

**Weaning Template (4-7 weeks):**

- 4-5x daily: Feed puppies (gruel â†’ puppy food)
- 4x daily: Water check
- 4x daily: Potty area clean
- 3x daily: Socialization session (15-30 min)
- 2x daily: Health check all puppies
- Daily: Introduce new experiences
- Weekly: Bath, nails, photos, weights

**Pre-Placement Template (7-12 weeks):**

- 3-4x daily: Feeding
- 4x daily: Potty breaks and cleanup
- 2x daily: Training sessions (5-10 min each)
- 2x daily: Individual playtime
- Daily: Grooming practice, crate time
- Weekly: Photos, videos, buyer updates

> ðŸ’¡ **Tip**: Start with template, then customize based on your specific needs and litter

#### Custom Schedule Creation

**Building from Scratch:**

1. Care Schedule tab
2. Click "Create Custom Schedule"
3. Choose start date (usually birth date)
4. Select schedule duration
5. Add tasks individually
6. Set recurrence patterns
7. Assign time slots
8. Save schedule

### Adding Care Tasks

![Screenshot: Add task form]

#### Task Creation Form

**Required Information:**

**Task Name:**

- Clear, actionable title
- Examples:
  - "Feed puppies breakfast"
  - "Weigh all puppies"
  - "Clean whelping box"
  - "Socialization: vacuum noise exposure"
  - "Trim nails"

**Category:**

- ðŸ½ï¸ Feeding
- ðŸ§¹ Cleaning
- ðŸ¥ Health Check
- âš–ï¸ Weight Check
- ðŸŽ“ Training/Socialization
- ðŸ’‰ Medical
- ðŸ“¸ Documentation
- ðŸ‘¨â€ðŸ‘©â€ðŸ‘§ Mom Care
- ðŸ› ï¸ Maintenance
- ðŸ“‹ Other

**Timing:**

- Specific time (e.g., 8:00 AM)
- Time range (e.g., 8-9 AM)
- Frequency:
  - One-time
  - Daily
  - Every X hours
  - Specific days of week
  - Weekly
  - Monthly
  - Custom pattern

**Duration:**

- How long task takes
- Helps with time management
- 5, 10, 15, 30, 60 minutes
- Custom duration

**Optional Information:**

**Description:**

- Detailed instructions
- Exactly how to do task
- Quantities/measurements
- Special considerations
- Tips for success

**Example Description for "Feed Puppies":**

```
- Mix 1 cup puppy kibble with 1/2 cup warm water
- Let soak 5 minutes
- Divide equally into 4 bowls
- Place bowls in feeding area
- Monitor to ensure all eating
- Remove bowls after 20 minutes
- Clean bowls immediately
```

**Assigned To:**

- Who's responsible
- Yourself
- Helper/assistant
- Family member
- Rotating assignment

**Priority:**

- ðŸ”´ High (critical, time-sensitive)
- ðŸŸ¡ Medium (important, some flexibility)
- ðŸŸ¢ Low (helpful, can be rescheduled)

**Reminders:**

- Alert 15 min before
- Alert 30 min before
- Alert 1 hour before
- Alert day before
- Custom reminder time

**Photos Required:**

- Checkbox to require photo with completion
- Useful for:
  - Proof of cleaning
  - Before/after documentation
  - Meal portions
  - Puppy activities
  - Health checks

### Managing Task Schedules

![Screenshot: Daily task list view]

#### Daily Task View

**Today's Tasks:**

- Shows all tasks due today
- Organized by time
- Color-coded by status:
  - âšª Not started
  - ðŸ”µ In progress
  - âœ… Completed
  - â­ï¸ Skipped
  - âš ï¸ Overdue

**Task Actions:**

- âœ“ Mark complete
- â­ï¸ Skip (with reason)
- ðŸ“ Add notes
- ðŸ“¸ Attach photo
- â° Reschedule
- âž• Add subtasks

**Completion Process:**

1. Click task card
2. Review instructions
3. Complete the task
4. Take photo if required
5. Add notes if needed
6. Click "Mark Complete"
7. Timestamp recorded
8. Task moves to completed

#### Weekly Overview

**Calendar View:**

- See full week at glance
- All litters combined or filtered
- Time blocks for tasks
- Drag to reschedule
- Identify busy times
- Plan helpers accordingly

**Recurring Tasks:**

- Auto-generate per schedule
- Edit instance or series
- Skip specific dates
- Adjust patterns as needed

### Task Templates and Shortcuts

![Screenshot: Task template library]

#### Reusable Task Templates

**Creating Templates:**

1. Create task with all details
2. Click "Save as Template"
3. Name template
4. Choose category
5. Available for future use

**Template Library:**

- Your saved templates
- Community templates (optional)
- Breed-specific templates
- Searchable/filterable
- Quick add to schedules

**Common Template Examples:**

**Feeding Template:**

```
Name: Puppy Feeding
Category: Feeding
Time: [Variable]
Duration: 20 min
Description:
- Prepare food (see quantity chart)
- Supervise eating
- Remove uneaten food after 20 min
- Clean dishes
- Note any non-eaters
```

**Weight Check Template:**

```
Name: Daily Weight Check
Category: Health
Time: Before first feeding
Duration: 15 min
Description:
- Weigh each puppy
- Record in app
- Note any losses/concerns
- Compare to previous day
- Alert if any issues
Photo: Required
```

**Socialization Template:**

```
Name: Socialization Session
Category: Training
Time: [Variable]
Duration: 30 min
Description:
- New experience (see rotation list)
- Positive reinforcement
- Individual and group exposure
- Note reactions
- Increase difficulty gradually
Photo: Required
```

### Age-Based Schedule Transitions

![Screenshot: Schedule transition wizard]

#### Automatic Transitions

**How It Works:**

- Schedule linked to puppy age
- Transitions automatic at milestones
- Tasks update appropriately
- Frequencies adjust
- Notifications about changes

**Key Transition Points:**

**Week 2 â†’ Week 3:**

- Reduce weight checks (4x daily â†’ daily)
- Add nail trimming (weekly)
- Increase handling time
- Begin sound exposure

**Week 3 â†’ Week 4:**

- Prepare for weaning
- Introduce lapping (water, gruel)
- More frequent cleaning
- Enhanced socialization

**Week 4 â†’ Week 5:**

- Begin weaning process
- Scheduled feedings start
- Potty area introduced
- Mom separation periods

**Week 7 â†’ Week 8:**

- First vaccinations
- Increased independent time
- Basic training introduction
- Buyer preparation tasks

#### Manual Adjustments

**When to Adjust:**

- Litter developing faster/slower
- Specific puppy needs
- Your schedule changes
- Helper availability
- Special circumstances

**How to Adjust:**

1. Open schedule
2. Click "Edit Schedule"
3. Modify tasks:
   - Change times
   - Adjust frequency
   - Add/remove tasks
   - Update descriptions
4. Save changes
5. Applies going forward

### Tracking Completion

![Screenshot: Completion history and statistics]

#### Completion Dashboard

**Statistics Display:**

- Completion rate (%)
- Tasks completed today
- Tasks completed this week
- Overdue tasks
- Upcoming tasks (next 24h)
- Average completion time

**Trends:**

- Daily completion pattern
- Most missed tasks
- Time of day analysis
- Category breakdown
- Helper performance (if assigned)

**Historical View:**

- Calendar view of completed tasks
- Search past completions
- Filter by task type
- Export completion reports
- Identify patterns

#### Task Notes and Photos

**Adding Context:**

- Click completed task
- View completion details
- Add follow-up notes
- Upload additional photos
- Link related health events

**Examples of Useful Notes:**

```
Feeding 8AM:
"Yellow collar puppy ate slowly, monitored.
All others ate well. Reduced portion slightly."

Weight Check:
"All puppies gained. Blue collar +2oz,
best gain of the week!"

Socialization:
"Vacuum exposure - most curious,
pink collar initially nervous but warmed up"

Cleaning:
"Deep clean complete. Replaced bedding.
Added extra blanket - temps dropping"
```

### Multiple Litter Management

![Screenshot: Multi-litter schedule view]

#### Managing Multiple Schedules

**When You Have Multiple Litters:**

- Different age groups
- Different care needs
- Overlapping tasks
- Complex scheduling
- Need for helpers

**Multi-Litter View:**

- All litters on one screen
- Color-coded by litter
- Filter to specific litter
- Batch complete similar tasks
- Time block planning

**Efficiency Tips:**

- Group similar tasks
- Do all feeding at once
- Batch cleaning tasks
- Coordinate weigh-ins
- Stagger schedules if possible

**Example Combined Schedule:**

```
8:00 AM - Feed both litters
8:30 AM - Weigh Litter A (newborns)
9:00 AM - Clean Litter B area
9:30 AM - Socialize Litter B
10:00 AM - Monitor Litter A
11:00 AM - Weigh Litter A again
12:00 PM - Feed both litters
```

### Sharing Schedules with Helpers

![Screenshot: Share schedule interface]

#### Collaboration Features

**Inviting Helpers:**

1. Open litter schedule
2. Click "Share Schedule"
3. Enter helper's email
4. Set permissions:
   - View only
   - View and complete tasks
   - Full edit access
5. Send invitation
6. Helper receives email link

**Helper View:**

- See assigned tasks
- Receive reminders
- Complete tasks
- Add notes
- Upload photos
- No access to other data

**Communication:**

- In-task comments
- @mention helpers
- Flag issues
- Request assistance
- Provide feedback

**Notification Settings:**

- Helper gets alerts for assigned tasks
- You get alerts when tasks completed
- Daily summary emails
- Issue alerts

### Creating Reusable Templates

![Screenshot: Template creation interface]

#### Template Builder

**When to Create Templates:**

- Schedule works well for litter
- Want to reuse for future litters
- Share with other breeders
- Standardize your process

**Template Creation:**

1. Complete litter with good schedule
2. Go to Care Schedule
3. Click "Save as Template"
4. Template wizard opens
5. Name template: "My Golden Retriever Schedule"
6. Add description
7. Set age range: 0-12 weeks
8. Review all tasks
9. Set as private or public
10. Save template

**Template Includes:**

- All tasks and details
- Timing patterns
- Categories
- Descriptions
- Photo requirements
- But NOT specific dates/puppies

**Using Your Templates:**

- New litter â†’ Care Schedule
- Click "Use Template"
- Select your saved template
- Choose start date
- Customize if needed
- Activate

### Practice Exercises

**Exercise 1: Apply Pre-Built Template**

1. Open any litter (preferably just born)
2. Go to Care Schedule tab
3. Click "Create Schedule"
4. Select "Newborn Template (0-2 weeks)"
5. Review tasks included
6. Set start date to birth date
7. Activate schedule
8. View today's tasks

**Exercise 2: Complete Daily Tasks**

1. View today's tasks for litter
2. Find "Check puppies nursing" task
3. Click task to open
4. Review instructions
5. Mark task as complete
6. Add note: "All nursing well, active"
7. Note completion time
8. View updated task list

**Exercise 3: Add Custom Task**

1. Open litter care schedule
2. Click "Add Task"
3. Name: "Introduce new toy"
4. Category: Training/Socialization
5. Time: 2:00 PM
6. Frequency: Daily
7. Duration: 15 min
8. Description: "Introduce different textured toy, observe reactions"
9. Require photo: Yes
10. Save task

**Exercise 4: Create Weekly Task**

1. Add new task
2. Name: "Puppy photo session"
3. Category: Documentation
4. Frequency: Weekly (Sundays)
5. Time: 10:00 AM
6. Duration: 30 min
7. Description: "Individual and group photos. Natural light. Include size reference."
8. Require photo: Yes
9. Reminder: 1 day before
10. Save

**Exercise 5: Build Custom Template**

1. Create or open a litter schedule you like
2. Add at least 5 different tasks
3. Include various categories
4. Set appropriate timing
5. Add detailed descriptions
6. Click "Save as Template"
7. Name: "[YourName]'s Custom Schedule"
8. Save for future use

**Exercise 6: Multi-Litter Management**

1. If you have 2+ litters, open multi-litter view
2. View all tasks for today
3. Filter by specific litter
4. Filter by task category (e.g., Feeding)
5. Complete a task from each litter
6. Add notes to differentiate
7. View completion statistics

### Tooltips and Quick Help

> ðŸ“… **Auto-Schedule**: Templates automatically adjust task times based on puppy age

> â° **Smart Reminders**: System learns your completion patterns and adjusts reminder timing

> ðŸ“¸ **Photo Tasks**: Required photos can't be skipped - ensures documentation compliance

> ðŸ‘¥ **Delegation**: Assign specific tasks to helpers for clear responsibility

> ðŸ“Š **Analytics**: Track which tasks take longest to optimize your schedule

> ðŸ”„ **Recurring Edits**: Edit one instance or the entire recurring series

> ðŸ’¡ **Task Templates**: Save time by creating templates for frequently used tasks

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Too many tasks overwhelming**

- Solution: Start with minimal essential tasks, gradually add more

**Problem: Tasks piling up as overdue**

- Solution: Adjust timing to realistic schedule, reduce frequency if needed

**Problem: Can't mark task complete**

- Solution: Check if photo required but not uploaded, or permissions issue

**Problem: Helper not receiving notifications**

- Solution: Verify email address correct, check spam folder, confirm permission level

**Problem: Template not showing all tasks**

- Solution: Check age range filter, ensure template properly saved

**Problem: Tasks showing on wrong days**

- Solution: Verify litter birth date correct, check recurring pattern settings

### Advanced Features

**Task Dependencies:**

- Some tasks must complete before others
- Example: Weight before feeding
- System can enforce order
- Helpful for helpers

**Conditional Tasks:**

- Tasks appear based on conditions
- Example: "If weight loss, add supplemental feeding"
- Smart scheduling
- Adaptive care

**Integration with Health:**

- Weight checks auto-populate data
- Health observations create health records
- Vaccination tasks generate certificates
- Seamless workflow

**Time Tracking:**

- Actual time spent vs estimated
- Identify time-consuming tasks
- Optimize schedule
- Plan helper coverage

**Mobile Optimization:**

- Quick task completion on phone
- Voice notes
- Fast photo upload
- Offline mode (syncs later)

### Knowledge Check

- â˜ I can apply pre-built care schedule templates
- â˜ I understand age-based schedule differences
- â˜ I can create custom care tasks
- â˜ I know how to mark tasks complete
- â˜ I can set up recurring tasks
- â˜ I understand task categories and priorities
- â˜ I can manage multiple litter schedules
- â˜ I can share schedules with helpers
- â˜ I can create reusable templates
- â˜ I know how to track completion and identify patterns

# Module 4: Customer Relations

## Lesson 13: Customer Records and CRM

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Add and manage customer records
- Track buyer interactions and communications
- Record preferences and requirements
- Manage customer documents
- Track customer history
- Use CRM tools effectively
- Segment customers by status
- Generate customer reports

### Understanding Customer Relationship Management

#### Why Use CRM?

Professional customer management helps you:

- **Build Relationships**: Track every interaction
- **Improve Service**: Remember preferences and details
- **Stay Organized**: All information in one place
- **Follow Up**: Never miss important communications
- **Referrals**: Track recommendations and success stories
- **Reputation**: Demonstrate professionalism
- **Efficiency**: Quickly access customer information
- **Legal Protection**: Complete documentation

> ðŸ’¡ **Professional Standard**: Good CRM is the difference between a hobby breeder and a professional business

### Customer Record Basics

![Screenshot: Customers page overview]

#### What is a Customer Record?

A customer record contains:

- **Contact Information**: Name, email, phone, address
- **Communication History**: All interactions logged
- **Preferences**: Breed, color, sex, temperament needs
- **Requirements**: Home type, family situation, experience
- **Documents**: Applications, contracts, photos
- **Puppy Assignments**: Which puppy(ies) they've purchased
- **Payment History**: Deposits, payments, balance
- **Status**: Inquiry â†’ Waitlist â†’ Active Buyer â†’ Past Buyer
- **Notes**: Any relevant information

### Adding a New Customer

![Screenshot: Add customer form]

#### Accessing Customer Creation

**Method 1: From Customers Page**

1. Click **"Customers"** in sidebar
2. Click **"+ Add Customer"** button (top right)
3. Customer form opens

**Method 2: From Inquiry**

1. Open inquiry details
2. Click **"Convert to Customer"**
3. Information pre-filled
4. Complete additional details
5. Save

**Method 3: From Waitlist**

1. Open waitlist application
2. Click **"Add to Customers"**
3. Application data transfers
4. Add contact details
5. Save customer record

**Method 4: Quick Add**

1. From Dashboard
2. Quick Actions widget
3. Click "Add Customer"
4. Minimal form for speed
5. Edit details later

### Customer Information Form

![Screenshot: Complete customer creation form]

#### Essential Contact Information

**Personal Details:**

**First Name** (Required)

- Buyer's first name
- Proper capitalization
- Example: "Sarah"

**Last Name** (Required)

- Buyer's last name
- Example: "Johnson"
- Display: "Sarah Johnson"

**Email Address** (Required)

- Primary contact email
- Validated format
- Example: sarah.johnson@email.com
- Used for all notifications

**Phone Number** (Required)

- Primary phone
- Format: (555) 123-4567 or 555-123-4567
- Mobile preferred
- Used for text updates

**Secondary Phone** (Optional)

- Alternate contact
- Home phone
- Work phone
- Emergency contact

**Address Information:**

**Street Address**

- Full street address
- Include apartment/unit
- Example: "123 Main Street, Apt 4B"

**City** (Required)

- Customer's city
- Example: "San Diego"

**State/Province** (Required)

- Two-letter code or full name
- Example: "CA" or "California"

**ZIP/Postal Code**

- 5 or 9 digit ZIP
- Canadian postal code
- Example: 92101

**Country**

- Default: United States
- Select from list
- International buyers supported

> ðŸ’¡ **Privacy Note**: Address optional for inquiries, required for contracts and pickup

#### Buyer Preferences

**Desired Traits:**

**Breed Preference**

- Primary breed interested in
- If you breed multiple
- Auto-filled if single breed

**Gender Preference**

- Male
- Female
- No preference
- Helps with puppy matching

**Color Preference**

- Specific colors desired
- Multiple selections allowed
- Example: "Golden, Light Cream"
- Rank by priority

**Size Preference**

- Small, Medium, Large
- Weight range
- Helps predict adult size
- Breed-specific

**Temperament Needs**

- Active/Energetic
- Calm/Mellow
- Confident/Bold
- Gentle/Sensitive
- Family-friendly
- Single-person bond

**Purpose:**

- Family pet
- Service/therapy dog
- Show prospect
- Breeding prospect
- Working dog
- Sport/competition

> ðŸ’¡ **Matching Tip**: Detailed preferences help match perfect puppy to family

#### Family and Home Situation

**Household Information:**

**Family Composition**

- Adults in home (number)
- Children (ages)
- Other pets (types)
- Elderly family members
- Frequent visitors

**Example:**

```
2 adults, children ages 8 and 12
1 cat (indoor)
Grandmother visits weekly
```

**Home Type**

- House with yard
- Apartment
- Condo
- Townhouse
- Farm/rural
- Urban/suburban

**Yard Details**

- Fenced (type)
- Size (square feet)
- No yard
- Shared space
- Dog park nearby

**Activity Level**

- Very active family
- Moderately active
- Sedentary/quiet
- Varies by season
- Specific activities (hiking, running, etc.)

**Experience Level**

- First-time dog owner
- Previous dog owner (breed)
- Current dog owner
- Professional experience
- Breed-specific experience

**Work Schedule**

- Home all day
- Work from home
- Part-time outside home
- Full-time away
- Rotating schedule
- Plan for dog during work

#### Special Requirements

**Restrictions/Needs:**

**Allergies**

- Family member allergies
- Severity level
- Previous experience with breed
- Grooming considerations

**Physical Limitations**

- Elderly owner
- Disabilities
- Strength concerns
- Mobility issues
- Need for calmer dog

**HOA/Rental Restrictions**

- Weight limits
- Breed restrictions
- Pet deposits required
- Landlord approval needed

**Travel Plans**

- Frequent travel
- Vacation homes
- Dog care during travel
- Plans to take dog

**Budget Considerations**

- Purchase price range
- Ongoing care budget
- Emergency fund
- Insurance plans

### Customer Status Management

![Screenshot: Customer status options]

#### Status Types

**Inquiry**

- Initial contact

- Information gathering
- No commitment

**Qualified Lead**

- Meets basic criteria
- Serious interest
- Application submitted
- Reference checks pending
- Moving forward

**Waitlist**

- On official waitlist
- Deposit may be placed
- Waiting for litter
- Priority assigned
- Active communication

**Active Buyer**

- Puppy reserved
- Deposit received
- Awaiting pickup
- Contract in progress
- High priority

**Placed**

- Puppy delivered
- Contract complete
- Payment finalized
- Follow-up phase
- Past customer

**Alumni**

- Multiple purchases
- Long-term relationship
- Referral source
- Success story
- VIP status

**Not a Fit**

- Did not qualify
- Chose different breeder
- Requirements don't match
- Declined application
- Archived

**Lost Contact**

- Stopped responding
- Email bouncing
- Phone disconnected
- No longer interested
- Archive after attempts

4. Select new status
5. Add note explaining change
6. Save

**Automatic Status Updates:**

- Inquiry â†’ Qualified (when application approved)
- Qualified â†’ Waitlist (when deposit received)
- Waitlist â†’ Active Buyer (when puppy assigned)
- Active Buyer â†’ Placed (when puppy goes home)

**Status Triggers:**

- Email notifications
- Task creation
- Document generation
- Priority changes
- Dashboard updates

#### Adding Interaction Records

![Screenshot: Add interaction form]

**Recording Process:**

1. Open customer record
2. Go to **"Interactions"** tab
3. Click **"+ Add Interaction"**
4. Fill in details
5. Save

**Interaction Form:**

**Type** (Required)

- Select from list above
- Determines icon/color
- Filters available

**Date/Time** (Required)

- When interaction occurred
- Auto-defaults to now
- Can backdate if needed

**Duration** (Optional)

- How long communication took
- Helps with time tracking
- 5, 10, 15, 30, 60 min

**Subject/Title** (Required)

- Brief description
- Searchable
- Examples:
  - "Initial inquiry about puppies"
  - "Reference check call"
  - "Contract review meeting"
  - "6-month puppy update"

**Details** (Required)

- Full notes on conversation
- Questions asked
- Information provided
- Concerns raised
- Next steps
- Action items

**Example Details:**

```
Discussed upcoming litter due in March.
Customer interested in male, golden color,
family pet temperament. Has 2 children
ages 6 and 9, fenced yard, previous golden
owner (dog passed last year). Very knowledgeable
and prepared.

Action Items:
- Send application
- Add to March litter waitlist
- Follow up in 2 weeks

Next Contact: 12/15/2025
```

**Follow-Up Date** (Optional)

- When to contact again
- Creates reminder
- Shows on calendar
- Helps stay organized

**Priority** (Optional)

- High: Urgent follow-up needed
- Medium: Normal priority
- Low: FYI only

**Attachments** (Optional)

- Upload documents
- Photos shared
- Email threads
- Contracts
- Forms

**Tags** (Optional)

- Categorize interactions
- Easy filtering
- Examples:
  - #application
  - #reference-check
  - #pickup-scheduled
  - #complaint
  - #referral

- â˜‘ Inquiry

- â˜‘ Active Buyer
- â˜‘ Placed
- â˜‘ Alumni

**By Location:**

- State/Province
- City
- ZIP code radius
- Country

**By Preferences:**

- Gender preference
- Color preference
- Breed (if multiple)
- Purpose (pet, show, etc.)

**By Date:**

- Added date range
- Last contact date
- Next follow-up due
- Placement date

**By Assignment:**

- Has puppy assigned
- Waitlist position
- Litter preference
- Specific puppy reserved

**By Tags:**

- Custom tags you created
- Multiple tag selection
- AND/OR logic

**Saved Searches:**

- Save filter combinations
- Quick access
- One-click filtering
- Share with team

#### Bulk Operations

   - Update status
   - Send email

   - Assign to litter
   - Export data
   - Delete (careful!)

### Customer Segmentation

![Screenshot: Customer segments and lists]

#### Creating Segments

**Why Segment?**

- Targeted communication
- Different messages for different stages
- Personalized service
- Efficient marketing
- Better organization

**Common Segments:**

**"Hot Leads"**

- Inquiries in last 30 days
- Highly engaged
- Application submitted
- Quick follow-up needed

**"Active Waitlist"**

- Deposit paid
- Awaiting specific litter
- Monthly updates
- High priority

**"Past Buyers - Repeat Potential"**

- Purchased 2+ years ago
- Positive experience
- May want another puppy
- Referral opportunities

**"Local Customers"**

- Within 100 miles
- Easy pickup
- Home visits possible
- Community events

**"Out of State"**

- Shipping required
- Different requirements
- Travel coordination
- Higher commitment

**"First-Time Owners"**

- Extra education needed
- More hand-holding
- Training resources
- Post-placement support

**Creating Custom Segments:**

1. Customers page
2. Apply filters
3. Click "Save as Segment"
4. Name segment
5. Available in dropdown

### Tooltips and Quick Help

> ðŸ“± **Mobile Access**: Customer records available on mobile app for on-the-go updates

> ðŸ”” **Smart Reminders**: System alerts when you haven't contacted a customer in set timeframe

> ðŸ“Š **Dashboard Widgets**: Pin frequently contacted customers to dashboard

> ðŸ·ï¸ **Quick Tags**: Use keyboard shortcuts to quickly tag customers during entry

> ðŸ”— **Linked Records**: Customer records automatically link to puppies, contracts, payments

> ðŸ“§ **Email Tracking**: See when customers open emails and click links

> ðŸŽ¯ **Lead Scoring**: System can automatically score leads based on engagement

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Can't find customer in search**

- Solution: Check spelling, try partial name, search by phone or email instead

**Problem: Duplicate customer records**

- Solution: Use merge function in customer menu to combine records

**Problem: Customer not receiving emails**

- Solution: Verify email address, check spam folder, confirm email preferences

**Problem: Lost interaction notes**

- Solution: Check all interaction types (filter may be hiding), use search function

**Problem: Status not updating automatically**

- Solution: Check automation settings, may need manual update in some cases

**Problem: Too many customers to manage**

- Solution: Use segments and filters, prioritize by status, delegate to team members

- Marketing platforms

**Team Collaboration:**

- Assign customers to staff
- Share notes and tasks
- Team chat on customer records
- Activity feeds

**Analytics and Insights:**

- Conversion funnel analysis
- Customer lifetime value
- Churn prediction
- Satisfaction scoring

**Mobile CRM:**

- Full functionality on phone
- Offline mode
- Quick actions
- Voice notes
- GPS check-ins

## Lesson 14: Inquiry Management

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Receive and process inquiries
- Qualify potential buyers
- Respond to common questions
- Track inquiry sources
- Convert inquiries to customers
- Manage inquiry workflow
- Use inquiry templates
- Measure inquiry performance

### Understanding Inquiry Management

#### What is an Inquiry?

An inquiry is:

- Initial contact from potential buyer
- Questions about your breeding program
- Request for puppy availability
- Application for waitlist
- General information request

**Inquiry Channels:**

- Website contact form
- Email
- Phone call
- Social media message
- Referral
- Pet marketplace sites
- Breed club referrals

> ðŸ’¡ **First Impression**: How you handle inquiries sets tone for entire relationship

### Inquiry Workflow

![Screenshot: Inquiry workflow diagram]

#### Inquiry Lifecycle

**1. Receipt**

- Inquiry comes in
- System notification
- Auto-reply sent
- Added to inquiry list
- Status: New

**2. Review**

- Read inquiry details
- Assess seriousness
- Check red flags
- Determine fit
- Status: Under Review

**3. Initial Response**

- Send information
- Answer questions
- Share availability
- Request details
- Status: Responded

**4. Qualification**

- Application sent/received
- References checked
- Home/lifestyle assessed
- Decision made
- Status: Qualified OR Not a Fit

**5. Conversion**

- Accept to waitlist
- Assign to litter
- Deposit received
- Create customer record
- Status: Converted

### Receiving Inquiries

![Screenshot: Inquiry list view]

#### Inquiry Sources

**Website Contact Form:**

- Automatic entry to system
- Email notification sent
- All form fields captured
- Source tracking automatic
- Highest quality leads

**Email Inquiries:**

- Sent to your breeder email
- Can forward to system
- Manual entry option
- Include full email thread
- Attach email as document

**Phone Inquiries:**

- Manual entry after call
- Record during conversation
- Note caller information
- Set follow-up reminder
- Send follow-up email

**Social Media:**

- Facebook, Instagram messages
- Copy/paste conversation
- Link to social profile
- Track social source
- Note platform

**Referrals:**

- Note referring customer
- Track referral source
- Special priority
- Thank referrer
- Offer referral bonus

#### Inquiry Form Fields

**Automatic Capture (Website Form):**

- Name (first/last)
- Email address
- Phone number
- Location (city/state)
- Message/questions
- Preferred contact method
- Best time to reach
- How they found you

**Additional Information:**

- Desired timeline
- Gender preference
- Color preference
- Previous dog experience
- Current pets
- Home type
- Purpose for dog

### Inquiry List Management

![Screenshot: Inquiry dashboard]

#### Viewing Inquiries

**Inbox Style Layout:**

- List of all inquiries
- Sorted by date (newest first)
- Status indicators
- Priority flags
- Unread count
- Quick preview

**Inquiry Card Shows:**

- Contact name
- Subject line
- Preview of message (first 100 chars)
- Date received
- Source icon
- Status badge
- Priority indicator
- Has replied (checkmark)

**Status Color Coding:**

- ðŸ”µ New (blue) - Unread
- ðŸŸ¡ Under Review (yellow) - In progress
- ðŸŸ¢ Responded (green) - Waiting for reply
- ðŸŸ£ Qualified (purple) - Approved
- âš« Not a Fit (gray) - Declined
- âœ… Converted (green check) - Now customer

#### Filtering and Sorting

**Filter Options:**

- Status (New, Responded, etc.)
- Date range
- Source (website, email, referral, etc.)
- Priority (high, medium, low)
- Assigned to (team member)
- Litter interest (if specified)

**Sort Options:**

- Date received (newest/oldest)
- Last activity
- Priority
- Name (A-Z)
- Status

**Search:**

- By name
- By email
- By keywords in message
- By location

### Opening and Reading Inquiries

![Screenshot: Inquiry detail view]

#### Inquiry Details Page

**Header Information:**

- Contact name (large)
- Email address (clickable)
- Phone number (clickable)
- Location
- Date received
- Time since received
- Source

**Message Content:**

- Full inquiry text
- Original formatting
- Quoted text if email
- Attached images/files
- Links in message

**Quick Info Panel:**

- Previous inquiries from this person?
- Already in customer database?
- Existing pet owner with you?
- Referral source
- Match score (automatic)

**Action Buttons:**

- Reply
- Call
- Convert to Customer
- Add to Waitlist
- Mark as Not a Fit
- Archive
- Forward to Team

### Qualifying Inquiries

![Screenshot: Qualification checklist]

#### Red Flags to Watch For

**Concerning Behaviors:**

- âš ï¸ Only asking about price
- âš ï¸ Wants "pick of litter" immediately
- âš ï¸ Unrealistic timeline (need puppy tomorrow)
- âš ï¸ No questions about health/temperament
- âš ï¸ Pushy or demanding
- âš ï¸ Won't provide information
- âš ï¸ Previous dogs "disappeared"
- âš ï¸ Multiple breeders at once
- âš ï¸ Plans to breed without proper knowledge
- âš ï¸ Wants to "flip" puppies

**Price Shopping:**

- First question is price
- Compares to cheaper sources
- Wants discount
- No interest in quality
- Looking for "deal"

> ðŸš© **Red Flag Response**: Politely decline or redirect to breed rescue if not a good fit

#### Green Flags (Good Inquiries)

**Positive Indicators:**

- âœ… Detailed questions about health testing
- âœ… Asks about temperament/personality
- âœ… Wants to visit/meet parents
- âœ… Flexible timeline
- âœ… Prepared for investment
- âœ… Previous breed experience
- âœ… Researched your program
- âœ… References ready
- âœ… Veterinarian established
- âœ… Understands puppy needs

**Excellent Inquiries:**

- Referred by past customer
- Follows you on social media
- Read all website info
- Asks thoughtful questions
- Professional communication
- Patience with timeline
- Excited but not desperate

#### Qualification Questions

**Key Questions to Ask:**

**1. Timeline:**

- "When are you hoping to bring a puppy home?"
- "Are you flexible on timing?"

**2. Experience:**

- "Have you owned this breed before?"
- "Tell me about your previous dogs."

**3. Home Situation:**

- "Do you own or rent?"
- "Is your yard fenced?"
- "Any HOA restrictions?"

**4. Lifestyle:**

- "What's your activity level?"
- "Who will be primary caregiver?"
- "Work schedule?"

**5. Purpose:**

- "What role will this dog play?"
- "Any specific activities planned?"
- "Breeding plans?" (if applicable)

**6. Preparation:**

- "Do you have a veterinarian?"
- "Budget for care?"
- "What have you read about the breed?"

### Responding to Inquiries

![Screenshot: Reply composition interface]

#### Response Best Practices

**Timing:**

- Respond within 24 hours (sooner is better)
- Same day for high-priority
- Weekends: At least auto-reply
- After hours: Auto-reply + respond next day

**Tone:**

- Professional yet friendly
- Enthusiastic but not desperate
- Honest and transparent
- Educational
- Respectful

**Content:**

- Answer their questions
- Provide additional info
- Explain your process
- Set expectations
- Next steps clear

#### Response Templates

**Template 1: Initial Response to Good Inquiry**

```
Subject: Thank you for your inquiry about [Breed] puppies

Dear [Name],

Thank you for your interest in [Your Kennel Name]! I'm
delighted to hear you're considering adding one of our
[breed] puppies to your family.

Based on your message, it sounds like you'd be a wonderful
home. I especially appreciate that [mention something
specific from their inquiry].

Here's information about our current/upcoming litters:
[Litter details, expected dates, availability]

Our Process:
1. Complete puppy application (attached)
2. Phone interview
3. Reference check
4. Waitlist placement
5. Match puppy to family
6. Pickup at 8-10 weeks

Investment: $[price] for pet homes, includes:
- Health guarantee
- First vaccinations
- Microchip
- Puppy starter pack
- Lifetime support

I'd love to learn more about your family and lifestyle
to ensure we're the right fit. Please complete the
attached application and we can schedule a call.

Looking forward to hearing from you!

Best regards,
[Your Name]
[Contact Info]
```

**Template 2: Response to Price-Only Inquiry**

```
Subject: Re: Puppy price inquiry

Hello [Name],

Thank you for your interest in our [breed] puppies.

Our puppies are $[price] for pet homes. This investment
reflects our commitment to:
- Comprehensive health testing of parents
- Superior bloodlines and temperament
- Early socialization and training
- Health guarantee and lifetime support
- Proper nutrition and veterinary care

I'd be happy to discuss what goes into raising quality
puppies and answer any questions. If you're looking for
more detailed information about our breeding program,
please visit [website] or let me know what else you'd
like to know.

Best regards,
[Your Name]
```

**Template 3: Not a Good Fit**

```
Subject: Re: Your puppy inquiry

Dear [Name],

Thank you for your interest in our puppies. After reviewing
your inquiry, I don't believe we're the best match for your
needs at this time.

[Specific reason if appropriate - timeline, experience level,
living situation, etc.]

I'd like to recommend:
- [Breed rescue organization] if you're open to adoption
- [Other breeder who might be better fit]
- [Resources for learning more about the breed]

I wish you the best in finding the perfect companion.

Best regards,
[Your Name]
```

**Template 4: Waitlist Information**

```
Subject: Waitlist information for [Breed] puppies

Hi [Name],

Great news! Based on our conversation and your application,
I'd love to add you to our waitlist for [litter details].

Waitlist Process:
1. Waitlist deposit: $[amount] (applied to purchase price)
2. Updates throughout pregnancy and after birth
3. Priority selection based on deposit order and match
4. Balance due at pickup: $[remaining amount]

Expected Timeline:
- Litter due: [date]
- Puppies go home: [date range]
- Your estimated position: [number] on waitlist

Next Steps:
1. Review attached contract
2. Submit deposit via [payment methods]
3. Stay in touch for updates

Excited to work with you!

[Your Name]
```

#### Using Response Templates

**Accessing Templates:**

1. Open inquiry
2. Click "Reply"
3. Click "Templates" button
4. Select appropriate template
5. Customize for this person
6. Review carefully
7. Send

**Personalizing Templates:**

- Replace [placeholders]
- Add specific details from their inquiry
- Reference their situation
- Use their name multiple times
- Sign personally

**Creating Custom Templates:**

1. Write great response
2. Click "Save as Template"
3. Name template
4. Select category
5. Available for future use

### Converting Inquiries

![Screenshot: Conversion workflow]

#### Inquiry to Customer

**When to Convert:**

- Application approved
- References checked
- Home suitable
- Timeline works
- Deposit ready/received
- Good communication

**Conversion Process:**

1. Open inquiry
2. Click **"Convert to Customer"**
3. Customer form pre-filled
4. Add additional details
5. Set appropriate status (Waitlist or Active Buyer)
6. Transfer all interactions
7. Link to litter if applicable
8. Save

**What Happens:**

- Customer record created
- Inquiry marked "Converted"
- All notes transferred
- Communication history preserved
- Inquiry archived
- Customer receives welcome email

#### Inquiry to Waitlist

**Direct Waitlist Add:**

1. Inquiry details
2. Click **"Add to Waitlist"**
3. Select litter
4. Set priority
5. Deposit amount
6. Creates both customer and waitlist entry
7. Sends confirmation

**Waitlist Entry Includes:**

- Customer information
- Preferences
- Priority position
- Deposit status
- Litter assignment
- Expected date

> See Lesson 15 for detailed waitlist management

- Inquiry â†’ Response

### Tooltips and Quick Help

> âš¡ **Quick Reply**: Use keyboard shortcuts to respond faster (R for reply)

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Not receiving inquiry notifications**

- Solution: Check notification settings, verify email correct, check spam folder

**Problem: Inquiry form spam**

- Solution: Add CAPTCHA, require phone verification, review form fields

**Problem: Duplicate inquiries from same person**

- Solution: System should detect and link, or manually merge

**Problem: Lost inquiry in system**

- Solution: Use search function, check archived inquiries, check all statuses

**Problem: Can't convert inquiry to customer**

- Solution: Ensure all required fields complete, check for duplicate customer

**Problem: Response templates not personalizing**

- Solution: Check placeholder syntax, manually edit after inserting template

**Auto-Response System:**

- Instant auto-reply to inquiries

- Auto-assign based on criteria

- Breed-specific routing
- VIP flagging

- Answer common questions

- Seamless data flow

## Lesson 15: Waitlist Processing

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Create and manage waitlists
- Process waitlist applications
- Prioritize waitlist positions
- Communicate with waitlist members
- Match puppies to waitlist families
- Manage deposits and commitments
- Handle waitlist changes and cancellations
- Generate waitlist reports

### Understanding Waitlist Management

#### What is a Waitlist?

A waitlist is:

- Queue of approved buyers awaiting puppies
- Organized by priority and preference
- Commitment demonstrated by deposit
- Pipeline for future litters
- Professional buyer management system

**Benefits of Waitlists:**

- **For Breeders:**

  - Know puppy homes in advance
  - Financial planning (deposits)
  - Quality buyer pool
  - Less pressure per litter
  - Professional image

- **For Buyers:**
  - Guaranteed consideration
  - Priority access
  - Time to prepare
  - Relationship building
  - Peace of mind

> ðŸ’¡ **Best Practice**: Most professional breeders maintain waitlists for quality control

### Waitlist Basics

![Screenshot: Waitlist overview page]

#### Waitlist Structure

**By Litter:**

- Specific litter waitlist
- Due date known
- Position matters
- First choice by order
- Clear timeline

**General Waitlist:**

- No specific litter assigned
- Next available puppy
- More flexible
- Preferences matter more
- Longer wait possible

**Puppy-Specific Waitlist:**

- Waiting for very specific traits
- Rare colors
- Show prospects
- Specific temperament
- May wait multiple litters

#### Waitlist Positions

**Priority Levels:**

**1. Priority/VIP**

- Past customers (first right)
- Referral customers
- Co-breeder arrangements
- Special circumstances
- Top of list

**2. Standard**

- Deposit paid
- Application approved
- Order by deposit date
- Normal queue

**3. Interested**

- No deposit yet
- Approved but not committed
- Below deposited families
- May lose position

**4. Backup**

- Secondary choice
- If preferences not met
- Below active waitlist
- Gets notifications but no guarantee

### Adding to Waitlist

![Screenshot: Add to waitlist form]

#### Waitlist Application

**Required Information:**

**Customer Details:**

- Must exist in customer database
- All contact info complete
- Application approved
- References checked

**Litter Assignment:**

- Specific litter (recommended)
- Next available (any litter)
- Seasonal (Spring 2025, etc.)
- Breed (if you breed multiple)

**Preferences:**

- Gender: Male, Female, No preference
- Color: Specific or any
- Size: Small, medium, large (within breed)
- Temperament: Active, calm, balanced, etc.
- Purpose: Pet, show, breeding, sport, service

**Priority Level:**

- Select from dropdown
- Affects position
- Can adjust later
- Note reason if VIP

**Deposit Information:**

- Deposit amount: $[amount]
- Payment method: Check, credit, wire, etc.
- Date received
- Applied to purchase price
- Refund policy acknowledged

**Timeline:**

- Preferred pickup date
- Earliest acceptable
- Latest acceptable
- Flexibility level

**Special Requests:**

- Gender must-have vs. preference
- Color dealbreaker or flexible?
- Specific traits required
- Health considerations
- Training needs

#### Waitlist Position Assignment

**Automatic Positioning:**

- System assigns based on:
  - Priority level (VIP first)
  - Deposit date/time
  - Preferences match
  - Litter assignment

**Manual Positioning:**

- Override automatic
- Move up/down list
- Swap positions
- Note reason for change

**Example Waitlist:**

```
Spring 2025 Litter Waitlist:

1. VIP - Smith Family (repeat customer)
   Female, golden, family pet - Deposit paid 11/1

2. Martinez Family
   No gender pref, any color, active family - Deposit paid 11/15

3. Johnson Family
   Male, dark golden, show prospect - Deposit paid 11/20

4. Chen Family
   Female, golden, service prospect - Deposit paid 11/22

5. INTERESTED - Davis Family
   Male, any color, family pet - No deposit yet
```

### Matching Puppies to Waitlist

![Screenshot: Puppy matching interface]

#### The Matching Process

**When to Match:**

- Puppies 6-7 weeks old
- Temperaments emerging
- Health confirmed
- Evaluations complete

**Matching Criteria:**

**1. Position Priority:**

- VIP/Priority first choice
- Then by deposit order
- Preferences considered
- Must-haves vs. wants

**2. Temperament Match:**

- Active family â†’ energetic puppy
- Quiet home â†’ calm puppy
- Experienced â†’ confident puppy
- First-time â†’ easy puppy

**3. Purpose Match:**

- Show prospect â†’ best structure
- Service/therapy â†’ specific temperament
- Family pet â†’ well-rounded
- Sport â†’ drive and focus

**4. Physical Preferences:**

- Gender (if must-have)
- Size (within litter range)
- Color (if dealbreaker)
- Markings

**5. Lifestyle Match:**

- Activity level compatibility
- Home environment fit
- Family dynamics
- Experience level

#### Matching Interface

**Matching Tool:**

1. Select litter
2. View waitlist
3. View available puppies
4. Drag puppy to family OR
5. Click "Suggest Match"
6. System recommends based on preferences
7. Review and adjust
8. Confirm matches
9. Send notifications

**Match Card Shows:**

- Family name and position
- Their preferences
- Matched puppy
- Match score (%)
- Reasons for match
- Approval status

**Example Matches:**

```
Position 1: Smith Family
Matched: Female, Golden, "Sunny"
Match Score: 95%
Reasons:
âœ“ Gender preference met
âœ“ Color preference met
âœ“ Calm temperament for older couple
âœ“ Medium size perfect
Status: Confirmed

Position 2: Martinez Family
Matched: Male, Dark Golden, "Bear"
Match Score: 88%
Reasons:
âœ“ Active family = energetic puppy
âœ“ Color preference met
âœ“ Larger size for active lifestyle
Note: Gender was "no preference"
Status: Awaiting approval
```

### Deposits and Financial Tracking

![Screenshot: Deposit management]

#### Deposit Management

**Recording Deposits:**

1. Waitlist entry
2. Enter deposit amount
3. Payment method
4. Date received
5. Payment processor reference
6. Generates receipt
7. Marks waitlist entry "Deposit Paid"

**Deposit Amounts:**

- Standard: $[amount]
- Refundable until [timeframe]
- Applied to purchase price
- Hold position on list
- Document policy clearly

**Payment Methods:**

- Credit/debit card
- PayPal/Venmo
- Check/money order
- Wire transfer
- Cash (receipt required)

**Receipt Generation:**

- Automatic upon entry
- Email to customer
- Include deposit terms
- Refund policy
- Applied to invoice

**Deposit Tracking:**

- Total deposits held
- By litter
- Pending deposits
- Refunded deposits
- Applied deposits

#### Balance Due Management

**When Match Confirmed:**

1. Puppy assigned
2. Calculate balance:
   - Purchase price
   - Minus deposit
   - Plus any extras
3. Generate invoice
4. Send to customer
5. Set due date
6. Track payment

**Payment Schedule:**

- Deposit: At waitlist entry
- Partial payment: [timeframe] (optional)
- Balance due: Before pickup (typically 1 week)
- Final payment: At pickup or before

**Late Payment Process:**

1. Payment past due
2. Send reminder (auto)
3. Phone call if still late
4. Escalation if needed
5. Could forfeit puppy (policy dependent)

### Waitlist Changes and Cancellations

![Screenshot: Waitlist modification options]

#### Customer Withdrawals

**Reasons for Withdrawal:**

- Life changes (moving, divorce, etc.)
- Financial hardship
- Timeline doesn't work
- Found puppy elsewhere
- Changed mind
- Health issues

**Withdrawal Process:**

1. Customer notifies you
2. Update waitlist entry status
3. Process refund (if applicable)
4. Send confirmation
5. Move others up
6. Notify affected parties
7. Document reason

**Refund Policy:**

- Before litter born: Full refund OR
- After birth, before selection: Partial OR
- After selection: Non-refundable
- **Must be clearly stated in contract**

#### Breeder-Initiated Removal

**When to Remove:**

- Failed reference check (late discovery)
- Misrepresentation on application
- Communication breakdown
- Disrespectful behavior
- Changed circumstances (home, etc.)
- Non-responsive
- Deposit disputes

**Removal Process:**

1. Document reasons
2. Notify customer
3. Explain decision
4. Process refund
5. Update waitlist
6. Move others up
7. Keep records

**Professional Communication:**

```
Dear [Name],

After careful consideration, I've decided that we may
not be the best fit for your family at this time.

[Specific reason if appropriate]

I'm issuing a full refund of your deposit, which you
should receive within [timeframe].

I wish you the best in finding the perfect companion
and recommend [alternative if appropriate].

Best regards,
[Your Name]
```

   - Gender: Female
   - Color: Any

8. Check if notifications sent

**Exercise 4: Match Puppies to Waitlist**

1. Litter with puppies (6+ weeks old)
2. Go to waitlist tab
3. Click "Match Puppies"
4. Review each family's preferences
5. Review each puppy's traits
6. Assign puppies to families:
   - Position 1 gets first choice match
   - Consider preferences and temperament
7. Save matches
8. Send match notifications

**Exercise 5: Process Waitlist Withdrawal**

1. Select waitlist entry
2. Click "Edit" or menu â†’ "Withdraw"
3. Select reason: "Life change"
4. Process refund:
   - Amount: $500 (full deposit)
   - Method: Original payment method
5. Add note: "Family relocated for job"
6. Update status to "Cancelled"
7. Send confirmation email
8. Check others moved up

**Exercise 6: Generate Waitlist Report**

1. Go to Waitlist â†’ Reports
2. Select "Waitlist Summary"
3. Date range: Last 6 months
4. Include:
   - Positions filled
   - Average wait time
   - Deposits received
   - Cancellation rate
5. Generate report
6. Review metrics
7. Export as PDF
8. Identify insights

### Tooltips and Quick Help

> ðŸ“Š **Position Calculator**: System estimates likely match date based on breeding schedule

> ðŸ”” **Auto-Updates**: Waitlist auto-notified at key milestones without manual emails

> ðŸ’° **Deposit Security**: Deposits held securely, automatically applied at purchase

> ðŸŽ¯ **Match Scoring**: Algorithm suggests best puppy matches based on 20+ factors

> ðŸ“± **Waitlist Portal**: Customers can view their position and updates online

> ðŸ”„ **Waitlist Transfer**: Move customers between litters if needed

> ðŸ“§ **Bulk Actions**: Email, update, or export multiple waitlist entries at once

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Customer disputes waitlist position**

- Solution: Show deposit timestamp, explain priority system, offer transparency

**Problem: Not enough puppies for entire waitlist**

- Solution: Discuss with bottom positions, offer next litter, refund if desired

**Problem: Everyone wants same gender/color**

- Solution: Review preferences (must-have vs. nice-to-have), emphasize temperament match

**Problem: Customer stops responding**

- Solution: Multiple contact attempts, deadline for response, move to backup if no reply

**Problem: Deposit refund disputed**

- Solution: Reference signed contract, show policy, document everything, legal advice if needed

**Problem: Waitlist member wants to skip ahead**

- Solution: Politely decline, explain fairness, offer next litter priority if flexible

### Advanced Features

**Waitlist Website Integration:**

- Public waitlist count display
- Online application submission
- Deposit payment portal
- Position checking
- Update notifications

**Automated Waitlist Management:**

- Auto-advance positions
- Smart matching suggestions
- Automated communications
- Payment reminders
- Timeline projections

**Waitlist Analytics:**

- Predictive modeling
- Demand forecasting
- Optimal pricing
- Breeding schedule optimization

**Multi-Breeder Waitlists:**

- Co-breeder shared waitlists
- Transfer between breeders
- Collaborative matching
- Split litters

**Waitlist Marketing:**

- Waitlist-only content
- Early access to photos
- VIP treatment
- Referral incentives
- Alumni benefits

# Module 5: Sales and Contracts

## Lesson 16: Puppy Sales Process

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Guide buyers through the sales process
- Manage puppy reservations and deposits
- Process final payments
- Track sales transactions
- Handle payment methods securely
- Generate sales receipts and invoices
- Manage refunds and disputes
- Maintain financial records

### Understanding the Sales Process

#### Sales Process Overview

The complete sales journey:

1. **Inquiry** - Initial contact
2. **Qualification** - Application and approval
3. **Waitlist** - Deposit and position
4. **Matching** - Puppy assignment
5. **Reservation** - Commitment confirmed
6. **Payment** - Balance due
7. **Pickup** - Puppy goes home
8. **Follow-up** - Post-placement support

> ðŸ’¡ **Professional Standard**: Clear, documented sales process protects both breeder and buyer

### Reservation Process

![Screenshot: Puppy reservation interface]

#### Creating a Reservation

**When Puppy is Matched:**

1. Puppy assigned to buyer
2. Reservation automatically created
3. Status changes: Available â†’ Reserved
4. Buyer notified
5. Payment timeline starts

**Manual Reservation:**

1. Open puppy details
2. Click **"Reserve Puppy"**
3. Select customer from list
4. Enter reservation details
5. Set payment terms
6. Generate contract
7. Save reservation

**Reservation Details:**

**Puppy Information:**

- Name/collar color
- Age
- Gender
- Color/markings
- Microchip number (if chipped)
- Health status

**Buyer Information:**

- Customer name
- Contact details
- Address
- Email for documents
- Phone for coordination

**Financial Terms:**

- Purchase price: $[amount]
- Deposit paid: $[amount]
- Balance due: $[calculated]
- Due date: [date]
- Payment method options
- Late payment policy

**Pickup Details:**

- Pickup date: [date]
- Pickup time: [time]
- Location: Your kennel OR
- Delivery/shipping arranged
- Requirements (crate, paperwork, etc.)

**Status Tracking:**

- Reservation date
- Contract status (sent/signed/complete)
- Payment status (partial/pending/paid)
- Pickup status (scheduled/complete)

### Payment Management

![Screenshot: Payment tracking dashboard]

#### Payment Structure

**Standard Payment Schedule:**

**Deposit (Waitlist Stage):**

- Amount: $[amount] (typically $500-1000)
- Purpose: Hold position on waitlist
- Timing: When joining waitlist
- Refundable: Per policy terms
- Applied: Toward purchase price

**Balance Due:**

- Amount: Purchase price minus deposit
- Timing: Typically 1 week before pickup
- Methods: Multiple options
- Required: Before puppy goes home
- Invoice: Generated automatically

**Payment at Pickup:**

- If balance still owed
- Cash or certified funds
- Immediate receipt
- Complete transaction
- Release puppy

**Example:**

```
Purchase Price: $3,000
Deposit Paid: $500 (11/15/2024)
Balance Due: $2,500
Due Date: 1/20/2025 (1 week before pickup)
Final Pickup: 1/27/2025
```

#### Recording Payments

![Screenshot: Add payment form]

**Adding Payment Record:**

1. Open puppy or customer record
2. Go to **"Payments"** tab
3. Click **"Add Payment"**
4. Enter payment details
5. Generate receipt
6. Email to customer
7. Update balance

**Payment Form Fields:**

**Amount** (Required)

- Dollar amount received
- Example: $500.00
- Validates against balance

**Date** (Required)

- Date payment received
- Format: MM/DD/YYYY
- Defaults to today
- Can backdate if needed

**Payment Method** (Required)

- Credit/Debit Card
- PayPal
- Venmo/Zelle/CashApp
- Check
- Money Order
- Wire Transfer
- Cash

**Reference Number** (Recommended)

- Check number
- Transaction ID
- Confirmation code
- Tracking for disputes
- Required for some methods

**Notes** (Optional)

- Any special circumstances
- Partial payment arrangements
- Late fee applied
- Discount given
- Payment plan details

**Applied To:**

- Deposit
- Balance
- Additional fees (shipping, etc.)
- Supplies/extras
- Refund (negative amount)

#### Payment Methods

**Credit/Debit Cards:**

- Pros: Instant, secure, convenient
- Cons: Processing fees (2-3%)
- Tools: Square, Stripe, PayPal
- Documentation: Transaction ID
- Chargeback: Risk exists

**PayPal/Payment Apps:**

- Pros: Popular, easy, secure
- Cons: Fees, friends/family policy violations
- Options: PayPal, Venmo, Zelle, CashApp
- Documentation: Transaction ID and screenshot
- Policy: Use "goods and services" for protection

**Checks:**

- Pros: No fees, paper trail
- Cons: Can bounce, processing time
- Requirements: Clear funds before puppy goes home
- Hold time: 5-7 business days
- Bounced check: Fee + possible legal action

**Money Orders:**

- Pros: Guaranteed funds, no bounce
- Cons: Inconvenient for buyer
- Verification: Call issuing bank
- Safe option: Especially for large amounts

**Wire Transfer:**

- Pros: Secure, instant, large amounts
- Cons: Fees, international complexity
- Use for: Distant/international buyers
- Verification: Confirm receipt before release

**Cash:**

- Pros: Immediate, no fees
- Cons: Security risk, no automatic record
- Best practice: Count together, immediate receipt
- Large amounts: Meet at bank
- Documentation: Essential

> âš ï¸ **Security**: Never release puppy until all funds cleared and verified

### Invoicing

![Screenshot: Invoice generation interface]

#### Creating Invoices

**Automatic Invoice Generation:**

- Created when puppy reserved
- Updates with payments
- Shows balance due
- Payment terms included
- Emailed automatically

**Manual Invoice Creation:**

1. Customer or puppy record
2. Click **"Generate Invoice"**
3. Select items/services
4. Review amounts
5. Set due date
6. Add payment instructions
7. Send to customer

**Invoice Components:**

**Header:**

- Your business name/logo
- Address and contact
- Invoice number (auto-generated)
- Invoice date
- Due date

**Bill To:**

- Customer name
- Address
- Email
- Phone

**Line Items:**

- Puppy: [Name/ID] - $[price]
- Microchip (if charged separately) - $[amount]
- Registration (if included) - $[amount]
- Shipping (if applicable) - $[amount]
- Puppy supplies - $[amount]
- **Subtotal**

**Payments Applied:**

- Deposit (Date) - -$[amount]
- Payment (Date) - -$[amount]
- **Total Paid**

**Balance Due:** $[amount]

**Payment Instructions:**

- Accepted methods
- Payment links (if online)
- Due date reminder
- Late payment policy
- Contact for questions

**Footer:**

- Thank you message
- Terms and conditions reference
- Tax ID (if applicable)
- Business registration info

#### Invoice Tracking

**Invoice Status:**

- **Draft**: Not yet sent
- **Sent**: Emailed to customer
- **Viewed**: Customer opened email
- **Partial**: Some payment received
- **Paid**: Fully paid
- **Overdue**: Past due date
- **Cancelled**: Voided/refunded

**Automatic Reminders:**

- 7 days before due date
- 3 days before due date
- On due date
- 3 days overdue
- 7 days overdue
- Custom reminder schedule

**Payment Links:**

- Include in invoice email
- Direct payment portal
- Secure processing
- Instant confirmation
- Reduces friction

### Sales Documentation

![Screenshot: Sales documents checklist]

#### Required Documents

**Sales Contract:**

- Terms of sale
- Health guarantee
- Buyer responsibilities
- Return policy
- Breeding rights (if applicable)
- Both parties sign
- Each keeps copy

**Bill of Sale:**

- Legal proof of ownership
- Purchase price
- Date of sale
- Puppy identification
- Buyer and seller signatures
- Required for some registrations

**Health Certificate:**

- Vet health exam
- Vaccination records
- Deworming history
- Microchip information
- Health guarantee terms
- Vet signature and date

**Registration Papers:**

- AKC/CKC application
- Limited or full registration
- Instructions for buyer
- Transfer information
- Registration fees (who pays)

**Puppy Information Packet:**

- Care instructions
- Feeding schedule
- Training tips
- Socialization recommendations
- Emergency contacts
- Your contact info
- Recommended products

**Receipt of Payment:**

- Deposit receipt
- Final payment receipt
- Total amount paid
- Payment method
- Date of payment
- Both parties copy

#### Document Management

**Organization System:**

- By customer name
- By puppy ID
- By date
- By litter
- Digital and physical copies

**Digital Storage:**

- Scan all signed documents
- Cloud backup
- Searchable by customer/puppy
- Access anywhere
- Secure/encrypted

**Physical Storage:**

- File by year
- Alphabetical by customer
- Fire-safe if possible
- Organized system
- Easy retrieval

**Retention Period:**

- Keep indefinitely recommended
- Minimum 7 years (legal)
- Digital permanent storage
- Physical space allowing
- Important for disputes/claims
