**Forms and Reporting:**

- 1099 if applicable
- Business income (Schedule C)
- Sales tax (if applicable)
- State requirements
- Professional guidance recommended

> ðŸ’¡ **Tax Tip**: Consult with accountant familiar with breeding businesses

### Handling Special Situations

![Screenshot: Refund and adjustment interface]

#### Refunds and Cancellations

**Buyer Cancellation:**

**Before Puppy Born:**

- Full refund typical
- Or transfer to another litter
- Minimal loss to breeder
- Waitlist adjusted

**After Born, Before Pickup:**

- Per contract terms
- Partial refund common
- Or no refund (varies)
- Resell puppy to next person
- Clear policy prevents disputes

**After Pickup:**

- Rare
- Per return policy
- May take puppy back
- Partial refund possible
- Reselling/rehoming costs

**Processing Refund:**

1. Confirm cancellation in writing
2. Review contract terms
3. Calculate refund amount
4. Process refund via original method
5. Update records
6. Remove reservation
7. Adjust waitlist
8. Resell puppy

**Breeder Cancellation:**

**Valid Reasons:**

- Puppy health issues
- Buyer misrepresented situation
- Buyer became unsuitable
- Litter didn't happen
- Fewer puppies than expected

**Process:**

1. Notify buyer immediately
2. Explain situation clearly
3. Offer alternatives:
   - Different puppy
   - Next litter
   - Full refund
4. Process per contract
5. Maintain professionalism
6. Document everything

#### Payment Plans

**When to Offer:**

- Qualified buyer, temporary hardship
- Large balance
- Repeat customer
- Builds relationship
- Your discretion

**Payment Plan Structure:**

```
Example Payment Plan:
Total Price: $3,000
Deposit Paid: $500
Balance: $2,500

Plan:
- $500 due 1/1/2025
- $500 due 1/15/2025
- $500 due 1/30/2025
- $500 due 2/15/2025
- $500 due 2/28/2025 (pickup date)

Terms:
- All payments must clear before pickup
- Missed payment = puppy available to others
- No interest charged
- Puppy held until fully paid
```

**Payment Plan Agreement:**

- Written terms
- Payment schedule
- Consequences of late payment
- Signed by both parties
- Attached to contract

**Tracking Payment Plans:**

- Schedule in system
- Automatic reminders
- Track paid/pending
- Alert on missed payments
- Update customer record

#### Disputes and Issues

**Common Disputes:**

- Payment not received/recorded
- Refund disagreement
- Pricing confusion
- Hidden fees claim
- Contract interpretation

**Resolution Steps:**

1. Stay calm and professional
2. Review documentation
3. Understand buyer perspective
4. Reference contract terms
5. Seek fair resolution
6. Document conversation
7. Get agreement in writing
8. Follow through completely

**Prevention:**

- Clear contracts
- Transparent pricing
- Document everything
- Communication
- Set expectations early
- Professional conduct

**When to Involve Legal:**

- Large amounts disputed
- Threats or harassment
- Fraud suspected
- Contract breach
- Small claims consideration
- Consult attorney first

> ðŸ“± **Mobile Payments**: Accept payments via mobile card readers on the go

> ðŸ’° **Deposit Tracking**: System automatically applies deposits to final balance

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Payment showing as not received**

- Solution: Check all payment records, search by transaction ID, contact payment processor

**Problem: Invoice showing wrong amount**

- Solution: Review line items, check for duplicate entries, recalculate manually

**Problem: Customer claims they paid but no record**

- Solution: Request proof (screenshot, receipt), check all payment methods, verify dates

**Problem: Refund processing error**

- Solution: Verify original payment method still valid, try different method, contact support

**Problem: Cannot reconcile accounts**

- Solution: Export all transactions, compare to bank statements, identify discrepancies

**Problem: Duplicate payment recorded**

- Solution: Void one entry, issue refund if money actually charged twice

- Recurring payments

## Lesson 17: Contract Generation

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Create puppy sales contracts
- Customize contract templates
- Include essential legal terms
- Generate contracts for different scenarios
- Obtain digital signatures
- Store and manage signed contracts
- Understand contract enforceability
- Handle contract amendments

### Understanding Puppy Contracts

#### Why Contracts Matter

Contracts protect:

- **Breeder**: From misuse, neglect, breeding violations
- **Buyer**: Investment, health guarantees, support
- **Puppy**: Proper care, return if needed, welfare

**Legal Benefits:**

- Enforceable terms
- Clear expectations
- Dispute resolution
- Liability protection
- Professional standard

> âš ï¸ **Legal Note**: Have attorney review your contract template for your state/region

### Contract Essentials

![Screenshot: Contract template editor]

#### Core Contract Elements

**1. Party Identification:**

```
This agreement made on [DATE] between:

BREEDER:
[Your Name/Business Name]
[Address]
[City, State ZIP]
[Phone]
[Email]

BUYER:
[Buyer Name]
[Address]
[City, State ZIP]
[Phone]
[Email]
```

**2. Puppy Identification:**

```
PUPPY DESCRIPTION:
Breed: [Breed]
Sex: [Male/Female]
Date of Birth: [DOB]
Color: [Color and markings]
Microchip #: [Number]
Registration #: [If applicable]
Sire: [Father's name and registration]
Dam: [Mother's name and registration]
```

**3. Purchase Price:**

```
PURCHASE PRICE: $[Amount]

Payment Schedule:
- Deposit: $[Amount] paid [Date]
- Balance: $[Amount] due [Date]
- Total Paid: $[Total]

Payment Method: [Method]
```

**4. Health Guarantee:**

- Coverage period (typically 1-2 years)
- Covered conditions (genetic/congenital)
- Excluded conditions (accidents, neglect)
- Veterinary requirements (timeline for exam)
- Remedy options (replacement, refund)
- Buyer responsibilities (proper care)

**Example Health Guarantee:**

```
HEALTH GUARANTEE:

Breeder guarantees this puppy to be free from life-threatening
genetic defects for a period of TWO (2) YEARS from date of birth.

Covered Conditions:
- Hip dysplasia (OFA/PennHIP confirmed severe)
- Elbow dysplasia (OFA grade III)
- Heart defects (congenital, confirmed by specialist)
- Eye defects (hereditary, confirmed by ophthalmologist)

Buyer Responsibilities:
- Veterinary exam within 72 hours of pickup
- Maintain proper weight and nutrition
- Follow exercise restrictions for large breed puppies
- Provide veterinary care as needed

Remedy:
In the event of a covered condition, Breeder will:
1. Replacement puppy from next available litter, OR
2. Refund of purchase price

Return of affected dog is NOT required.
Veterinary expenses are NOT covered.
```

**5. Spay/Neuter Agreement:**

```
LIMITED REGISTRATION / PET CONTRACT:

Buyer agrees to spay/neuter this puppy by [age] months.

Proof Required:
- Veterinary certificate of sterilization
- To be sent to Breeder within 30 days of procedure

Penalty:
- Failure to comply voids health guarantee
- $[Amount] penalty
- Puppy may be reclaimed

OR

BREEDING RIGHTS:
This puppy is sold with full AKC registration and
breeding rights. Buyer agrees to:
- Complete all health testing before breeding
- Follow breed club code of ethics
- Screen all puppy buyers
- Provide lifetime support to puppy buyers
```

**6. Return Policy:**

```
RETURN / REHOMING POLICY:

If Buyer cannot keep puppy at ANY time in the dog's life:

Required:
- Contact Breeder first
- Give Breeder right of first refusal
- DO NOT take to shelter or rescue

Breeder Will:
- Take dog back (no refund)
- Assist in rehoming (approved home)
- Provide support and resources

Buyer Must NEVER:
- Sell or give to unknown parties
- Relinquish to shelter or pound
- Use for research or experimentation
```

**7. Buyer Responsibilities:**

```
BUYER AGREES TO:

Medical Care:
- Veterinary exam within 72 hours
- Complete vaccination series
- Annual veterinary check-ups
- Heartworm and flea prevention
- Immediate care for illness/injury

Nutrition:
- Feed high-quality dog food
- Maintain healthy weight
- Fresh water always available
- No table scraps or harmful foods

Environment:
- Safe, secure housing
- Adequate exercise and socialization
- Protection from weather extremes
- Never chained or confined excessively

Training:
- Basic obedience training
- Positive reinforcement methods
- Proper socialization
- No aggressive training methods
```

**8. Breeder Rights:**

```
BREEDER RESERVES RIGHT TO:

- Visit dog with reasonable notice
- Reclaim dog if contract violated
- Void health guarantee if terms broken
- Require proof of proper care
- Be notified of major medical issues
- Approve any breeding (if applicable)
```

**9. Dispute Resolution:**

```
GOVERNING LAW:
This agreement governed by laws of [State].

Disputes:
- Mediation required before litigation
- Venue: [County], [State]
- Prevailing party entitled to legal fees
- Severability: Invalid clauses don't void contract
```

**10. Signatures:**

```
BREEDER SIGNATURE: _________________ DATE: _______
[Printed Name]

BUYER SIGNATURE: _________________ DATE: _______
[Printed Name]

WITNESS (optional): _________________ DATE: _______
```

### Contract Templates

![Screenshot: Template library]

#### Pre-Built Templates

**Pet Home Contract:**

- Standard pet sale
- Limited registration
- Spay/neuter required
- No breeding rights
- Basic health guarantee
- Most common type

**Show Prospect Contract:**

- Full registration included
- Higher price point
- Show requirements/goals
- Health testing requirements
- Co-ownership optional
- Return if not show quality

**Breeding Rights Contract:**

- Full registration
- Breeding allowed
- Health testing mandatory
- Screening requirements
- Code of ethics compliance
- Breeding restrictions (age, frequency)
- Puppy placement standards

**Co-Ownership Contract:**

- Shared ownership
- Define each party's rights
- Breeding schedule
- Puppy selection/placement
- Financial split
- Decision-making
- Term length
- Exit strategy

**Guardian Home Contract:**

- Dog lives with family
- Breeder retains breeding rights
- Return for breeding
- Care requirements
- Financial arrangements
- Offspring rights
- Length of agreement
- Ownership transfer when retired

**Stud Service Contract:**

- Use of your stud
- Stud fee amount
- Payment terms
- Breeding schedule
- Pick puppy vs. fee
- Health requirements
- Liability

#### Customizing Templates

**Template Customization:**

1. Select base template
2. Click **"Customize"**
3. Edit standard clauses
4. Add custom clauses
5. Adjust terms
6. Set defaults
7. Save as custom template
8. Use for future sales

**Merge Fields:**

- {buyer_name}
- {buyer_address}
- {puppy_name}
- {puppy_dob}
- {puppy_microchip}
- {purchase_price}
- {deposit_amount}
- {balance_due}
- {pickup_date}
- {breeder_name}
- {current_date}

**Auto-Population:**

- Fields fill from database
- Reduce errors
- Save time
- Consistent formatting
- Professional appearance

1. Puppy assigned to buyer

6. Customize if needed
7. Generate PDF
8. Email to buyer
9. Await signature

**Manual Generation:**

1. Open puppy or customer record
2. Click **"Generate Contract"**
3. Select contract type
4. Choose template
5. Review and edit
6. Generate document
7. Send for signature

**Multi-Document Packages:**

- Sales contract
- Bill of sale
- Health certificate
- Registration application
- Care instructions
- Return policy
- All in one PDF

#### Contract Review Checklist

**Before Sending:**

- â˜ All fields populated correctly
- â˜ Names spelled correctly
- â˜ Dates accurate
- â˜ Prices correct
- â˜ Terms appropriate for this sale
- â˜ Custom clauses added if needed
- â˜ Grammar and spelling checked
- â˜ Legal review if major changes
- â˜ Formatted professionally
- â˜ All pages included

**Common Errors:**

- Wrong buyer name
- Incorrect puppy info

- Missing pages

- Wrong prices
- Conflicting terms

### Digital Signatures

![Screenshot: Digital signature interface]

#### E-Signature Process

**Sending for Signature:**

1. Generate contract
2. Click **"Send for Signature"**
3. Enter buyer email
4. Add message
5. Set signing order (if multiple parties)
6. Send invitation

**Buyer Experience:**

1. Receives email
2. Clicks signature link
3. Reviews contract
4. Signs with mouse/touch
5. Types name
6. Submits signature
7. Receives signed copy

**E-Signature Features:**

- Legally binding (ESIGN Act)
- Timestamped
- IP address recorded
- Audit trail maintained
- Can't be altered after signing
- Automatic storage
- Instant notifications

**Signature Methods:**

- Draw signature
- Type name (cursive font)
- Upload signature image
- Initial each page option
- Date automatically added

**Platform Options:**

- DocuSign
- HelloSign
- Adobe Sign
- PandaDoc
- Built-in system

#### Paper Signatures

**When to Use:**

- Buyer preference
- At pickup
- No internet access
- Legal requirements
- Backup copy

**Process:**

1. Print contract (2 copies minimum)
2. Review with buyer
3. Both parties sign all copies
4. Both parties initial each page (optional)
5. Date all signatures
6. Each party keeps signed copy
7. Scan for digital storage

**Storage:**

- File physical copy
- Scan to PDF
- Upload to system
- Attach to customer record
- Cloud backup

### Contract Management

![Screenshot: Contract management dashboard]

#### Tracking Contract Status

**Contract Statuses:**

- **Draft**: Created but not sent
- **Sent**: Sent to buyer, awaiting signature
- **Viewed**: Buyer opened document
- **Signed**: Buyer completed signature
- **Complete**: All parties signed
- **Voided**: Cancelled/invalidated
- **Expired**: Signature deadline passed

**Status Dashboard:**

- Contracts awaiting signature
- Recently completed
- Expiring soon
- Overdue
- Filter by status
- Sort by date
- Quick actions

**Reminders:**

- Sent X days after initial
- Before expiration
- Follow-up schedule
- Automatic or manual
- Customizable timing

#### Contract Storage

**Organization:**

- By customer name
- By puppy
- By date
- By contract type
- By litter
- Searchable database

**Document Linking:**

- Link to customer record
- Link to puppy record
- Link to litter
- Link to payments
- Link to correspondence
- Complete audit trail

**Backup:**

- Cloud storage
- Automatic backup
- Multiple locations
- Encrypted
- Retrieval tested
- Retention forever

**Access Control:**

- Who can view
- Who can edit
- Who can delete
- Audit log
- Version history
- Permission levels

### Contract Amendments

![Screenshot: Amendment creation form]

#### When Amendments Needed

**Common Reasons:**

- Price adjustment
- Payment plan change
- Date change
- Terms clarification
- Additional agreements
- Correcting errors

**Amendment Process:**

1. Identify needed change
2. Document reason
3. Create amendment document
4. Reference original contract
5. Specify changes
6. Both parties sign amendment
7. Attach to original
8. Update records

**Amendment Template:**

```
AMENDMENT TO PUPPY SALES CONTRACT

Original Contract Date: [Date]
Between: [Breeder] and [Buyer]
Regarding: [Puppy identification]

The parties agree to amend the contract as follows:

AMENDED TERMS:
[Specific changes detailed]

UNCHANGED TERMS:
All other terms of the original contract remain in
full force and effect.

Breeder Signature: _____________ Date: _______
Buyer Signature: _____________ Date: _______
```

**Amendment Best Practices:**

- Get in writing
- Both parties agree
- Reference original
- Be specific
- Sign and date
- Store with original
- Update system records

### Special Contract Scenarios

![Screenshot: Specialized contract options]

#### Co-Ownership Agreements

**Structure:**

```
CO-OWNERSHIP AGREEMENT

This agreement made between:
OWNER 1 (Breeder): [Name]
OWNER 2 (Guardian): [Name]

Regarding: [Puppy identification]

TERMS:

Ownership:
- Dog owned jointly
- Registration shows both owners
- Equal rights unless specified

Physical Custody:
- Dog resides with: [Guardian name]
- At: [Guardian address]

Breeding Rights:
- Breeding decisions by: [Breeder]
- Return for breeding: [Terms]
- Whelping location: [Location]
- Care during pregnancy: [Details]

Financial Responsibility:
- Routine care: [Guardian pays]
- Breeding-related: [Breeder pays]
- Major medical: [Split or specify]

Offspring:
- Pick puppy: [Who gets what]
- Stud fees: [If applicable]
- Puppy placement: [Who handles]

Duration:
- [X] litters OR [X] years
- Full ownership transfers to: [Guardian]
- Upon: [Condition - retirement, age, etc.]

Termination:
- Either party may terminate with [notice]
- Dog custody upon termination: [Guardian]
- Registration transfer: [Process]
```

#### Guardian Home Programs

**Guardian Agreement:**

- Family raises dog
- Dog lives in home
- Breeder retains breeding rights
- Return for breeding
- Free or reduced price puppy
- Ownership transfers after retirement

**Key Terms:**

- Care requirements
- Return schedule
- Breeding expectations
- Financial arrangements
- Veterinary decisions
- Termination conditions

#### Breeding Rights

**Selling Breeding Rights:**

- Higher purchase price
- Health testing required
- Breeder approval of mates
- Puppy placement standards
- Code of ethics
- Can revoke if violated

**Breeding Rights Clause:**

```
FULL REGISTRATION WITH BREEDING RIGHTS

Buyer purchases breeding rights for $[Additional Amount].

Requirements:
1. Complete all breed-recommended health testing
2. Achieve minimum health certification scores
3. Obtain breeder approval for all breeding
4. Follow [Breed] Club Code of Ethics
5. Screen all puppy buyers thoroughly
6. Provide proper puppy care and socialization
7. Issue health guarantees to buyers
8. Offer lifetime support to buyers

Breeder May Revoke Rights If:
- Health testing not completed by age [X]
- Breeding without approval
- Substandard care or placement
- Code of ethics violations

Upon Revocation:
- No refund of breeding rights fee
- Registration changed to limited
- Legal action for violations
```

- Solution: Check PDF settings, try different browser, regenerate document

**Problem: Signature not saving**

- Solution: Check browser compatibility, clear cache, try different device

**Problem: Lost signed contract**

- Solution: Check document storage, search by customer name, contact e-sign platform

**Problem: Need to void signed contract**

- Solution: Mark as void in system, create new contract, document reason

## Lesson 18: Digital Signatures and Document Management

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Implement digital signature workflows
- Understand e-signature legal requirements
- Set up signature reminders and deadlines
- Manage document versions
- Track signature status
- Handle signature issues
- Ensure document security
- Maintain compliance records

### Digital Signature Basics

#### Legal Framework

**ESIGN Act (USA):**

- Electronic signatures legally binding
- Same validity as handwritten signatures
- Must show intent to sign
- Consent to electronic transactions
- Record retention required

**UETA (Uniform Electronic Transactions Act):**

- Adopted by most US states
- Electronic records admissible
- Cannot be denied legal effect
- Party must consent

**International Considerations:**

- eIDAS (European Union)
- Other country regulations
- Cross-border enforceability
- Compliance requirements

> âš ï¸ **Important**: E-signatures valid for most contracts, but check specific requirements for your jurisdiction

#### E-Signature Types

**Simple Electronic Signature:**

- Typed name
- Scanned signature
- Checkbox consent
- Basic authentication
- Common for low-risk documents

**Advanced Electronic Signature:**

- Uniquely linked to signatory
- Identity verification
- Signer control only
- Detects subsequent changes
- Higher security

**Qualified Electronic Signature:**

- Highest legal weight
- Certificate-based
- Secure signature device
- Identity strongly verified
- EU standard (eIDAS)

**For Puppy Contracts:**

- Advanced e-signature recommended
- Audit trail included
- Timestamp recorded
- IP address logged
- Tamper-evident

### Setting Up Digital Signatures

![Screenshot: E-signature configuration]

#### Platform Configuration

**Built-In System:**

1. Go to Settings > Documents
2. Enable E-Signatures
3. Configure signature fields
4. Set default options
5. Test signature flow
6. Customize email templates
7. Set up reminders

**Third-Party Integration:**

**DocuSign:**

- Industry leader
- Extensive features
- API integration
- Mobile apps
- Audit trails
- Certificate of completion

**HelloSign (Dropbox):**

- User-friendly
- Affordable
- API available
- Templates supported
- Legally binding

**Adobe Sign:**

- Part of Adobe ecosystem
- Enterprise features
- Workflow automation
- Advanced security
- Global compliance

**PandaDoc:**

- All-in-one platform
- Payments integrated
- Analytics included
- Template library
- CRM integration

**Integration Setup:**

1. Sign up for platform
2. Generate API key
3. Enter in system settings
4. Map document fields
5. Test connection
6. Configure defaults
7. Train on workflow

#### Signature Field Placement

![Screenshot: Document with signature fields]

**Standard Signature Locations:**

**Final Page:**

- Breeder signature
- Buyer signature
- Date fields (auto-fill)
- Witness signature (optional)
- Printed names

**Each Page (Optional):**

- Initials at bottom
- Confirms reviewed
- Prevents disputes
- Professional standard

**Field Types:**

- Signature
- Initial
- Date signed
- Text (printed name)
- Checkbox (agreements)
- Radio buttons (options)

**Field Properties:**

- Required vs. optional
- Assigned to specific party
- Validation rules
- Tab order
- Field size
- Default values

### Signature Workflow

![Screenshot: Signature workflow diagram]

#### Sending for Signature

**Step 1: Prepare Document**

- Generate final contract
- Review all terms
- Verify information
- Check formatting
- Add signature fields
- Set field properties

**Step 2: Configure Signing**

- Signer order (sequential/parallel)
- Expiration date (e.g., 7 days)
- Reminder schedule
- CC recipients
- Authentication method
- Language preference

**Step 3: Send**

- Click "Send for Signature"
- Enter recipient email(s)
- Add personal message
- Preview email
- Confirm and send
- Track delivery

**Email to Signer:**

```
Subject: Please Sign: Puppy Sales Contract

Hi [Buyer Name],

[Your personal message]

Please review and sign the attached puppy sales
contract for [Puppy Name].

Click below to review and sign:
[REVIEW & SIGN BUTTON]

This signature request expires on [Date].

Thank you!
[Your Name]
[Business Name]
```

#### Signing Process (Buyer's View)

**Step 1: Receive Email**

- Opens secure email
- Clicks "Review & Sign"
- Redirected to platform

**Step 2: Identity Verification (Optional)**

- Enter access code
- Answer security questions
- SMS verification
- Email confirmation

**Step 3: Review Document**

- Read contract thoroughly
- Scroll through all pages
- Review terms and conditions
- Note any questions

**Step 4: Sign**

- Click signature field
- Choose signature method:
  - Draw with mouse/finger
  - Type name (cursive font)
  - Upload image
- Review signature
- Accept if satisfied

**Step 5: Initial Pages (If Required)**

- Click each initial field
- Apply initials
- Confirm each page reviewed

**Step 6: Complete**

- Review summary
- Confirm completion
- Receive signed copy
- Email confirmation

**Step 7: Download**

- Access signed document
- Save to personal records
- Print if desired

#### Tracking Signature Status

![Screenshot: Signature tracking dashboard]

**Status Options:**

**Draft**

- Document prepared
- Not yet sent
- Can still edit
- No recipient action

**Sent**

- Email delivered
- Awaiting action
- Timer started
- Reminders scheduled

**Viewed**

- Recipient opened document
- Reviewing content
- Not yet signed
- Engagement confirmed

**Signed by Buyer**

- Buyer completed signature
- Waiting for breeder (if sequential)
- Timestamp recorded
- Partial completion

**Complete**

- All parties signed
- Legally binding
- Final copy generated
- Stored securely

**Declined**

- Recipient rejected
- Reason given (optional)
- Follow-up needed
- Can resend

**Expired**

- Deadline passed
- No action taken
- Must regenerate
- Set new deadline

**Voided**

- Cancelled by sender
- No longer valid
- Reason documented
- Can create new

**Status Dashboard Features:**

- Real-time updates
- Filter by status
- Sort by date
- Search by signer
- Bulk actions
- Quick view

### Reminders and Notifications

![Screenshot: Reminder configuration]

#### Automatic Reminders

**Reminder Schedule:**

**Before Expiration:**

- 3 days before deadline
- 1 day before deadline
- 2 hours before deadline (optional)

**After Sending:**

- 2 days after sent (if not viewed)
- 4 days after sent (if viewed, not signed)
- Daily after first reminder

**Custom Schedule:**

- Set specific days
- Multiple reminders
- Time of day
- Escalation pattern

**Reminder Email:**

```
Subject: Reminder: Signature Requested

Hi [Buyer Name],

This is a friendly reminder that your signature is
still needed on the puppy sales contract for
[Puppy Name].

[REVIEW & SIGN BUTTON]

This request expires in [X] days.

If you have questions, please contact me.

Thank you,
[Your Name]
```

**Reminder Best Practices:**

- Friendly, not demanding tone
- Clear deadline
- Easy action button
- Offer to help
- Professional follow-up

#### Notifications for Breeder

**You'll Be Notified When:**

- Document sent successfully
- Recipient viewed document
- Recipient signed document
- All parties completed
- Document declined
- Document expired
- Reminder sent
- Error occurred

**Notification Channels:**

- Email
- In-app notification
- SMS (optional)
- Push notification (mobile)
- Webhook (for integrations)

**Notification Settings:**

1. Go to Settings > Notifications
2. Select events to monitor
3. Choose notification method
4. Set frequency
5. Configure alerts
6. Test notifications

### Document Version Control

![Screenshot: Version history interface]

#### Version Management

**Why Version Control Matters:**

- Track changes over time
- Audit trail
- Revert if needed
- Compare versions
- Compliance requirements

**Version Types:**

**Draft Versions:**

- Before sending
- Multiple edits possible
- Saved automatically
- Can delete
- Not signed

**Sent Version:**

- Locked for signing
- Cannot edit
- Preserved exactly
- Legally binding
- Permanent record

**Amended Version:**

- After original signed
- References original
- New signature required
- Linked together
- Supersedes if conflict

**Version History Display:**

```
Contract Version History:

v1.0 - Created 11/15/2024 2:30 PM
v1.1 - Edited 11/15/2024 3:45 PM (price corrected)
v2.0 - Sent 11/15/2024 4:00 PM (CURRENT)
v2.0 - Signed by Buyer 11/16/2024 10:30 AM
v2.0 - Signed by Breeder 11/16/2024 2:15 PM
v3.0 - Amendment sent 12/1/2024 (payment plan)
v3.0 - Fully executed 12/1/2024
```

**Version Actions:**

- View any version
- Download specific version
- Compare versions (side-by-side)
- Restore draft version
- Export version history

#### Document Comparison

**Comparing Versions:**

1. Select two versions
2. Click "Compare"
3. System highlights differences:
   - Added text (green)
   - Removed text (red)
   - Changed text (yellow)
4. Review changes
5. Export comparison report

**Use Cases:**

- Review amendments
- Verify changes
- Dispute resolution
- Compliance audit
- Template improvements

### Security and Compliance

![Screenshot: Security settings]

#### Document Security

**Access Control:**

- Password protection (optional)
- Access code required
- Email verification
- SMS authentication
- IP address restrictions

**Encryption:**

- 256-bit SSL/TLS
- End-to-end encryption
- Encrypted storage
- Secure transmission
- Tamper-evident seal

**Audit Trail:**

- Who accessed
- When accessed
- IP addresses
- Actions taken
- Changes made
- Complete history

**Tamper Protection:**

- Digital seal
- Checksum verification
- Detect any changes
- Invalidate if altered
- Certificate of authenticity

#### Compliance Records

**What's Recorded:**

**Document Information:**

- Document name/type
- Creation date
- Send date
- Completion date
- Version number

**Signer Information:**

- Name
- Email address
- IP address
- Timestamp
- Authentication method

**Signature Information:**

- Signature image
- Date/time signed
- Device used
- Browser/OS
- Location (if enabled)

**Events:**

- Sent
- Viewed
- Signed
- Declined
- Voided
- Expired
- Reminder sent

**Audit Report:**

```
Certificate of Completion

Document: Puppy Sales Contract
Document ID: ABC123456
Created: 11/15/2024 4:00 PM EST

Parties:
1. Breeder: [Your Name] (sender@email.com)
2. Buyer: [Buyer Name] (buyer@email.com)

Timeline:
11/15/2024 4:00 PM - Sent by [Your Name]
11/15/2024 4:05 PM - Delivered to buyer@email.com
11/16/2024 10:15 AM - Viewed by [Buyer Name]
                       IP: 192.168.1.1
11/16/2024 10:30 AM - Signed by [Buyer Name]
                       Device: iPhone
11/16/2024 2:15 PM - Signed by [Your Name]
                       IP: 192.168.1.2
11/16/2024 2:15 PM - Completed

Certificate Hash: [cryptographic hash]
Verified By: [E-Signature Platform]
```

**Retention:**

- Store indefinitely
- Downloadable anytime
- Export to PDF
- Include in backup
- Meet legal requirements

### Handling Signature Issues

![Screenshot: Troubleshooting guide]

#### Common Problems

**Buyer Can't Access Document:**

**Check:**

- Email in spam/junk folder
- Correct email address
- Link not expired
- Not blocked by firewall

**Solutions:**

- Resend to different email
- Send access code separately
- Extend deadline
- Use different platform
- Offer paper option

**Signature Not Saving:**

**Possible Causes:**

- Browser compatibility
- Device limitations
- JavaScript disabled
- Connection interrupted
- Platform issue

**Solutions:**

- Try different browser (Chrome, Firefox, Safari)
- Clear cache and cookies
- Disable browser extensions
- Use mobile device
- Contact platform support

**Buyer Declined Document:**

**Follow-Up:**

- Contact immediately
- Understand concerns
- Address questions
- Revise if needed
- Resend when resolved

**Common Reasons:**

- Terms unclear
- Didn't read carefully
- Price confusion
- Wants changes
- Needs time to decide

**Expiration Issues:**

**Prevention:**

- Set realistic deadline (7+ days)
- Send reminders
- Follow up proactively
- Clear communication

**Resolution:**

- Regenerate document
- Extend deadline
- Resend quickly
- Apologize for inconvenience

**Technical Errors:**

**Platform Down:**

- Check platform status
- Wait and retry
- Use backup method
- Paper signature if urgent

**Integration Issues:**

- Check API connection
- Verify credentials
- Test with simple document
- Contact support

### Paper Backup Process

![Screenshot: Paper signature workflow]

#### When to Use Paper

**Appropriate Situations:**

- Buyer prefers paper
- No internet access
- In-person signing
- Backup for records
- Legal requirement
- Platform unavailable

**Paper Signature Process:**

**Step 1: Print Contract**

- Print 2-3 copies (minimum)
- Check all pages present
- Verify readable quality
- Bring to pickup/meeting

**Step 2: Review Together**

- Read through contract
- Explain key terms
- Answer questions
- Allow time to read
- Encourage thoroughness

**Step 3: Sign and Initial**

- Sign last page
- Initial each page (if required)
- Date all signatures
- Witness signature (optional)
- All copies signed

**Step 4: Distribute Copies**

- Buyer keeps original
- You keep original
- Extra copy for records
- Both parties have same version

**Step 5: Digitize**

- Scan all pages
- Save as PDF
- Upload to system
- Attach to records
- Shred or file physical

**Hybrid Approach:**

- E-sign when possible
- Paper at pickup
- Scan and upload
- Both methods valid

   - Draw signature
   - Type name

6. Download certificate of completion

### Tooltips and Quick Help

> ðŸ“§ **Delivery**: Emails may take a few minutes; check spam folders if not received

> ðŸ” **Security**: All documents encrypted in transit and at rest

> â° **Expiration**: Set realistic deadlines; 7-14 days recommended

> ðŸ“± **Mobile**: Buyers can sign on any device with internet

> ðŸ”” **Reminders**: Automatic reminders increase completion rates by 50%

> ðŸ“Š **Analytics**: Track completion rates and optimize workflow

> ðŸ’¼ **Legal**: E-signatures legally binding in most jurisdictions

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Buyer says they didn't receive email**

- Solution: Check spam/junk, resend, verify email address, send to alternate email

**Problem: Signature link expired**

- Solution: Regenerate and resend, extend deadline, apologize for inconvenience

**Problem: Can't draw signature on device**

- Solution: Try typing name instead, use different device, switch to paper

**Problem: Document won't open**

- Solution: Different browser, disable ad blocker, update browser, check platform status

**Problem: Signed document looks different than sent**

- Solution: Download official version, check for tampering, verify certificate, contact platform

**Problem: Multiple versions sent by accident**

- Solution: Void incorrect version, clarify which to sign, only accept correct version

### Advanced Features

**Bulk Sending:**

- Send multiple contracts
- Same template, different buyers
- Automated personalization
- Batch tracking
- Progress dashboard

**Conditional Logic:**

- Show fields based on selections
- Different paths
- Dynamic contracts
- Simplified experience
- Reduce confusion

**Sequential Signing:**

- Buyer signs first
- Then breeder reviews and signs
- Or reverse order
- Defined workflow
- Automatic routing

**Delegated Signing:**

- Assign to representative
- Guardian for minor
- Business authorized signer
- Power of attorney
- Documented authority

**Template Libraries:**

- Pre-built contracts
- Industry standard terms
- Customizable
- Quick deployment
- Consistent quality

**Analytics Dashboard:**

- Completion rates
- Average time to sign
- Decline reasons
- Optimization insights
- Bottleneck identification

## Lesson 19: Payment Tracking and Financial Management

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Track all financial transactions
- Record deposits and payments accurately
- Generate financial reports
- Reconcile accounts
- Handle payment disputes
- Manage refunds and chargebacks
- Export financial data for tax purposes
- Analyze breeding program profitability

### Payment Tracking System

#### Financial Dashboard Overview

![Screenshot: Financial dashboard]

**Dashboard Metrics:**

**Current Period (This Month):**

- Total Revenue: $[amount]
- Deposits Received: $[amount]
- Balances Collected: $[amount]
- Refunds Issued: $[amount]
- Net Revenue: $[calculated]

**Outstanding:**

- Pending Deposits: $[amount] ([count] customers)
- Balances Due: $[amount] ([count] puppies)
- Overdue Payments: $[amount] ([count] invoices)
- Total Receivables: $[calculated]

**Year to Date:**

- Total Sales: $[amount]
- Puppies Sold: [count]
- Average Sale Price: $[calculated]
- Revenue Growth: [%] vs last year
- Expenses: $[amount] (if tracked)
- Net Profit: $[calculated]

**Quick Actions:**

- Record Payment
- Issue Refund
- Send Invoice Reminder
- Generate Report
- Export Data
- Reconcile Account

### Recording Payments

![Screenshot: Payment entry form]

#### Payment Entry Process

**Accessing Payment Entry:**

**From Puppy Record:**

1. Open puppy details
2. Go to "Payments" tab
3. Click "Add Payment"
4. Enter details
5. Save

**From Customer Record:**

1. Open customer profile
2. Go to "Transactions" tab
3. Click "Record Payment"
4. Select puppy/invoice
5. Enter amount and details
6. Save

**From Dashboard:**

1. Financial dashboard
2. "Record Payment" button
3. Search for customer/puppy
4. Enter transaction details
5. Generate receipt
6. Email to customer

#### Payment Form Fields

**Required Information:**

**Amount** (Required)

- Dollar amount received
- Format: $0,000.00
- Validates against outstanding balance
- Cannot exceed balance (unless overpayment)

**Date** (Required)

- Date payment received
- Not processed date
- Can backdate
- Format: MM/DD/YYYY
- Defaults to today

**Payment Method** (Required)

- Credit/Debit Card
- PayPal
- Venmo
- Zelle
- Cash App
- Check
- Money Order
- Wire Transfer
- Cash
- Other

**Reference/Transaction ID** (Recommended)

- Check number
- Confirmation code
- Last 4 digits of card
- Transaction ID
- Receipt number
- For tracking and disputes

**Applied To** (Required)

- Deposit
- Balance
- Shipping fee
- Supplies
- Additional services
- Refund (negative)

**Payment Status** (Auto)

- Pending (checks)
- Cleared
- Failed
- Reversed
- Refunded

**Notes** (Optional)

- Any relevant information
- Partial payment reason
- Payment plan reference
- Special circumstances
- Internal notes

**Receipt Generation:**

- â˜ Generate receipt
- â˜ Email to customer
- â˜ Print copy
- â˜ Attach to record

#### Payment Types

**Deposit Payments:**

**Characteristics:**

- First payment
- Holds position
- Typically $500-1,000
- Before matching
- Refundable per policy

**Recording Process:**

1. Customer pays deposit
2. Record payment
3. Type: "Deposit"
4. Status: Waitlist confirmed
5. Generate receipt
6. Email confirmation

**Balance Payments:**

**Characteristics:**

- Before pickup
- Purchase price minus deposit
- Required before release
- Various methods accepted
- Must clear first

**Recording Process:**

1. Invoice sent
2. Payment received
3. Record payment
4. Type: "Balance"
5. Verify cleared
6. Status: Paid in full
7. Puppy ready for pickup

**Partial Payments:**

**When Used:**

- Payment plans
- Split payments
- Installments
- Budget constraints
- By agreement

**Recording Process:**

1. Record partial amount
2. Note: "Payment 1 of 3"
3. Balance updates automatically
4. Schedule next payment
5. Track completion

**Overpayments:**

**Handling:**

- Record full amount received
- Note overpayment
- Options:
  - Refund difference
  - Credit to account
  - Apply to extras
- Customer chooses

### Payment Methods Management

![Screenshot: Payment methods configuration]

#### Accepted Payment Methods

**Credit/Debit Cards:**

**Pros:**

- Instant processing
- Secure
- Convenient for buyer
- Tracking easy
- Buyer protection

**Cons:**

- Processing fees (2.5-3.5%)
- Chargeback risk
- Equipment/software needed
- Monthly fees possible

**Processing Options:**

- Square: 2.6% + $0.10
- Stripe: 2.9% + $0.30
- PayPal: 2.9% + $0.30
- Others: Varies

**Recording:**

- Transaction ID required
- Last 4 digits of card
- Authorization code
- Receipt generated
- Immediate confirmation

**Digital Payment Apps:**

**PayPal:**

- Most common
- Goods & Services (3.49% + $0.49)
- Friends & Family (free but against TOS)
- Buyer protection
- Seller protection available

**Venmo:**

- Popular with younger buyers
- Business account: 1.9% + $0.10
- Instant transfer option
- Mobile-friendly
- Not designed for business

**Zelle:**

- Bank-to-bank transfer
- No fees
- Fast (usually instant)
- No buyer protection
- No seller protection
- Use for trusted transactions

**Cash App:**

- Similar to Venmo
- Business account available
- 2.75% card processing
- Bitcoin option
- Popular alternative

**Recording Digital Payments:**

- Screenshot transaction
- Save confirmation email
- Record transaction ID
- Note payment app used
- Verify amount received

**Checks:**

**Pros:**

- No processing fees
- Paper trail
- Familiar method
- Stops fraud (stop payment)

**Cons:**

- Can bounce
- Processing delay (5-7 days)
- Bank fees if NSF
- Must deposit

**Best Practices:**

- Wait for check to clear
- Don't release puppy until cleared
- Photo of check
- Record check number
- Deposit promptly
- Track clearance

**NSF (Bounced Check):**

- Mark payment as failed
- Contact customer immediately
- Charge NSF fee ($30-50)
- Re-invoice with fee
- New payment required
- Hold puppy release

**Money Orders:**

**Pros:**

- Guaranteed funds
- No bounce risk
- Accepted everywhere
- Traceable

**Cons:**

- Inconvenient for buyer
- Can be forged (rare)
- Must verify

**Verification:**

- Check watermarks
- UV light test
- Call issuing institution
- Compare to genuine sample

**Cash:**

**Pros:**

- Immediate
- No fees
- No chargeback risk
- No processing delay

**Cons:**

- Security risk
- No automatic record
- Must deposit
- Theft risk
- Large amounts suspicious

**Best Practices:**

- Count together
- Issue receipt immediately
- Deposit same day
- Secure storage
- Meet in public if large amount
- Consider bank meeting

**Wire Transfer:**

**Pros:**

- Secure
- Fast
- Large amounts
- International capable
- Low fraud risk

**Cons:**

- Fees ($15-50)
- More complex
- Bank account info shared
- Less common

**Information Needed:**

- Bank name
- Routing number
- Account number
- Account name
- Bank address
- SWIFT code (international)

### Financial Reporting

![Screenshot: Financial reports interface]

#### Report Types

**Sales Summary Report:**

**Includes:**

- Date range
- Total revenue
- Number of transactions
- Average transaction
- Payment method breakdown
- Deposit vs balance split
- Pending payments
- Overdue payments

**Example Output:**

```
Sales Summary Report
January 1 - December 31, 2024

Total Revenue: $45,000
Transactions: 15
Average Sale: $3,000

By Payment Method:
Credit Card:    $21,000 (47%)
PayPal:         $12,000 (27%)
Check:          $9,000 (20%)
Cash:           $3,000 (6%)

Payment Status:
Deposits:       $7,500 (5 pending matches)
Paid in Full:   $37,500 (12 puppies placed)
Outstanding:    $4,500 (3 balance payments due)
```

**Customer Payment Report:**

**Shows:**

- Customer name
- Total paid
- Payment dates
- Payment methods
- Outstanding balance
- Payment history
- Status

**Use Cases:**

- Verify customer claims
- Track payment plans
- Identify late payers
- Account reconciliation
- Tax documentation

**Litter Profitability Report:**

**Calculates:**

- Revenue per litter
- Costs per litter (if tracked)
- Profit per litter
- Profit per puppy
- ROI percentage
- Time to sell out

**Example:**

```
Litter Profitability: Spring 2024 Litter

Revenue:
8 puppies Ã— $3,000 =      $24,000

Expenses:
Stud fee:                  $2,000
Vet care (pregnancy):      $800
Whelping supplies:         $300
Puppy food (8 weeks):      $400
Vet care (puppies):        $1,200
Microchips:                $240
Registration:              $320
Marketing:                 $200
Total Expenses:            $5,460

Net Profit:                $18,540
ROI:                       340%
Profit per puppy:          $2,318
```

**Outstanding Balances Report:**

**Details:**

- Who owes money
- Amount owed
- Due date
- Days overdue
- Contact information
- Last contact attempt
- Priority level

**Actions:**

- Send reminders
- Follow up calls
- Payment plans
- Collections consideration

**Tax Report:**

**Exports:**

- All income
- By payment method
- By date
- Customer information
- Transaction details
- Ready for accountant

**Formats:**

- PDF summary
- CSV detailed
- QuickBooks format
- Excel spreadsheet
- IRS Schedule C ready

### Account Reconciliation

![Screenshot: Reconciliation interface]

#### Reconciliation Process

**Why Reconcile:**

- Ensure accuracy
- Catch errors
- Prevent fraud
- Tax compliance
- Professional practice
- Financial clarity

**Monthly Reconciliation:**

**Step 1: Gather Information**

- Bank statement
- System payment records
- Credit card statements
- PayPal/app statements
- Cash receipt log

**Step 2: Compare Totals**

- System shows: $X received
- Bank shows: $Y deposited
- Should match (or have explanation)

**Step 3: Match Transactions**

- Check off each bank transaction
- Find matching system record
- Mark as reconciled
- Note any discrepancies

**Step 4: Investigate Differences**

**Common Discrepancies:**

- Pending transactions
- Processing delays
- Fees deducted
- Chargebacks
- Recording errors
- Duplicate entries
- Missing entries

**Step 5: Adjust Records**

- Correct errors
- Add missing entries
- Remove duplicates
- Note explanations
- Update balances

**Step 6: Document**

- Save reconciliation report
- Date completed
- Sign off
- File with records
- Ready for next month

**Reconciliation Report:**

```
Reconciliation Report - January 2025

System Records:
Total Payments: $12,500
Payment Count: 5

Bank Statement:
Total Deposits: $12,100
Deposit Count: 5

Difference: -$400

Explanation:
- PayPal fee: -$150
- Stripe fee: -$100
- Pending check: -$150 (will clear Feb 1)

Status: RECONCILED âœ“
Completed by: [Your name]
Date: 1/31/2025
```

### Handling Disputes

![Screenshot: Dispute management]

#### Payment Disputes

**Types of Disputes:**

**Customer Claims Non-Receipt:**

- Check all records
- Search by date, amount, name
- Review all payment methods
- Request proof from customer
- Check email confirmations
- Call payment processor

**Resolution:**

- Provide transaction records
- Show receipts
- Check bank statement
- Confirm or apologize
- Re-record if legitimate

**Duplicate Charge Claimed:**

- Check records for duplicates
- Verify with bank statement
- Contact payment processor
- Refund if confirmed
- Apologize and correct

**Amount Disputed:**

- Review contract/invoice
- Check agreed-upon price
- Provide documentation
- Explain any changes
- Show signed agreements
- Resolve fairly

**Chargeback (Credit Card):**

**What Is It:**

- Buyer disputes charge with bank
- Bank reverses payment
- You lose money + fee
- Must respond quickly
- Evidence required

**Response Process:**

1. Notification received (10-14 days to respond)
2. Gather evidence:
   - Signed contract
   - Invoice
   - Communications
   - Delivery confirmation
   - Photos of healthy puppy
   - Any other proof
3. Submit response through processor
4. Wait for decision (30-60 days)
5. If won: Money restored
6. If lost: Money gone, consider collections

**Preventing Chargebacks:**

- Clear communication
- Document everything
- Signed contracts
- Good customer service
- Respond to concerns quickly
- Set proper expectations
- Use "goods and services" payment

**Chargeback Fees:**

- $15-100 per chargeback
- Charged even if you win
- High chargeback rate = account risk
- Prevent whenever possible

### Refunds and Credits

![Screenshot: Refund processing]

#### Processing Refunds

**Valid Refund Reasons:**

- Cancellation per contract
- Litter didn't happen
- Health issue with puppy
- Buyer became unsuitable
- Mutual agreement
- Overpayment

**Refund Process:**

**Step 1: Verify Eligibility**

- Check contract terms
- Confirm reason
- Calculate amount
- Get approval if needed

**Step 2: Create Refund Record**

- Open transaction
- Click "Issue Refund"
- Enter refund amount
- Select reason
- Add notes

**Step 3: Process Refund**

- Same method as payment (when possible)
- Credit card: 5-10 days
- PayPal: 1-3 days
- Check: Mail within 7 days
- Cash: Immediate

**Step 4: Document**

- Generate refund receipt
- Email to customer
- Update all records
- Note in customer file
- Remove reservation

**Step 5: Adjust Accounting**

- Deduct from revenue
- Update reports
- Note in tax records
- Track refund rate

**Partial Refunds:**

**Common Scenarios:**

- Kept deposit, refund balance
- Cancelled late (partial forfeit)
- Puppy had minor issue (discount)
- Resold quickly (partial refund)

**Example:**

```
Refund Calculation:

Deposit Paid: $500
Balance Paid: $2,500
Total Paid: $3,000

Scenario: Buyer cancelled, per contract deposit
is non-refundable

Refund Amount: $2,500
Retained: $500 (deposit)
```

**Account Credits:**

**Instead of Refund:**

- Credit toward future puppy
- Next litter priority
- Upgrade options
- Services/supplies
- Expires after time period

**Tracking Credits:**

- Record in customer account
- Set expiration date
- Note restrictions
- Apply to future purchase
- Adjust invoice accordingly

#### Recording Breeding Expenses

**Why Track Expenses:**

**Breeding Expenses:**

- Cleaning supplies

**Health Care:**

- Grooming
- Training
- Facility maintenance
- Utilities
- Insurance

**Recording Expenses:**

1. Save all receipts
2. Enter in system or spreadsheet
3. Categorize accurately
4. Note which litter (if applicable)
5. Track payment method
6. Export for taxes

### Tooltips and Quick Help

> ðŸ’° **Auto-Calculate**: System automatically calculates balances and totals

> ðŸ”” **Payment Reminders**: Set up automatic reminders for due balances

> ðŸ“Š **Real-Time Reports**: Financial data updates instantly with each transaction

> ðŸ’³ **Multi-Method**: Accept all major payment methods in one system

> ðŸ“§ **Instant Receipts**: Automatic receipt generation and email delivery

> ðŸ”’ **Secure**: All financial data encrypted and PCI compliant

> ðŸ“± **Mobile**: Record payments on-the-go from any device

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Payment not showing in bank account**

- Solution: Check processing time (2-3 days), verify it cleared, contact payment processor

**Problem: Can't reconcile accounts**

- Solution: Check for pending transactions, verify fees deducted, look for duplicates

**Problem: Customer claims payment not received**

- Solution: Check all records, provide receipt copy, verify transaction cleared

**Problem: Wrong amount recorded**

- Solution: Edit transaction if not reconciled, or create adjustment entry with notes

**Problem: Duplicate payment showing**

- Solution: Verify actual charge, void duplicate if error, refund if double-charged

**Problem: Missing transactions**

- Solution: Search by date/amount, check all payment methods, manually add if confirmed

### Advanced Features

**Automated Payment Reminders:**

- Schedule reminder series
- Custom email templates
- SMS reminders
- Escalation workflow
- Stop when paid

**Payment Plans:**

- Set up installments
- Auto-generate invoices
- Track payment schedule
- Alert on missed payments
- Auto-apply when received

**QuickBooks Integration:**

- Sync transactions
- Automatic categorization
- Match customers
- Export expenses
- Tax-ready reports

**Multi-Currency Support:**

- Accept international payments
- Auto-convert to USD
- Track exchange rates
- Show in buyer's currency
- Settlement in your currency

**Subscription Payments:**

- Recurring billing
- Auto-charge saved cards
- Subscription management
- Failed payment handling
- Cancellation process

**Financial Forecasting:**

- Project future revenue
- Based on pipeline
- Seasonal adjustments
- Growth predictions
- Budget planning

### Sales Analytics Dashboard

![Screenshot: Analytics overview dashboard]

#### Key Performance Indicators (KPIs)

**Revenue Metrics:**

**Total Revenue:**

- All sales income
- By period (month, quarter, year)
- Trend over time
- Growth rate
- Comparison to previous periods

**Average Sale Price:**

- Total revenue Ã· puppies sold
- Varies by quality/traits
- Market positioning indicator
- Pricing effectiveness
- Competitive analysis

**Revenue Per Litter:**

- Total from each litter
- Compare litter performance
- Identify best producers
- Breeding decisions
- Profitability analysis

```

Q2: $15,000 (5 puppies)
Q3: $9,000 (3 puppies)
Q4: $9,000 (3 puppies)

Growth: +15% vs 2023
```

**Sales Volume Metrics:**

**Puppies Sold:**

- Total count
- By time period
- By litter
- By sex
- By color/markings

**Sell-Through Rate:**

- % of puppies sold
- How quickly sold
- Remaining inventory
- Demand indicator

**Time to Sale:**

- Days from birth to placement
- Average per litter
- By puppy characteristics
- Faster = better demand

**Example:**

```

Spring 2024 Litter:
- 8 puppies total

- Sell-through: 2 weeks after available

Fall 2024 Litter:
- 6 puppies total
- Sold: 4 (67%)
- Still available: 2
- Average age at placement: 85 days
- Waitlist demand: 4 families
- Sell-through: Ongoing
```

**Customer Metrics:**

- First-time buyers
- Repeat customers
- Referrals
- Return rate
- Loyalty indicator

- Total spent per customer
- Repeat purchases
- Referral value
- Long-term relationship
- VIP identification

**Acquisition Cost:**

- Marketing spend Ã· new customers
- By marketing channel
- ROI calculation
- Efficiency metric

#### Inquiry-to-Sale Funnel

**Funnel Stages:**

1. **Inquiry (Top of Funnel):**

   - Initial contact
   - 130 total inquiries

2. **Application Submitted:**

   - Serious interest
   - 50 applications (38%)

3. **Approved/Qualified:**

   - Suitable homes
   - 40 approved (80% of applications)

4. **Waitlist Joined:**

   - Deposit paid
   - 25 joined (62% of approved)

5. **Puppy Matched:**

   - Assigned puppy
   - 20 matched (80% of waitlist)

6. **Sale Completed:**
   - Pickup occurred
   - 18 completed (90% of matched)

**Funnel Analysis:**

```
Conversion Funnel - 2024:

130 Inquiries
    â†“ 38%
50 Applications
    â†“ 80%
40 Approved
    â†“ 62%
25 Waitlist
    â†“ 80%
20 Matched
    â†“ 90%
18 Completed Sales

Overall Conversion: 13.8% (inquiry to sale)
```

**Drop-Off Analysis:**

**Where People Drop:**

- 80 didn't apply (not serious/browsing)
- 10 not approved (unsuitable)
- 15 approved but didn't join waitlist (price, timing)
- 5 waitlist but no match (too long, changed mind)
- 2 matched but didn't complete (rare)

**Improvement Opportunities:**

- Increase application rate: Better website, faster response
- Reduce waitlist drop-off: Shorter wait times, better communication
- Higher match completion: Address concerns quickly

### Sales Forecasting

![Screenshot: Sales forecast dashboard]

#### Predictive Analytics

**Based on Historical Data:**

- Current inquiries

- Planned future litters
- Historical demand
- Market growth

Range: Conservative to optimistic
```

- Waitlist length

**Breeding Schedule Optimization:**

```
Demand Analysis:

Current waitlist: 15 families
Inquiry rate: 10/month
Typical conversion: 30%
Expected additions: 3/month

6-month projection: 15 + (3 Ã— 6) = 33 families

Planned litters:
- Spring litter: 8 puppies (covers 8 families)
- Fall litter: 8 puppies (covers 8 families)
- Total capacity: 16 puppies

Gap: 33 demand - 16 supply = 17 unmet

Options:
1. Plan additional litter
2. Increase prices (reduce demand to match supply)
3. Extend waitlist timeline
4. Refer to trusted breeders
```

- Revenue, count, percentage

**Achievable:**

- Based on capacity and market

**Relevant:**

- Aligns with business objectives

**Time-Bound:**

- Deadlines and milestones

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Data seems inaccurate**

- Solution: Verify all sales recorded, check date ranges, ensure no duplicates

**Problem: Can't identify trends**

- Solution: Need more historical data (6-12 months minimum), adjust date range

**Problem: Forecasts seem off**

- Solution: Update with current pipeline, adjust conversion rates, consider market changes

**Problem: Goals not tracking**

- Solution: Ensure goals are set correctly, check date alignment, verify data source

**Problem: Metrics don't match expectations**

- Solution: Review methodology, compare to industry standards, adjust targets if needed

**Problem: Too much data, overwhelmed**

- Solution: Focus on key metrics first, use summary dashboards, schedule regular reviews

# Module 6: Automation and Communication

## Lesson 21: Calendar and Scheduling

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Use the integrated calendar system
- Schedule important breeding events
- Track due dates and milestones
- Set up pickup appointments
- Manage veterinary appointments
- View calendar by different views
- Sync with external calendars
- Coordinate multiple schedules

### Calendar Overview

#### Accessing the Calendar

![Screenshot: Calendar main view]

**Navigation:**

1. Click **"Calendar"** in main menu
2. View opens to current month
3. Today highlighted
4. Events displayed on dates
5. Quick filters available
6. Multiple view options

**Calendar Features:**

- All breeding-related events
- Color-coded by type
- Click event for details
- Add new events quickly
- Drag to reschedule
- Search events
- Export to other calendars

#### Calendar Views

**Month View:**

- See entire month
- Events as dots or mini-labels
- Best for overview
- Plan long-term
- Spot conflicts
- Default view

**Week View:**

- 7-day spread
- Hour-by-hour detail
- More event information
- Current week focus
- Day-to-day planning

**Day View:**

- Single day
- Complete schedule
- Hourly breakdown
- Full event details
- Detailed planning

**Agenda View:**

- List format
- Upcoming events
- Sorted chronologically
- See details without clicking
- Filter by type
- Print-friendly

**View Switching:**

- Buttons at top right
- Month | Week | Day | Agenda
- Remember preference
- Quick toggle

#### Color-Coded Categories

**Breeding Events (Red):**

- Heat cycle expected
- Breeding dates
- Progesterone testing
- Tie confirmed
- AI scheduled

**Pregnancy Events (Purple):**

- Ultrasound appointment
- X-ray appointment
- Due date

**Puppy Events (Blue):**

- Birth date
- Vet check (puppies)
- Vaccination dates

- Microchipping
- Pickup dates

**Customer Events (Green):**

- Meet & greet scheduled
- Home visit

- Adult dog vet appointments

- Grooming appointments

- Annual check-ups

- Registration deadlines
- Document submission

**Personal Reminders (Yellow):**

- Supply ordering
- Facility maintenance

- Other notes

### Adding Events

![Screenshot: Add event form]

#### Creating New Events

**Quick Add:**

1. Click on date in calendar
2. Quick form appears
3. Enter event title
4. Select type
5. Save

**Detailed Add:**

1. Click **"+ Add Event"** button
2. Complete form:
   - Event title
   - Event type/category
   - Date and time
   - Duration
   - Location (optional)
   - Description/notes
   - Related record (dog, litter, customer)
   - Reminders
   - Repeat settings
3. Save event

**Event Form Fields:**

**Title** (Required)

- Brief description
- Examples:
  - "Bella's Heat Cycle Expected"
  - "Litter Vet Check"
  - "Puppy Pickup - Smith Family"
  - "Ultrasound - Dr. Johnson"

**Type/Category** (Required)

- Select from color-coded list
- Determines color on calendar
- Helps with filtering
- Organizational tool

**Date** (Required)

- Single date or
- Date range (multi-day)
- Start and end times
- All-day event option

**Time** (Optional)

- Specific time: 2:00 PM
- Or time range: 2:00 PM - 3:00 PM
- All-day if no time needed

**Location** (Optional)

- Your kennel
- Veterinary clinic address
- Customer's home
- Show venue
- Other location

**Description/Notes** (Optional)

- Additional details
- Preparation needed
- Supplies to bring
- Contact information
- Special instructions

**Link to Record** (Recommended)

- Select dog
- Select litter
- Select customer
- Select waitlist entry
- Shows related information
- Appears in both places

**Reminders** (Optional)

- None
- At time of event
- 15 minutes before
- 30 minutes before
- 1 hour before
- 1 day before
- 1 week before
- Custom timing
- Multiple reminders possible

**Repeat** (Optional)

- Does not repeat (default)
- Daily
- Weekly
- Monthly
- Yearly
- Custom pattern
- End date or count

#### Auto-Generated Events

**System Creates Automatically:**

**From Heat Cycles:**

- Next heat expected (calculated)
- Progesterone testing window
- Optimal breeding window

**From Breeding:**

- Ultrasound date (28 days)
- X-ray date (55 days)
- Due date (63 days)
- Whelping watch (60 days)

**From Litter Birth:**

- Dewclaw removal (3 days)
- First vet check (1 week)
- Second vet check (3 weeks)
- First shots (6 weeks)
- Second shots (9 weeks)
- Ready to go home (8 weeks)

**From Reservations:**

- Pickup date
- Payment due date
- Contract deadline

**From Waitlist:**

- Deposit expiration
- Follow-up dates
- Priority review dates

**You Can:**

- Edit auto-generated events
- Change dates if needed
- Add details
- Delete if not needed
- Reschedule easily

Title: Puppy Socialization Time

Day: Saturday
Time: 10:00 AM - 12:00 PM
Ends: After 8 weeks
```

```
Title: Adult Dog Vet Check
Repeats: Monthly
Day: First Monday
Time: 9:00 AM
Ends: After 12 occurrences
```

```
Title: Deworming Puppies
Repeats: Every 2 weeks
Starting: Birth date
Ending: 8 weeks old
```

### Important Breeding Dates

![Screenshot: Breeding timeline on calendar]

#### Heat Cycle Tracking

**Expected Heat:**

- Auto-calculated from last heat
- Typically 6 months apart
- Displayed as "Expected"
- Update when confirmed
- Set reminder 1 week before

**Heat Confirmed:**

- Mark actual start date
- Updates next expected
- Progesterone testing window shown
- Breeding window calculated

**Optimal Breeding Window:**

- Days 10-14 typical
- Progesterone-based more accurate
- Displayed on calendar
- Updated with test results

#### Pregnancy Timeline

**Key Dates Display:**

**Day 0: Breeding**

- Tie or AI date
- Starting point

**Day 28-32: Ultrasound**

- Confirm pregnancy
- Count puppies (estimate)
- Schedule appointment

**Day 45: X-Ray**

- More accurate count
- Skeletal development visible
- Final preparation

**Day 58: Nesting Box**

- Introduce whelping area
- Dam gets comfortable
- Watch for signs

**Day 60-63: Whelping Watch**

- Temperature drop signals labor
- Stay close
- Whelping kit ready

**Day 63: Due Date**

- Average gestation
- Range: 58-68 days
- Be prepared early

**Calendar Display:**

```
March 2025

1  Bella Bred (Day 0)
15
29 Ultrasound (Day 28) ðŸ”µ

April 2025

1
15 X-Ray (Day 45) ðŸ”µ
29 Nest Box Setup (Day 58) ðŸ”µ

May 2025

1  Whelping Watch (Day 60) ðŸ”´
3  DUE DATE (Day 63) ðŸ”´ðŸ”´ðŸ”´
```

#### Puppy Development Schedule

**Auto-Populated After Birth:**

**Week 1:**

- Day 3: Dewclaw removal (if doing)
- Day 7: First weigh-in
- Daily: Weigh puppies

**Week 2:**

- Eyes opening
- Weight check
- Socialization begins

**Week 3:**

- Start hearing
- More active
- First worming

**Week 4:**

- Starting solids
- Vet check
- Second worming

**Week 6:**

- First vaccinations
- Puppy evaluations
- Individual photos
- Third worming

**Week 8:**

- Go-home age
- Pickup appointments
- Final vet check
- Second vaccinations

**Week 9:**

- Extended pickups
- Follow-up starts

### Pickup Scheduling

![Screenshot: Pickup appointment scheduler]

#### Scheduling Puppy Pickups

**Appointment Slots:**

- Create time slots
- Prevent overcrowding
- Space out appointments
- 1-2 hour gaps recommended
- Same day or spread over days

**Creating Pickup Schedule:**

**Option 1: Manual Scheduling**

1. Customer contacts to schedule
2. Offer available dates/times
3. Add to calendar
4. Link to customer and puppy
5. Send confirmation

**Option 2: Self-Scheduling**

1. Share calendar link
2. Customers book own slot
3. Auto-adds to calendar
4. Confirmation sent automatically
5. Reduces back-and-forth

**Pickup Event Details:**

**Include in Event:**

- Customer name
- Puppy name/ID
- Pickup date and time
- Duration (30-60 min typical)
- What to bring:
  - Crate/carrier
  - Collar and leash
  - Payment (if balance due)
  - ID
- Your address/directions
- Parking information
- Contact number

**Confirmation Email:**

```
Subject: Puppy Pickup Appointment - [Puppy Name]

Hi [Customer Name],

Your puppy pickup is confirmed!

Date: [Date]
Time: [Time]
Duration: Approximately 1 hour
Location: [Your Address]

Please Bring:
âœ“ Crate or secure carrier
âœ“ Collar and leash
âœ“ Payment if balance due ($[amount])
âœ“ Photo ID

We'll provide:
âœ“ Puppy's records (vet, vaccination)
âœ“ Registration papers
âœ“ Care instructions
âœ“ Food sample
âœ“ Toy with littermate scent

Looking forward to seeing you!
[Your Name]
[Phone]
```

**Day-Of Reminders:**

- Automatic reminder sent
- Morning of pickup
- Includes all details
- Your contact number

### Calendar Sharing & Export

![Screenshot: Calendar export options]

#### Syncing with External Calendars

**Export to:**

- Google Calendar
- Apple Calendar
- Outlook
- Yahoo Calendar
- iCal format
- Other calendar apps

**Setup Process:**

**Method 1: iCal Subscription**

1. Go to Calendar Settings
2. Click "Export/Share"
3. Copy iCal URL
4. Add to your personal calendar app
5. Choose update frequency
6. Calendar syncs automatically

**Method 2: One-Time Export**

1. Select date range
2. Choose events to export
3. Download .ics file
4. Import to your calendar
5. Manual process
6. Good for one-time events

**Privacy Settings:**

- Share all events
- Share only specific types
- Hide sensitive details
- Show only busy/free
- Password protect
- Expiration date

**Benefits of Syncing:**

- One master calendar
- Check on phone
- Personal + breeding combined
- Automated updates
- No double-booking
- Reminders on all devices

#### Sharing with Others

**Use Cases:**

- Co-owner access
- Partner/family member
- Assistant/helper
- Vet clinic integration
- Customer pickup portal

**Sharing Options:**

**View-Only Access:**

- Recipients can see events
- Cannot edit
- Good for customers (pickup dates)
- Good for family awareness

**Edit Access:**

- Recipients can add/edit
- Full calendar control
- For co-breeders
- For business partners

**Filtered Sharing:**

- Share only puppy pickups
- Share only breeding schedule
- Share only vet appointments
- Selective access

### Calendar Notifications

![Screenshot: Calendar notification settings]

#### Setting Up Reminders

**Notification Types:**

**Email Reminders:**

- Sent to your email
- Advance notice
- Event details included
- Click to view/edit

**In-App Notifications:**

- Bell icon badge
- Notification panel
- Real-time alerts
- Dismiss or act

**SMS Text Reminders:**

- Text to your phone
- For urgent events
- Brief details
- Optional (carrier rates apply)

**Push Notifications (Mobile):**

- Phone notification
- Even when app closed
- Time-sensitive
- Configure in app settings

**Reminder Timing:**

**Default Reminder Schedule:**

- 1 week before: Major events (whelping, shows)
- 1 day before: Appointments, pickups
- 1 hour before: Vet appointments, meetings
- At time of: Tasks, to-dos

**Custom Reminders:**

- Multiple reminders per event
- Different timing each
- Different methods each
- Example:
  - 1 week before: Email
  - 1 day before: Email + SMS
  - 1 hour before: Push notification

**Reminder Settings:**

1. Go to Calendar Settings
2. Notification Preferences
3. Select default reminder times
4. Choose notification methods
5. Configure quiet hours
6. Save preferences

### Practice Exercises

**Exercise 1: Add Breeding Event**

1. Go to Calendar
2. Click on date 2 weeks from now
3. Add event:
   - Title: "Bella Heat Cycle Expected"
   - Type: Breeding
   - All-day event
   - Link to Bella's record
   - Reminder: 1 week before
4. Save
5. Verify appears on calendar in red

**Exercise 2: Schedule Vet Appointment**

1. Click "+ Add Event"
2. Create appointment:
   - Title: "Litter Vet Check - Dr. Smith"
   - Type: Veterinary
   - Date: [Select date]
   - Time: 10:00 AM - 11:00 AM
   - Location: "Vet clinic address"
   - Link to current litter
   - Reminder: 1 day before
3. Save
4. Email yourself the details

**Exercise 3: Create Pickup Schedule**

1. Select pickup date (week puppies turn 8 weeks)
2. Create time slots:
   - 9:00 AM - 10:00 AM: Smith family
   - 11:00 AM - 12:00 PM: Johnson family
   - 2:00 PM - 3:00 PM: Williams family
3. Add details to each
4. Send confirmation emails

**Exercise 4: Set Up Recurring Event**

1. Add new event: "Weigh Puppies"
2. Set to repeat: Daily
3. Time: 8:00 AM
4. Duration: 4 weeks (birth to go-home)
5. Reminder: At time of event
6. Save series

**Exercise 5: Filter Calendar View**

1. Go to Calendar
2. Uncheck all event types
3. Check only "Puppy Events"
4. View filtered calendar
5. Now check only "Customer Events"
6. See how view changes
7. Re-enable all types

**Exercise 6: Export to Personal Calendar**

1. Go to Calendar Settings
2. Click "Export/Share"
3. Copy iCal URL
4. Open your Google/Apple Calendar
5. Add new calendar from URL
6. Paste URL
7. Verify events appear
8. Test sync with new event

### Tooltips and Quick Help

> ðŸ“… **Drag & Drop**: Easily reschedule by dragging events to new dates

> ðŸ”” **Smart Reminders**: System suggests optimal reminder times based on event type

> ðŸ”„ **Auto-Sync**: Calendar updates in real-time across all devices

> ðŸŽ¨ **Color Coding**: Instantly identify event types by color

> ðŸ“± **Mobile Access**: Full calendar functionality on your phone

> ðŸ”— **Deep Linking**: Click event to see related dog, litter, or customer details

> ðŸ“¤ **Easy Export**: Share calendar with family or sync with personal calendars

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Events not showing on calendar**

- Solution: Check filter settings, verify date range, ensure event saved properly

**Problem: Reminders not received**

- Solution: Check email spam folder, verify notification settings, confirm email address

**Problem: Can't reschedule event**

- Solution: Click event first, then edit, or try drag-and-drop in month/week view

**Problem: Recurring events creating too many instances**

- Solution: Edit series, adjust end date or occurrence count, delete extras

**Problem: Calendar sync not working with external app**

- Solution: Regenerate iCal URL, re-add to external app, check internet connection

**Problem: Double-booked appointments**

- Solution: Enable conflict warnings in settings, review before saving

### Advanced Features

**Calendar Analytics:**

- Busiest days/times
- Event type distribution
- Completion rates
- Scheduling patterns
- Optimization suggestions

**Smart Scheduling:**

- AI suggests best times
- Avoids conflicts
- Considers travel time
- Groups related events
- Optimizes your day

**Automated Workflows:**

- Event triggers actions
- Create task lists
- Send follow-up emails
- Update records
- Generate documents

**Calendar Templates:**

- Save common schedules
- Apply to new litters
- Standardize timelines
- One-click scheduling
- Consistent processes

**Multi-Calendar View:**

- Personal + Business
- Multiple breeders
- Separate facilities
- Toggle visibility
- Overlay or side-by-side

**Time Zone Support:**

- Automatic conversion
- International customers
- Travel adjustments
- Display preferences
- DST handling

## Lesson 22: Automated Reminders

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Configure automated reminder systems
- Set up breeding cycle reminders
- Create customer communication reminders
- Manage health care reminders
- Customize reminder templates
- Track reminder effectiveness
- Reduce manual follow-up work
- Never miss important tasks

### Reminder System Overview

#### Why Automated Reminders Matter

**Benefits:**

- Never forget critical tasks
- Professional customer communication
- Timely health care
- Consistent processes
- Reduce stress
- Improve outcomes
- Save time
- Build reputation

**What Can Be Automated:**

- Breeding cycle tracking
- Pregnancy milestones
- Vaccination schedules
- Customer follow-ups
- Payment reminders
- Contract deadlines
- Puppy milestone checks
- Administrative tasks

![Screenshot: Reminder dashboard]

### Types of Reminders

#### Breeding & Health Reminders

**Heat Cycle Reminders:**

**Expected Heat Alert:**

- Trigger: Based on last heat cycle
- Timing: 1 week before expected date
- Purpose: Prepare for breeding season
- Action: Watch for signs, schedule progesterone tests

**Example:**

```
ðŸ”” Reminder: Heat Cycle Expected

Bella's next heat cycle is expected around March 15, 2025.

Actions:
â€¢ Watch for behavioral changes
â€¢ Schedule progesterone testing
â€¢ Review breeding plans
â€¢ Contact stud dog owner
â€¢ Prepare supplies

[View Bella's Record] [Snooze Reminder]
```

**Progesterone Testing Reminder:**

- Trigger: Heat cycle confirmed
- Timing: Day 5-7 of heat
- Purpose: Determine optimal breeding time
- Action: Schedule vet appointment

**Breeding Window Alert:**

- Trigger: Progesterone results entered
- Timing: Optimal window identified
- Purpose: Don't miss breeding opportunity
- Action: Coordinate breeding/AI

**Pregnancy Milestone Reminders:**

**Ultrasound Reminder:**

- Trigger: Breeding date + 28 days
- Timing: Day 25 (3 days advance notice)
- Purpose: Schedule ultrasound
- Action: Call vet, confirm pregnancy

**X-Ray Reminder:**

- Trigger: Breeding date + 45 days
- Timing: Day 42 (3 days advance notice)
- Purpose: Schedule x-ray
- Action: Get accurate puppy count

**Whelping Preparation:**

- Trigger: Due date - 7 days
- Timing: Day 56
- Purpose: Prepare for birth
- Action: Whelping kit ready, clear schedule

**Temperature Monitoring:**

- Trigger: Due date - 3 days
- Timing: Day 60
- Purpose: Watch for labor
- Action: Take temperature 2x daily

**Due Date Alert:**

- Trigger: Day 63
- Timing: Day 63 + daily until birth
- Purpose: Labor expected
- Action: Stay close, monitor closely

**Puppy Health Reminders:**

**Vaccination Schedule:**

- Auto-generated from birth date
- Week 6: First shots reminder
- Week 9: Second shots reminder
- Week 12: Third shots reminder (if applicable)
- Links to vet appointment scheduling

**Example Series:**

```
Week 4: First Deworming Due
Week 6: Second Deworming + First Shots
Week 8: Third Deworming
Week 9: Second Shots + Vet Check
Week 10: Microchip if not done
```

**Deworming Reminders:**

- Every 2 weeks from week 2-8
- Automated schedule
- Track completion
- Never miss a dose

**Weight Check Reminders:**

- Daily for first 2 weeks
- Weekly after that
- Track growth rates
- Alert if concerns

#### Customer Communication Reminders

![Screenshot: Customer reminder settings]

**Waitlist Follow-Up:**

**Initial Contact Response:**

- Trigger: New inquiry submitted
- Timing: Within 24 hours
- Purpose: Professional first impression
- Action: Send welcome email, application

**Application Follow-Up:**

- Trigger: Application received
- Timing: 3 days if not reviewed
- Purpose: Don't leave waiting
- Action: Review and respond

**Deposit Expiration Warning:**

- Trigger: Deposit date + time period
- Timing: 30 days before expiration
- Purpose: Retain customer
- Action: Offer renewal or refund

**Waitlist Position Update:**

- Trigger: Position changes
- Timing: Immediate
- Purpose: Keep informed
- Action: Automated email with update

**Litter Announcement:**

- Trigger: Litter born
- Timing: Within 24 hours
- Purpose: Exciting news!
- Action: Email with photos, count, next steps

**Match Notification:**

- Trigger: Puppy assigned to buyer
- Timing: Immediate
- Purpose: Assignment communication
- Action: Email with puppy info, next steps

**Payment Reminders:**

**Balance Due Reminder:**

- Trigger: Invoice created
- Timing: 7 days before due date
- Purpose: Gentle reminder
- Action: Send invoice link

**Example:**

```
ðŸ“§ Payment Reminder

Hi [Customer Name],

Your final balance of $2,500 for [Puppy Name]
is due in 7 days (January 20, 2025).

Payment Methods:
â€¢ Credit card: [Link]
â€¢ PayPal: [Link]
â€¢ Zelle: [Details]
â€¢ Check: [Address]

Questions? Reply to this email.

Thank you!
[Your Name]
```

**Overdue Notice:**

- Trigger: Payment due date passed
- Timing: 1 day, 3 days, 7 days overdue
- Purpose: Collect payment
- Action: Increasingly urgent emails
- Tone: Professional but firm

**Pickup Preparation:**

**One Week Before:**

- Trigger: Pickup date - 7 days
- Purpose: Final preparations
- Content:
  - Confirm date/time
  - What to bring
  - Payment reminder
  - Directions
  - Contact info

**One Day Before:**

- Trigger: Pickup date - 1 day
- Purpose: Immediate reminder
- Content:
  - Tomorrow's appointment
  - Time and location
  - Weather considerations
  - Your phone number

**Post-Pickup Follow-Up:**

**24-Hour Check-In:**

- Trigger: Pickup date + 1 day
- Purpose: First night support
- Content:
  - How's it going?
  - Common questions answered
  - Reassurance
  - Your availability

**One Week Check-In:**

- Trigger: Pickup date + 7 days
- Purpose: Settling in
- Content:
  - How's puppy adjusting?
  - Any concerns?
  - Vet visit reminder
  - Training tips

**One Month Check-In:**

- Trigger: Pickup date + 30 days
- Purpose: Long-term support
- Content:
  - Progress update request
  - Photo request
  - Next vaccination reminder
  - Ongoing availability

**Three Month Check-In:**

- Trigger: Pickup date + 90 days
- Purpose: Milestone check
- Content:
  - Growth update
  - Training progress
  - Health check
  - Spay/neuter reminder (if applicable)

**One Year Anniversary:**

- Trigger: Pickup date + 365 days
- Purpose: Maintain relationship
- Content:
  - Happy birthday wishes
  - Photo request
  - Health update
  - Referral request

### Setting Up Reminders

![Screenshot: Reminder configuration interface]

#### Configuring Automated Reminders

**Accessing Reminder Settings:**

1. Go to Settings
2. Click "Reminders & Notifications"
3. See all reminder types
4. Enable/disable each
5. Customize timing
6. Edit templates

**Enable/Disable Reminders:**

- Toggle switch for each type
- Green = Active
- Gray = Disabled
- Bulk enable/disable by category
- Save preferences

**Timing Configuration:**

**For Each Reminder Type:**

- Set trigger condition
- Set timing offset
- Choose frequency
- Set duration/retry
- Configure escalation

**Example Configuration:**

```
Balance Due Reminder:
âœ“ Enabled

Send When:
Invoice due date - 7 days

Frequency:
Send once

Follow-Up:
If not paid by due date, send:
â€¢ 1 day overdue
â€¢ 3 days overdue
â€¢ 7 days overdue

Stop When:
Payment received
```

#### Customizing Reminder Templates

![Screenshot: Template editor]

**Email Template Editor:**

**Components:**

- Subject line
- Email body
- Merge fields
- Call-to-action buttons
- Signature
- Footer

**Merge Fields Available:**

- {customer_name}
- {puppy_name}
- {due_date}
- {amount_due}
- {breeder_name}
- {phone_number}
- {pickup_date}
- {litter_name}
- Many more...

**Template Example:**

```
Subject: {puppy_name} Pickup Tomorrow!

Hi {customer_name},

This is a friendly reminder that your puppy
pickup is scheduled for tomorrow!

Appointment Details:
Date: {pickup_date}
Time: {pickup_time}
Location: {breeder_address}

Please Bring:
âœ“ Secure carrier or crate
âœ“ Collar and leash
âœ“ Payment if balance due: ${balance_amount}
âœ“ Photo ID

We're excited to send {puppy_name} home with you!

Call or text with questions: {breeder_phone}

See you tomorrow!
{breeder_name}
```

**Editing Templates:**

1. Select reminder type
2. Click "Edit Template"
3. Modify subject and body
4. Add/remove merge fields
5. Preview with sample data
6. Send test email
7. Save changes

**Multiple Templates:**

- Create variations
- A/B test effectiveness
- Different tones
- Specific situations
- Rotate automatically

### Managing Active Reminders

![Screenshot: Active reminders list]

#### Reminder Queue

**Viewing Pending Reminders:**

- Next 7 days highlighted

- Filterable by type
- Action buttons available

**Reminder Status:**

- **Scheduled**: Will send on date
- **Sent**: Already delivered
- **Completed**: Action taken
- **Snoozed**: Delayed by user
- **Cancelled**: No longer needed
- **Failed**: Delivery issue

**Manual Actions:**

**Send Now:**

- Override timing
- Send immediately
- Useful for urgent matters

**Snooze:**

- Delay reminder
- Choose new date
- Temporarily dismiss
- Still tracked

**Cancel:**

- Won't send
- Reason noted
- Remove from queue

**Edit:**

- Modify content
- Change recipient
- Adjust timing
- One-time change

**Bulk Actions:**

- Select multiple reminders
- Send all
- Snooze all
- Cancel all
- Change timing
