### Reminder Best Practices

![Screenshot: Best practices checklist]

#### Effective Reminder Strategies

**Timing:**

- Not too early (forgotten)
- Not too late (missed)
- Consider urgency
- Respect time zones
- Avoid weekends for business

**Frequency:**

- Not too many (annoying)
- Not too few (ineffective)
- Escalate appropriately
- Stop when action taken
- Respect preferences

**Tone:**

- Professional but friendly
- Helpful, not nagging
- Clear call-to-action
- Positive language
- Respectful always

**Content:**

- Clear subject line
- Brief and scannable
- Essential information only
- Easy next step
- Contact info included

**Personalization:**

- Use customer name
- Reference specific puppy
- Relevant details only
- Show you care
- Build relationship

**Mobile-Friendly:**

- Short paragraphs
- Large buttons
- Readable on phone
- Quick to scan
- Easy to act

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Reminders not sending**

- Solution: Check enabled status, verify email settings, check internet connection

**Problem: Customer not receiving reminders**

- Solution: Verify email address, check spam folder, confirm opted in

**Problem: Too many reminders going out**

- Solution: Review enabled reminders, adjust frequency, disable unnecessary

**Problem: Wrong information in reminder**

- Solution: Check merge fields, update customer/puppy data, edit template

**Problem: Reminders sending at wrong time**

- Solution: Check time zone settings, verify trigger configuration, adjust offset

**Problem: Can't customize template**

- Solution: Check permissions, try different browser, contact support

## Lesson 23: Email Configuration and Integration

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Configure email integration
- Set up custom email templates
- Send professional emails from the system
- Track email engagement
- Manage email lists and campaigns
- Automate email workflows
- Maintain email deliverability
- Comply with email regulations

### Email System Overview

#### Why Integrated Email Matters

**Benefits:**

- Professional communication
- All correspondence in one place
- Automated follow-ups
- Track customer interactions
- Reduce manual work
- Consistent messaging
- Better organization
- Improved response times

**Email Capabilities:**

- Send from your domain
- Custom templates
- Bulk emails
- Drip campaigns
- Automated responses
- Engagement tracking
- Contact management
- Mobile-friendly

![Screenshot: Email dashboard]

### Email Integration Setup

#### Connecting Your Email

**Option 1: System Email (Basic)**

**Using Built-In Email:**

- Emails sent from system domain
- Example: notifications@breederapp.com
- On behalf of your name
- Quick setup
- Free
- Lower customization
- May land in spam more often

**Setup:**

1. Go to Settings > Email
2. Select "Use System Email"
3. Enter your reply-to address
4. Set display name
5. Save

**Option 2: Custom Domain (Professional)**

**Using Your Email:**

- Emails from your domain
- Example: you@yourkennel.com
- Professional appearance
- Better deliverability
- Full control
- Requires configuration

**Supported Providers:**

- Gmail/Google Workspace
- Outlook/Office 365
- Yahoo Mail
- Any SMTP server
- SendGrid
- Mailgun
- Amazon SES

**Gmail Setup Example:**

1. Go to Settings > Email Integration
2. Select "Gmail"
3. Click "Connect Gmail Account"
4. Authorize access
5. Select sending email
6. Test connection
7. Save

**SMTP Setup (Generic):**

1. Go to Settings > Email Integration
2. Select "Custom SMTP"
3. Enter details:
   - SMTP Server: smtp.yourhost.com
   - Port: 587 (TLS) or 465 (SSL)
   - Username: your@email.com
   - Password: [your password]
   - Encryption: TLS/SSL
4. Test connection
5. Send test email
6. Verify received
7. Save

**App Password (Gmail/Outlook):**

- Don't use regular password
- Create app-specific password
- More secure
- Required for 2FA accounts

**Gmail App Password:**

1. Google Account Settings
2. Security
3. 2-Step Verification
4. App passwords
5. Select app: Mail
6. Select device: Other (Custom)
7. Name: "Breeder App"
8. Generate
9. Copy password
10. Use in SMTP setup

![Screenshot: Email integration settings]

#### Email Authentication (Advanced)

**SPF, DKIM, DMARC:**

- Verify sender identity
- Prevent spoofing
- Improve deliverability
- Reduce spam classification
- Professional standard

**What They Do:**

**SPF (Sender Policy Framework):**

- Lists authorized sending servers
- DNS record
- Prevents forged sender addresses

**DKIM (DomainKeys Identified Mail):**

- Digital signature
- Verifies message integrity
- Prevents tampering

**DMARC (Domain-based Message Authentication):**

- Policy for failed authentication
- Reporting mechanism
- Tells receivers what to do

**Setup Assistance:**

- System provides DNS records
- Add to your domain DNS
- Ask hosting provider for help
- May take 24-48 hours to propagate
- Test with email tools

> ðŸ’¡ **Pro Tip**: Proper authentication dramatically improves email deliverability

### Email Templates

![Screenshot: Template library]

#### Pre-Built Templates

**Available Templates:**

**Customer Communication:**

#### Customizing Templates

![Screenshot: Template editor]

**Template Editor:**

**Components:**

- Subject line
- Preheader text
- Email body
- Header image (optional)
- Footer with contact info
- Unsubscribe link (required)

**Editing Process:**

1. Select template
2. Click "Customize"
3. Modify subject line
4. Edit body text
5. Add/remove sections
6. Insert merge fields
7. Add images
8. Style formatting
9. Preview
10. Save

**Merge Fields:**

- {customer_first_name}
- {customer_last_name}
- {customer_email}
- {puppy_name}
- {puppy_breed}
- {litter_name}
- {due_date}
- {pickup_date}
- {amount_due}
- {breeder_name}
- {breeder_phone}
- {breeder_website}
- {kennel_name}

**Example Template:**

```
Subject: Welcome to {kennel_name}, {customer_first_name}!

Hi {customer_first_name},

Thank you for your interest in a {puppy_breed} puppy
from {kennel_name}!

We're excited to help you find your perfect companion.
Here's what happens next:

1. Review Your Application
   We'll carefully review your application within
   24-48 hours.

2. Approval & Waitlist
   If approved, we'll send information about joining
   our waitlist.

3. Stay Connected
   Follow us on Instagram: @{instagram_handle}
   Visit our website: {breeder_website}

Questions? Simply reply to this email or call me at
{breeder_phone}.

Looking forward to working with you!

{breeder_name}
{kennel_name}
{breeder_phone}
{breeder_email}
```

**Design Best Practices:**

**Subject Lines:**

- Under 50 characters
- Clear and specific
- Avoid spam words
- Personalize when possible
- Create urgency (when appropriate)

**Email Body:**

- Conversational tone
- Short paragraphs (2-3 lines)
- Use bullet points
- Clear call-to-action
- Mobile-friendly
- Professional formatting

**Images:**

- High quality but compressed
- Alt text included
- Relevant to content
- Not too many (slow loading)
- Logo in header

**Formatting:**

- Consistent fonts
- Readable size (14-16px body)
- Good contrast
- White space
- Scannable layout

#### A/B Testing

**Test Variables:**

- Subject lines
- Send times
- Content variations
- Call-to-action
- Images vs. text

**Setup:**

1. Create campaign
2. Enable A/B test
3. Create version B
4. Set split % (50/50 typical)
5. Choose winner metric
6. Auto-send winner to remaining

**Example Test:**

```
A/B Test: Payment Reminder Subject Line

Version A: "Payment Reminder: Balance Due Soon"
Sent to: 50% of list
Open rate: 42%

Version B: "Action Needed: Complete Your Puppy Purchase"
Sent to: 50% of list
Open rate: 58%

Winner: Version B (â†‘16% open rate)
Remaining: Sent to future campaigns
```

### Email Automation Workflows

![Screenshot: Workflow builder]

#### Automated Email Sequences

**Drip Campaigns:**

- Series of timed emails
- Triggered by action
- Nurture leads
- Onboard customers
- Build relationships

**Example Workflow: New Inquiry**

```
Trigger: Inquiry form submitted

Email 1: Immediate
Subject: Thanks for Your Interest!
Content: Welcome, next steps, application link

Email 2: +2 days (if no application)
Subject: Have Questions About the Application?
Content: FAQs, offer to help, call-to-action

Email 3: +5 days (if still no application)
Subject: We'd Love to Meet You!
Content: Testimonials, photos, final invitation

Stop When: Application submitted
```

**Example Workflow: Post-Pickup**

```
Trigger: Puppy pickup completed

Email 1: +1 day
Subject: How's {puppy_name} Settling In?
Content: First night tips, reassurance

Email 2: +7 days
Subject: One Week Milestone! ðŸŽ‰
Content: What to expect, training tips

Email 3: +30 days
Subject: {puppy_name}'s First Month Update
Content: Request photos, vet reminder

Email 4: +90 days
Subject: {puppy_name} is Growing Up!
Content: Check-in, spay/neuter reminder

Email 5: +365 days
Subject: Happy 1st Birthday, {puppy_name}!
Content: Celebration, photo request, referral ask
```

**Building Workflows:**

1. Go to Email > Automation
2. Click "New Workflow"
3. Name workflow
4. Set trigger
5. Add email steps
6. Set delays between
7. Add conditions (if/then)
8. Test workflow
9. Activate

**Workflow Triggers:**

- Form submitted
- Status changed
- Date reached
- Action taken
- Payment received
- Contract signed
- Birthday/anniversary
- Custom event

### Email Compliance

![Screenshot: Compliance settings]

#### Legal Requirements

**CAN-SPAM Act (US):**

**Requirements:**

- Accurate header info
- Non-deceptive subject
- Identify as advertisement (if applicable)
- Physical address in footer
- Unsubscribe option
- Honor opt-outs within 10 days
- Monitor third-party senders

**GDPR (EU):**

- Explicit consent required
- Clear privacy policy
- Right to access data
- Right to be forgotten
- Data portability
- Breach notification

**CASL (Canada):**

- Express consent
- Implied consent (2 years)
- Clear identification
- Unsubscribe mechanism
- Consent records

**Best Practices:**

- Get explicit opt-in
- Double opt-in recommended
- Clear unsubscribe
- Honor immediately
- Keep consent records
- Segment lists
- Don't buy lists

#### Unsubscribe Management

**Unsubscribe Options:**

**One-Click Unsubscribe:**

- Click link in email
- Immediately removed
- Confirmation shown
- No login required
- Required by law

**Preference Center:**

- Choose email types
- Frequency preferences
- Update info
- Don't lose contact entirely

**Example Preference Center:**

```
Email Preferences for sarah@email.com

What would you like to receive?
â˜‘ Litter announcements
â˜‘ Available puppy alerts
â˜‘ Educational content
â˜ Newsletter
â˜ Promotional offers

How often?
â—‹ As it happens
â— Weekly digest
â—‹ Monthly digest

[Save Preferences] [Unsubscribe from All]
```

**Suppression List:**

- Unsubscribed emails stored
- Never email again
- Automatic checking
- Prevents accidental sends
- Export for compliance

### Email Deliverability

![Screenshot: Deliverability dashboard]

#### Maintaining Inbox Placement

**Factors Affecting Deliverability:**

**Sender Reputation:**

- Historical sending behavior
- Spam complaints
- Bounce rates
- Engagement rates
- Consistent sending

**Email Authentication:**

- SPF configured
- DKIM signing
- DMARC policy
- Reverse DNS
- IP reputation

**Content Quality:**

- Not spammy
- Good text-to-image ratio
- No misleading subject
- Professional formatting
- Personalized

**Engagement:**

- High open rates
- Click-throughs
- Low unsubscribes
- Few spam reports
- Replies

**List Quality:**

- Permission-based
- Regularly cleaned
- Remove bounces
- Re-engagement campaigns
- Quality over quantity

**Best Practices:**

**Do:**

- Warm up new IPs
- Consistent sending schedule
- Segment lists
- Personalize content
- Mobile-optimize
- Test before sending
- Monitor metrics
- Clean list regularly

**Don't:**

- Buy email lists
- Use all caps
- Overuse exclamation marks!!!
- Misleading subjects
- Large attachments
- Too many images
- Send to inactive contacts
- Ignore metrics

**Improving Deliverability:**

1. Review bounce reports
2. Remove invalid emails
3. Re-engage inactive subscribers
4. Improve content relevance
5. Increase engagement
6. Monitor spam reports
7. Test different ISPs
8. Adjust sending frequency

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Emails going to spam**

- Solution: Check authentication (SPF/DKIM), avoid spam trigger words, improve engagement

**Problem: Low open rates**

- Solution: Improve subject lines, test send times, clean list, segment better

**Problem: Connection failed**

- Solution: Verify credentials, use app password, check SMTP settings, test connection

**Problem: Emails not sending**

- Solution: Check sending limits, verify email activated, check internet, review error logs

**Problem: High bounce rate**

- Solution: Clean list, remove invalid emails, verify addresses, use double opt-in

**Problem: Unsubscribe link not working**

- Solution: Check link in template, verify system settings, test with own email

### Advanced Features

**Email Scoring:**

- Lead scoring based on engagement
- Hot leads identified
- Follow-up prioritization
- Conversion prediction
- Sales intelligence

**Dynamic Content:**

- Show different content by recipient
- Personalized product recommendations
- Location-based content
- Behavioral triggers
- Individual experiences

**Multi-Variate Testing:**

- Test multiple elements
- Complex combinations
- Statistical significance
- Continuous optimization
- Data-driven decisions

**API Integration:**

- Connect to CRM
- Sync with other tools
- Custom workflows
- Advanced automation
- Developer access

**White-Label Email:**

- Fully branded
- Custom domain
- No system branding
- Professional appearance
- Premium feature

**Advanced Segmentation:**

- Behavioral targeting
- Predictive segments
- RFM analysis
- Customer journey stage
- Lifetime value

## Lesson 24: Notification Management

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Configure notification preferences
- Manage in-app notifications
- Set up push notifications
- Customize notification sounds
- Control notification frequency
- Prioritize important alerts
- Reduce notification fatigue
- Stay informed without overwhelm

### Notification System Overview

#### Types of Notifications

![Screenshot: Notification center]

**In-App Notifications:**

- Bell icon with badge count
- Notification panel
- Real-time alerts
- Action buttons
- Dismiss or act
- History available

**Email Notifications:**

- Sent to your inbox
- Detailed information
- Links to system
- Archivable
- Searchable

**Push Notifications:**

- Mobile device alerts
- Desktop notifications
- Even when app closed
- Quick actions
- Time-sensitive

**SMS Notifications:**

- Text messages
- Critical alerts only
- Carrier charges apply
- Opt-in required
- Immediate delivery

**Webhook Notifications:**

- For integrations
- Developer feature
- Real-time data
- Custom actions
- Advanced use

### Notification Categories

![Screenshot: Notification settings by category]

#### What You Can Be Notified About

**Customer Activity:**

- New inquiry submitted
- Application received
- Waitlist deposit paid
- Customer message received
- Review/testimonial posted
- Reference check response
- Document uploaded

**Sales & Payments:**

- Payment received
- Invoice overdue
- Refund requested
- Contract signed
- Balance paid in full
- Payment plan missed
- Chargeback filed

**Breeding & Health:**

- Heat cycle expected
- Breeding window optimal
- Pregnancy milestone
- Whelping due soon
- Birth reported
- Vaccination due
- Health alert

**Puppy Updates:**

- Puppy born
- Weight milestone
- Ready for pickup
- Pickup scheduled
- Puppy goes home
- Follow-up due
- Birthday anniversary

**Calendar & Reminders:**

- Event starting soon
- Appointment tomorrow
- Task overdue
- Reminder triggered
- Schedule conflict
- Booking received

**System & Administrative:**

- New message
- Form submission
- Report generated
- Export complete
- Backup completed
- System update
- Error occurred

### Configuring Notifications

![Screenshot: Notification preferences]

#### Setting Your Preferences

**Accessing Settings:**

1. Click profile icon
2. Select "Notifications"
3. Or: Settings > Notifications
4. See all categories
5. Configure each

**For Each Notification Type:**

**Enable/Disable:**

- Toggle on/off
- Green = Active
- Gray = Disabled
- Bulk enable/disable

**Delivery Method:**

- â˜‘ In-app
- â˜‘ Email
- â˜ Push
- â˜ SMS

**Frequency:**

- Instant (as it happens)
- Digest (batch together)
- Daily summary
- Weekly summary
- Never

**Priority Level:**

- ðŸ”´ Critical (always notify)
- ðŸŸ¡ Important (normal)
- âšª Informational (can wait)

**Example Configuration:**

```
Customer Activity Notifications:

New Inquiry:
âœ“ In-app: Instant
âœ“ Email: Instant
âœ“ Push: Enabled
â˜ SMS: Disabled
Priority: Important

Application Received:
âœ“ In-app: Instant
âœ“ Email: Instant
â˜ Push: Disabled
â˜ SMS: Disabled
Priority: Important

Customer Message:
âœ“ In-app: Instant
âœ“ Email: Instant
âœ“ Push: Enabled
âœ“ SMS: Critical only
Priority: Critical
```

#### Quiet Hours

**Set Do Not Disturb:**

- Specify quiet hours
- No notifications during
- Exception: Critical only
- Different for weekdays/weekends

**Configuration:**

```
Quiet Hours:

Weekdays:
From: 10:00 PM
To: 7:00 AM

Weekends:
From: 11:00 PM
To: 8:00 AM

Allow Critical: âœ“
(Emergency alerts only)
```

**Critical Alerts:**

- Bypass quiet hours
- Emergency only
- Examples:
  - Whelping started
  - Payment chargeback
  - Security issue
  - System down

**Push Notification Features:**

### Notification Digest

![Screenshot: Digest settings]

#### Batched Notifications

**Why Use Digests:**

- Reduce interruptions
- Batch non-urgent items
- Review at once
- Stay informed
- Prevent fatigue
- Work efficiently

**Digest Options:**

**Hourly Digest:**

- Every hour
- For busy periods
- Quick review
- Manageable chunks

**Daily Digest:**

- Once per day
- Choose time (morning typical)
- Comprehensive summary
- Start day informed

**Weekly Digest:**

- Once per week
- Choose day (Monday typical)
- High-level overview
- Low-priority items

**Digest Content:**

```
Daily Notification Digest - December 2, 2024

Good Morning!

Here's your summary from the past 24 hours:

ðŸ“§ Customer Activity (5)
â€¢ 3 new inquiries
â€¢ 1 application received
â€¢ 1 waitlist deposit

ðŸ’° Payments (2)
â€¢ 2 balances paid ($5,500 total)
â€¢ 0 overdue payments

ðŸ• Breeding & Puppies (3)
â€¢ Bella's heat cycle started
â€¢ Litter A: Day 28 (ultrasound due)
â€¢ 2 puppies gained milestone weights

ðŸ“… Upcoming Today (4)
â€¢ Vet appointment: 10:00 AM
â€¢ Pickup: Johnson family, 2:00 PM
â€¢ Payment due: Williams family
â€¢ Follow-up call: Smith family

[View All Details] [Manage Notifications]
```

**Configuring Digests:**

1. Go to Notification Settings
2. Select notification type
3. Choose "Digest" frequency
4. Set delivery time
5. Preview digest
6. Save

### Priority Notifications

![Screenshot: Priority configuration]

#### Critical vs. Informational

**Priority Levels:**

**Critical (ðŸ”´):**

- Requires immediate attention
- Always notify all methods
- Bypass quiet hours
- Examples:
  - Whelping started
  - Emergency health alert
  - Payment chargeback
  - System security issue

**Important (ðŸŸ¡):**

- Should know soon
- Normal notification rules
- Can wait a bit
- Examples:
  - Payment received
  - Contract signed
  - New inquiry
  - Appointment tomorrow

**Informational (âšª):**

- Nice to know
- Can batch together
- Digest appropriate
- Examples:
  - Weight recorded
  - Task completed
  - Export finished
  - Newsletter sent

**Setting Priorities:**

1. Review notification types
2. Assign priority level
3. Critical: Only true emergencies
4. Important: Time-sensitive
5. Informational: Can wait
6. Save configuration

**Priority-Based Routing:**

```
Critical Notifications:
â†’ All methods immediately
â†’ Ignore quiet hours
â†’ Sound/vibration/banner
â†’ Persistent until acknowledged

Important Notifications:
â†’ User preferred methods
â†’ Respect quiet hours
â†’ Standard alerts
â†’ Auto-dismiss after read

Informational Notifications:
â†’ Digest or in-app only
â†’ No interruption
â†’ Review when convenient
â†’ Auto-clear after 7 days
```

### Notification History

![Screenshot: Notification history]

#### Reviewing Past Notifications

**Accessing History:**

1. Open notification panel
2. Click "View All"
3. Complete history shown
4. Search and filter
5. Paginated list

**History Features:**

**Filter Options:**

- By type/category
- By priority
- By date range
- Read/unread
- Archived

**Search:**

- Keyword search
- Customer name
- Puppy name
- Content search
- Quick find

**Actions:**

- View details
- Mark as read/unread
- Delete
- Archive
- Re-notify

**Retention:**

- Keep 90 days default
- Archive longer if needed
- Export to PDF/CSV
- Compliance records
- Audit trail

### Notification Best Practices

![Screenshot: Best practices guide]

#### Preventing Notification Fatigue

**Signs of Too Many Notifications:**

- Ignoring most alerts
- Disabling categories
- Missing important ones
- Feeling overwhelmed
- Reduced responsiveness

**Optimization Strategy:**

**1. Audit Current Settings:**

- Review what you receive
- Note what you ignore
- Identify truly important
- Disable unnecessary

**2. Use Digests:**

- Batch non-urgent
- Reduce interruptions
- Scheduled review
- Still informed

**3. Prioritize Properly:**

- Critical: Very few
- Important: Time-sensitive
- Informational: Most things

**4. Choose Right Methods:**

- Push: Urgent only
- Email: Can wait a bit
- In-app: Check regularly
- SMS: Emergencies

**5. Set Quiet Hours:**

- Work-life balance
- Uninterrupted sleep
- Focused work time
- Critical still gets through

**6. Regular Review:**

- Monthly settings check
- Adjust as needed
- Remove obsolete
- Optimize delivery

**Recommended Configuration:**

```
Suggested Settings for Balanced Notifications:

Critical (Push + SMS + Email):
â€¢ Whelping started
â€¢ Emergency health issues
â€¢ Security alerts

Important (Push + Email):
â€¢ New inquiry (business hours only)
â€¢ Payment received
â€¢ Contract signed
â€¢ Appointment tomorrow

Informational (Daily Digest):
â€¢ Weight recorded
â€¢ Task completed
â€¢ Reports generated
â€¢ Non-urgent updates

Disabled:
â€¢ System maintenance notices
â€¢ Minor updates
â€¢ Low-priority tasks
```

### Team Notifications

**Role-Based Notifications:**

- Owner: All critical
- Manager: Customer-related
- Assistant: Scheduling
- Vet Tech: Health alerts
- Custom roles

- Auto-assign by type
- Round-robin distribution

- Backup coverage

**Notification Routing:**

```
New Inquiry:
â†’ Primary: Sales Manager
â†’ Backup: Owner (if no response in 2 hours)
â†’ Method: Email + Push

Payment Issue:
â†’ Primary: Owner
â†’ Backup: Accountant
â†’ Method: All methods

Puppy Health Alert:
â†’ Primary: Vet Tech
â†’ CC: Owner
â†’ Method: SMS + Push
```

**Team Dashboard:**

- See team's notifications
- Who's handling what
- Response times
- Workload distribution
- Reassign if needed

### Practice Exercises

**Exercise 1: Configure Notification Preferences**

1. Go to Settings > Notifications
2. Review all categories
3. For "Customer Activity":
   - Enable in-app and email
   - Set to instant
   - Priority: Important
4. For "System Updates":
   - Enable in-app only
   - Set to weekly digest
   - Priority: Informational
5. Save preferences

**Exercise 2: Set Quiet Hours**

1. Go to Notification Settings
2. Find "Quiet Hours" section
3. Set weekday hours: 10 PM - 7 AM
4. Set weekend hours: 11 PM - 8 AM
5. Enable "Allow Critical Alerts"
6. Test by checking time
7. Save

**Exercise 3: Enable Push Notifications**

1. Open app on mobile device
2. Go to Settings > Notifications
3. Enable push notifications
4. Grant system permission
5. Select notification types for push
6. Test with test notification
7. Adjust as needed

**Exercise 4: Create Daily Digest**

1. Go to Notification Settings
2. Select "Informational" notifications
3. Change from "Instant" to "Daily Digest"
4. Set delivery time: 8:00 AM
5. Preview digest format
6. Save configuration

**Exercise 5: Review Notification History**

1. Click bell icon
2. Click "View All"
3. Filter by: Last 7 days
4. Search for: "Payment"
5. Review payment notifications
6. Mark any unread as read
7. Archive old notifications

**Exercise 6: Optimize Settings**

1. Review current notifications
2. Identify most frequent type
3. Ask: Is this interruption worth it?
4. Adjust method or timing
5. Move to digest if appropriate
6. Test for one week
7. Re-evaluate effectiveness

### Tooltips and Quick Help

> ðŸ”” **Smart Notifications**: AI learns your preferences and suggests optimizations

> ðŸ“± **Cross-Platform**: Sync notification states across all devices

> ðŸŽ¯ **Priority Aware**: Critical alerts always get through, even during quiet hours

> ðŸ“Š **Analytics**: Track notification engagement and response times

> ðŸ”‡ **Do Not Disturb**: Set quiet hours while allowing emergencies

> âš¡ **Instant Delivery**: Notifications arrive in under 5 seconds

> ðŸŽ¨ **Customizable**: Full control over what, when, and how you're notified

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Not receiving notifications**

- Solution: Check settings enabled, verify email/phone, check spam folder, test notification

**Problem: Too many notifications**

- Solution: Disable non-essential, use digests, adjust priorities, set quiet hours

**Problem: Push notifications not working on mobile**

- Solution: Check app permissions, reinstall if needed, verify notification settings in app

**Problem: Notifications delayed**

- Solution: Check internet connection, verify delivery method, contact support if persistent

**Problem: Can't dismiss notifications**

- Solution: Try different browser, clear cache, refresh page, check for updates

**Problem: Missing important notifications**

- Solution: Check filter settings, review archived, adjust priority levels, enable multiple methods

**Smart Notification Grouping:**

- Related items bundled
- Expandable threads
- Reduce clutter

- Intelligent sorting

**Notification Analytics:**

- Response time tracking

- Team performance
- Efficiency insights

**Conditional Notifications:**

- If/then rules
- Complex logic
- Business hours only
- Based on status
- Custom triggers

**Voice Notifications:**

- Text-to-speech
- Alexa/Google Assistant
- Hands-free alerts
- Smart home integration
- Accessibility feature

# Module 7: Public Features and Online Presence

## Lesson 25: Public Breeder Website

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Set up your public breeder website

### Public Website Overview

#### Why Have a Public Website

**Benefits:**

- Professional credibility
- 24/7 information access
- Showcase your program
- Attract quality buyers
- Reduce repetitive questions
- Build your brand
- Share your story
- Generate leads automatically

**What's Included:**

- Customizable design
- About your program
- Dog profiles
- Available/upcoming litters
- Contact form
- Photo galleries
- Testimonials
- Blog/updates (optional)
- Mobile-responsive
- SEO-optimized

![Screenshot: Public website example]

### Website Setup

#### Activating Your Public Website

**Initial Setup:**

1. Go to Settings > Public Website
2. Toggle "Enable Public Website"
3. Choose subdomain or custom domain
4. Select theme/template
5. Basic information auto-populated
6. Preview website
7. Publish when ready

**Default URL:**

- Format: `yourkennel.breederapp.com`
- Or custom: `www.yourkennelname.com`
- Instant activation
- Free SSL certificate
- Reliable hosting included

**Website Status:**

- **Draft**: Not public, editing
- **Preview**: Accessible via special link
- **Published**: Live to the world
- **Offline**: Temporarily disabled

**Display Logic:**

- Show based on status
- Hide sold-out (optional)
- Feature current availability
- Archive old litters
- Automatic updates

### SEO and Discoverability

![Screenshot: SEO settings]

#### Search Engine Optimization

**Why SEO Matters:**

- Found in Google searches
- Attract organic traffic
- Free marketing
- Quality leads
- Long-term benefit
- Competitive advantage

**SEO Settings:**

**Site Title:**

- Your kennel name
- Include breed
- Location (optional)
- Example: "Golden Dreams Kennel | Golden Retrievers | California"

**Meta Description:**

- Brief summary (150-160 characters)
- What you offer
- Key differentiators
- Appears in search results

**Example:**

```
Premium Golden Retriever puppies from health-tested,
champion bloodline parents. Family-raised with love.
Located in Northern California.
```

**Keywords:**

- Relevant search terms
- Breed name
- Location
- "puppies"
- "breeder"
- Specialties

**Example Keywords:**

- Golden Retriever puppies
- Golden Retriever breeder
- California Golden Retriever
- AKC Golden Retriever
- Champion bloodline Golden
- Family-raised puppies

**Page-Specific SEO:**

- Unique title per page
- Unique description per page
- Descriptive URLs
- Image alt text
- Header tags (H1, H2)

**URL Structure:**

```
Good:
yourkennel.com/available-puppies
yourkennel.com/about-us
yourkennel.com/our-dogs

Bad:
yourkennel.com/page1
yourkennel.com/p?id=123
```

**Image Optimization:**

- Descriptive file names
- Alt text for accessibility
- Compressed file size
- Relevant to content

**Example:**

```
File name: golden-retriever-puppy-spring-2025.jpg
Alt text: "Adorable Golden Retriever puppy from Spring 2025 litter playing in grass"
```

#### Google Business Integration

**Connecting Your Business:**

1. Create Google Business Profile
2. Verify ownership
3. Link to website
4. Add to Settings > Integrations
5. Photos sync automatically
6. Reviews display on site

**Benefits:**

- Appear in Google Maps
- Google search visibility
- Customer reviews
- Business information
- Direction requests
- Phone calls tracked

### Custom Domain Setup

![Screenshot: Custom domain configuration]

#### Using Your Own Domain Name

**Why Custom Domain:**

- Professional branding
- Easier to remember
- Better SEO
- Full ownership
- Credibility

**Domain Options:**

- Buy through system ($15/year)
- Connect existing domain
- Keep using subdomain (free)

**Buying Domain Through System:**

1. Go to Settings > Domain
2. Click "Purchase Domain"
3. Search availability
4. Select domain (.com recommended)
5. Complete purchase
6. Auto-configured
7. Live in minutes

**Connecting Existing Domain:**

**Steps:**

1. Go to Settings > Domain
2. Click "Connect Custom Domain"
3. Enter your domain name
4. Receive DNS instructions
5. Log into domain registrar
6. Add DNS records provided
7. Verify connection
8. Wait for propagation (24-48 hours)

**DNS Records Needed:**

```
Type: CNAME
Name: www
Value: yourkennel.breederapp.com

Type: A
Name: @
Value: [IP address provided]
```

**Domain Registrars:**

- GoDaddy
- Namecheap
- Google Domains
- Hover
- Other registrars

**SSL Certificate:**

- Automatic and free
- HTTPS enabled
- Secure connection
- Trust indicator
- Required for modern web

### Practice Exercises

**Exercise 1: Activate Public Website**

1. Go to Settings > Public Website
2. Enable public website
3. Choose subdomain name
4. Select theme: "Modern"
5. Review auto-populated content
6. Click "Preview"
7. Check all pages
8. Publish when satisfied

**Exercise 2: Customize Branding**

1. Go to Website > Design
2. Upload kennel logo
3. Set colors:
   - Primary: Choose brand color
   - Secondary: Complementary color
4. Select fonts
5. Upload banner image
6. Preview changes
7. Save and publish

**Exercise 3: Edit About Page**

1. Go to Website > Pages
2. Select "About Us"
3. Click "Edit"
4. Write your story:
   - Why you breed
   - Your experience
   - Your philosophy
   - What makes you different
5. Add your photo
6. Add kennel photos
7. Save and preview

**Exercise 4: Add Dog Profiles**

1. Go to Website > Our Dogs
2. Select which dogs to display
3. Choose layout: Grid
4. Set featured dog
5. Enable pedigree display
6. Add health testing info
7. Preview page
8. Publish

**Exercise 5: Configure SEO**

1. Go to Website > SEO
2. Edit site title
3. Write meta description (150 chars)
4. Add 10 relevant keywords
5. Set page-specific SEO for:
   - Home page
   - Available puppies page
6. Optimize image alt text
7. Save all changes

**Exercise 6: Review Analytics**

1. Go to Website > Analytics
2. View last 30 days
3. Identify top pages
4. Check traffic sources
5. Review mobile vs. desktop
6. Note conversion rate
7. Plan improvements based on data

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Website not showing updates**

- Solution: Clear browser cache, hard refresh (Ctrl+F5), wait for CDN update

**Problem: Images not loading**

- Solution: Check file size (< 5MB), verify file format (JPG/PNG), re-upload

**Problem: Custom domain not working**

- Solution: Verify DNS records correct, wait 24-48 hours for propagation, check with registrar

**Problem: Mobile view looks wrong**

- Solution: Try different theme, check image sizes, use mobile preview tool

**Problem: Contact form not receiving submissions**

- Solution: Check email address correct, check spam folder, verify form settings

**Problem: Website loading slowly**

- Solution: Compress images, reduce plugins, check hosting status, optimize content

## Lesson 26: Public Litter Pages

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Create and publish litter pages
- Share litter pages with prospects
- Display puppy photos and videos
- Update litter availability in real-time
- Enable puppy reservations through litter pages
- Track litter page engagement
- Customize litter page layouts
- Embed litter pages in social media

### Litter Page Overview

#### What Are Public Litter Pages

**Purpose:**

- Showcase specific litters
- Share with waitlist families
- Attract new applications
- Display puppy photos/videos
- Show availability status
- Enable online reservations
- Reduce repetitive questions
- Professional presentation

**Features:**

- Beautiful photo galleries
- Individual puppy profiles
- Dam and sire information
- Availability status (real-time)
- Application/waitlist links
- Progress updates
- Shareable links
- Mobile-optimized

![Screenshot: Litter page example]

### Creating Litter Pages

#### Setting Up a Public Litter Page

**Automatic Creation:**

- Litter created in system
- Public page auto-generated
- Unique URL assigned
- Initially private (draft)
- Publish when ready

**Page URL Format:**

```
yourkennel.breederapp.com/litters/spring-2025

Or with custom domain:
www.yourkennelname.com/litters/spring-2025
```

**Activation Process:**

1. Go to litter record
2. Click "Public Litter Page"
3. Review page preview
4. Customize settings
5. Add photos/content
6. Toggle "Public" on
7. Share URL

![Screenshot: Litter page settings]

#### Litter Page Content

**Information Displayed:**

**Header Section:**

- Litter name
- Status badge (Expected, Available, Sold Out)
- Primary photo
- Quick stats
- Call-to-action button

**Dam and Sire:**

- Photos
- Names and titles
- Age
- Color/markings
- Health testing
- Pedigree (optional)
- Temperament description
- View full profile links

**Litter Details:**

- Expected/actual birth date
- Number of puppies
- Gender breakdown
- Available count
- Ready to go home date
- Price
- What's included
- Application process

**Puppy Profiles:**

- Individual puppy cards
- Photos (multiple per puppy)
- Collar color identification
- Gender
- Weight/size
- Personality notes
- Availability status
- "Reserve" button

**Photo Gallery:**

- Litter photos
- Growth progression
- Videos
- Slideshow option
- Full-screen view
- Download option (optional)

**Progress Updates:**

- Timeline of milestones
- Weekly updates
- Recent photos
- Development notes
- Excitement builder

### Customizing Litter Pages

![Screenshot: Litter page customization options]

#### Layout Options

**Page Layouts:**

**Classic:**

- Traditional structure
- Information-focused
- Easy to scan
- Professional

**Gallery:**

- Photo-centric
- Visual storytelling
- Emotional connection
- Engaging

**Timeline:**

- Chronological updates
- Growth progression
- Story unfolds
- Anticipation builder

**Grid:**

- Puppy-focused
- Quick comparison
- Clean organization
- Modern

**Selecting Layout:**

1. Go to litter settings
2. Public Page tab
3. Choose layout style
4. Preview
5. Select and save

#### Privacy and Visibility Settings

**Visibility Options:**

**Private (Draft):**

- Not accessible publicly
- Only you can view
- For preparation
- Default for new litters

**Unlisted:**

- Accessible via link
- Not on website menu
- Not in search results
- For selective sharing
- Good for waitlist only

**Public:**

- Listed on website
- Appears in navigation
- Search engine indexed
- Open to everyone
- Maximum visibility

**Password Protected:**

- Requires password to view
- Share password with approved families
- Extra privacy layer
- Exclusive access

**Setting Visibility:**

1. Litter page settings
2. Visibility section
3. Select level
4. Set password if needed
5. Save

#### Display Preferences

**What to Show/Hide:**

- â˜ Pricing information
- â˜ Available count
- â˜ Individual puppy status
- â˜ Application link
- â˜ Breeder contact info
- â˜ Dam/sire pedigrees
- â˜ Health testing details
- â˜ Photo download option
- â˜ Video content
- â˜ Progress updates
- â˜ Share buttons

**Customizing Content:**

```
Litter Page Display Settings:

Show Pricing: âœ“ Yes

### Managing Puppy Availability

![Screenshot: Availability management]

#### Real-Time Status Updates

**Status Options:**

- âœ… **Available**: Ready to reserve
- â³ **Pending**: Hold/in process
- âŒ **Reserved**: Committed
- ðŸ  **Placed**: Gone to home
- ðŸ”’ **Not Available**: Keeping/other

**Automatic Updates:**

- Status changes in system
- Litter page updates immediately
- Available count adjusts
- Visual indicators update
- No manual website editing

**Batch Updates:**

- Update multiple puppies
- Change all to available
- Mark litter as sold out
- Quick status management

**Status History:**

- Track status changes
- Who made changes
- When changed
- Previous status
- Audit trail

### Online Reservations

![Screenshot: Reserve puppy button]

#### Enabling Direct Reservations

**Reservation Feature:**

- "Reserve Now" button
- Customer clicks
- Guided process
- Deposit collection
- Automatic updates

**Reservation Flow:**

```
1. Customer clicks "Reserve Now"
   â†“
2. Log in or create account
   â†“
3. Review puppy details
   â†“
4. Sign contract (if required first)
   â†“
5. Pay deposit
   â†“
6. Confirmation email
   â†“
7. Puppy marked as Reserved
   â†“
8. Litter page updates automatically
```

**Requirements:**

- Application approved first, OR
- Open reservation (risky)
- Contract acceptance
- Deposit payment
- Terms agreement

**Configuration:**

1. Litter settings
2. Reservation Options
3. Enable "Allow Online Reservations"
4. Set requirements:
   - â˜‘ Must be approved
   - â˜‘ Sign contract first
   - â˜‘ Deposit required
5. Set deposit amount
6. Configure payment methods
7. Save

**Benefits:**

- Faster reservations
- Reduce back-and-forth
- Immediate commitment
- Payment collected
- Professional process

### Litter Page Best Practices

![Screenshot: Best practices checklist]

#### Creating Effective Litter Pages

**Photo Quality:**

- High resolution
- Good lighting
- Multiple angles
- Individual AND group shots
- Show environment
- Clean background
- Puppy personality
- Update weekly

**Content Tips:**

- Clear, concise
- Highlight key info
- Answer common questions
- Compelling descriptions
- Professional tone
- Personal touch
- Call-to-action
- Mobile-friendly

**Update Frequency:**

- Weekly minimum
- New photos often
- Milestone updates
- Availability changes
- Keep excitement high
- Show growth
- Build anticipation

**Timing:**

**When to Publish:**

- **Planning Stage**: Optional teaser
- **Pregnancy Confirmed**: Yes, build waitlist
- **Puppies Born**: Definitely!
- **Ready Age**: Maximum visibility

**When to Archive:**

- All puppies placed
- 3+ months after placement
- Move to "Past Litters"
- Keep for reference

**Promotion Strategy:**

- Announce on social media
- Email to waitlist immediately
- Share in breed groups
- Update website banner
- Pin to social profiles
- Regular reminder posts
- Countdown to ready date

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Litter page not showing updates**

- Solution: Click "Publish Changes", clear cache, verify internet connection

**Problem: Photos not uploading**

- Solution: Check file size (< 10MB), use JPG/PNG format, compress if needed

**Problem: Reserve button not working**

- Solution: Verify puppy marked available, check reservation settings enabled

**Problem: Page not accessible via link**

- Solution: Check visibility setting (must be Unlisted or Public), verify URL correct

**Problem: Social share preview not showing image**

- Solution: Set custom preview image in settings, verify image uploaded correctly

**Problem: Low page views**

- Solution: Promote more frequently, improve SEO, share across more channels

## Lesson 27: Contact Forms and Lead Capture

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Create and customize contact forms
- Build inquiry and application forms
- Configure form fields and validation
- Set up form notifications
- Manage form submissions
- Prevent spam submissions
- Integrate forms with CRM
- Track form conversion rates

### Contact Form System

#### Why Contact Forms Matter

**Benefits:**

- Capture leads 24/7
- Collect structured information
- Reduce phone tag
- Pre-qualify prospects
- Automatic CRM entry
- Spam protection
- Professional appearance
- Track effectiveness

**Form Types:**

- General contact form
- Inquiry form
- Application form
- Waitlist form
- Reference check form
- Puppy selection form
- Feedback form
- Custom forms

![Screenshot: Form builder]

### General Contact Form

#### Basic Contact Form Setup

**Default Contact Form:**

- Pre-configured
- Standard fields
- Embedded on website
- "Contact Us" page
- Simple and effective

**Standard Fields:**

```
Contact Form

Name: [Required]
Email: [Required]
Phone: [Optional]
Subject: [Dropdown]
  - General Inquiry
  - Puppy Availability
  - Application Question
  - Other
Message: [Required, text area]
How did you hear about us? [Optional]

[Send Message]
```

**Form Location:**

- Contact page (default)
- Footer of all pages
- Popup/modal option
- Embedded anywhere
- Multiple placements

**Submission Handling:**

1. Visitor fills form
2. Validates required fields
3. Submits
4. Thank you message displays
5. Email sent to you
6. Creates inquiry record
7. Auto-response to visitor

![Screenshot: Contact form on website]

### Inquiry Form

#### Detailed Inquiry Capture

**Purpose:**

- More detailed than contact
- Pre-qualify interest
- Capture specific needs
- Better matching
- Professional screening

**Inquiry Form Fields:**

**Contact Information:**

- First name (required)
- Last name (required)
- Email (required)
- Phone (optional)
- City/State (optional)
- Country (optional)

**Interest Details:**

- Breed interested in (if multiple)
- Preferred gender (male/female/either)
- Preferred color (dropdown)
- Timeline (when ready)
- Puppy purpose (pet/show/breeding)

**Experience & Situation:**

- Dog experience level
- Current pets
- Household members
- Home type (house/apartment/farm)
- Fenced yard (yes/no)

**Additional Information:**

- How heard about us
- Questions/comments
- Specific requests

```

### Application Form

#### Comprehensive Application

**Full Application Form:**

- Detailed screening
- All necessary information
- Decision-making data
- Professional standard
- Serious buyers only

**Application Sections:**

**1. Personal Information:**

- Full name
- Date of birth
- Address (complete)
- Phone numbers (home/cell)
- Email
- Emergency contact
- ID verification (optional)

**2. Household Information:**

- Marital status
- Spouse/partner name
- Adults living in home
- Children (names and ages)
- Visitors/frequent guests
- Who will be primary caregiver

**3. Home & Property:**

- Own or rent
- If rent: Landlord contact, pet deposit
- Type of home
- Size of property
- Fencing details (height, type, area)
- Where will dog stay during day
- Where will dog sleep at night
- Climate control (heating/cooling)

**4. Pet Experience:**

- Previous dog ownership
- Current pets (species, age, spayed/neutered)
- What happened to previous pets
- Veterinarian contact info
- Training experience
- Breed-specific experience

**5. Dog Care Plans:**

- Exercise plan
- Training plan
- Grooming plan
- Budget for care
- Who cares for dog if you travel
- What if circumstances change

**6. Preferences:**

- Preferred puppy gender
- Preferred color/markings
- Temperament preferences
- Any special needs/requests

**7. References:**

- Veterinarian (name, clinic, phone)
- Personal reference 1
- Personal reference 2
- Landlord (if renting)
- Previous breeder (if applicable)

**8. Agreement & Signature:**

- Home visit consent
- Reference check authorization
- Information accuracy statement
- Digital signature
- Date

**Example Application Question:**

```
Previous Pet Experience

Have you owned dogs before? *
( ) Yes  ( ) No

If yes, please list:
[Table format]
Name | Breed | Years Owned | What Happened
â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€
     |       |             |
     |       |             |
[Add Another]

Do you currently have pets? *
( ) Yes  ( ) No

[Text area: Include species, ages, and
whether they are spayed/neutered]

Clinic Name: *
Veterinarian Name:
Phone Number: *

May we contact your veterinarian? *
( ) Yes  ( ) No
```

### Form Builder

![Screenshot: Form builder interface]

#### Creating Custom Forms

**Accessing Form Builder:**

1. Go to Settings > Forms
2. Click "Create New Form"
3. Or edit existing form
4. Drag-and-drop builder
5. Add/remove fields
6. Configure settings
7. Publish

**Available Field Types:**

**Text Fields:**

- Single line text
- Multi-line text area
- Email (with validation)
- Phone number
- URL
- Number

**Selection Fields:**

- Dropdown menu
- Radio buttons
- Checkboxes
- Multi-select

**Date & Time:**

- Date picker
- Time picker
- Date range

**File Upload:**

- Single file
- Multiple files
- File type restrictions
- Size limits

**Special Fields:**

- Signature pad
- Rating scale
- Address (formatted)
- Payment (if enabled)
- reCAPTCHA

**Layout Elements:**

- Section headers
- Descriptive text
- Images
- Dividers
- Page breaks (multi-page)

**Field Configuration:**

**For Each Field:**

- Field label
- Placeholder text
- Help text/tooltip
- Required or optional
- Validation rules
- Default value
- Conditional logic
- Field width (full/half/third)

**Example Configuration:**

```
Field: Email Address

Label: Email Address *
Placeholder: your@email.com
Help Text: We'll send your application
           confirmation here
Required: âœ“ Yes
Validation: Email format
Conditional: Always show
Width: Half

[Save Field]
```

#### Form Logic and Validation

**Conditional Logic:**

- Show/hide fields based on answers
- Skip sections if not applicable
- Dynamic form experience
- Reduce clutter
- Relevant questions only

**Example:**

```
Question: Do you currently have dogs?
( ) Yes  ( ) No

IF Yes THEN SHOW:
  - How many dogs?
  - Please describe your current dogs
  - Are they spayed/neutered?
  - Do they get along with other dogs?

IF No THEN SKIP above questions
```

**Validation Rules:**

**Built-In Validation:**

- Required fields
- Email format
- Phone format
- Number range
- Minimum/maximum length
- Date range
- File type/size

**Custom Validation:**

- Pattern matching
- Custom error messages
- Complex rules
- Cross-field validation

**Example Validation:**

```
Age Field:
- Must be 18 or older
- Error message: "You must be at least 18
  years old to apply"

Phone Field:
- Format: (XXX) XXX-XXXX
- Error: "Please enter a valid phone number"

File Upload:
- Types: .pdf, .jpg, .png only
- Max size: 5MB
- Error: "File must be under 5MB"
```

**Notification Preferences:**

1. Go to form settings

6. Set send conditions
7. Test notifications

### Spam Protection

![Screenshot: Spam protection settings]

#### Preventing Spam Submissions

**Built-In Protection:**

**reCAPTCHA:**

- Google reCAPTCHA v3
- Invisible to users
- Scores submissions
- Blocks bots
- Minimal friction

**Honeypot Fields:**

- Hidden fields
- Bots fill them
- Humans don't see them
- Auto-reject if filled
- No user impact

**Rate Limiting:**

- Limit submissions per IP
- Prevent flooding
- Configurable threshold
- Example: 3 per hour

**Email Validation:**

- Verify email format
- Check disposable domains
- Prevent fake emails
- Improve deliverability

**Spam Scoring:**

- Analyzes content
- Detects patterns
- Flags suspicious
- Manual review option

**Configuration:**

```
Spam Protection Settings

reCAPTCHA: âœ“ Enabled
  Site Key: [Your key]
  Secret Key: [Your secret]

Honeypot: âœ“ Enabled

Rate Limiting: âœ“ Enabled
  Max submissions per IP: 3
  Time window: 1 hour

Email Validation: âœ“ Enabled
  Block disposable emails: âœ“
  Verify MX records: âœ“

Spam Threshold: Medium
  Low: Catch obvious spam only
  Medium: Balanced (recommended)
  High: Aggressive filtering

[Save Settings]
```

**Manual Spam Management:**

- Review flagged submissions
- Mark as spam
- Unmark if false positive
- Block specific IPs
- Block email domains
- Spam list management

### Form Embedding

![Screenshot: Embed options]

#### Adding Forms to Your Website

**Embed Methods:**

**Direct Integration:**

- Forms on system pages
- Automatically embedded
- No extra work
- Styled to match

**Embed Code:**

- Copy embed code
- Paste on other sites
- External websites
- Landing pages
- Social media links

**Example Embed Code:**

```html
<iframe
  src="https://yourkennel.breederapp.com/forms/inquiry"
  width="100%"
  height="800"
  frameborder="0"
>
</iframe>
```

**Popup Forms:**

- Appear on page load
- After X seconds
- On exit intent
- Higher visibility
- Can be annoying (use wisely)

**Sticky Forms:**

- Fixed to bottom/side
- Always visible
- Minimal intrusion
- Good for contact
- Mobile-friendly

**Landing Pages:**

- Dedicated form pages
- No navigation
- Focused conversion
- For ad campaigns
- Track separately

### Practice Exercises

**Exercise 1: Customize Contact Form**

1. Go to Settings > Forms
2. Select "Contact Form"
3. Click "Edit"
4. Add field: "How did you hear about us?"
   - Type: Dropdown
   - Options: Google, Facebook, Instagram, Referral, Other

   - Contact Info
   - Puppy Preferences
   - Experience

5. Configure validation
6. Set up notifications

8. Get embed code

**Exercise 3: Set Up Conditional Logic**

1. Edit application form
2. Find question: "Do you rent or own?"
3. Add logic:
   - If "Rent" â†’ Show landlord fields
   - If "Own" â†’ Skip landlord fields
4. Test both paths
5. Adjust as needed
6. Save changes

**Exercise 4: Configure Spam Protection**

1. Go to form settings
2. Enable reCAPTCHA
3. Get keys from Google
4. Enter keys
5. Enable honeypot
6. Set rate limit: 3/hour
7. Test form submission
8. Verify protection working

**Exercise 5: Review Form Submissions**

1. Go to Forms > Submissions
2. Filter: Last 7 days
3. Review each new submission
4. Approve 2 inquiries
5. Decline 1 (with note)
6. Convert 1 to customer
7. Archive old submissions

**Exercise 6: Analyze Form Performance**

1. Go to Forms > Analytics
2. Select inquiry form
3. Review metrics:
   - Completion rate
   - Abandonment points
   - Conversion rate
4. Identify improvement areas
5. Note busiest submission times
6. Plan optimizations

### Tooltips and Quick Help

> ðŸ“ **Drag & Drop**: Build forms visually with no coding required

> ðŸ›¡ï¸ **Spam Protection**: Advanced filtering blocks 99% of spam automatically

> ðŸ“§ **Auto-Responses**: Professional thank-you emails sent instantly

> ðŸ“Š **Track Everything**: See completion rates, drop-offs, and conversions

> ðŸ”„ **Auto-Sync**: Form submissions automatically create CRM records

> ðŸ“± **Mobile-Optimized**: All forms perfect on phones and tablets

> ðŸŽ¨ **Branded**: Forms match your website design automatically

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Not receiving form notifications**

- Solution: Check spam folder, verify email settings, test notification

**Problem: Form submissions going to spam**

- Solution: Enable reCAPTCHA, adjust spam threshold, review filters

**Problem: High abandonment rate**

- Solution: Simplify form, reduce required fields, add progress indicator

**Problem: Form not displaying on website**

- Solution: Check embed code, verify form published, clear cache

**Problem: Conditional logic not working**

- Solution: Review logic rules, test each path, check field names match

**Problem: File uploads failing**

- Solution: Check file size limit, verify allowed file types, test smaller file

### Advanced Features

**Multi-Page Forms:**

- Break long forms into steps
- Progress indicator
- Save and continue later
- Reduce overwhelm
- Higher completion

**Payment Integration:**

- Collect deposits via form
- Application fees
- Reservation payments
- Secure processing
- Automatic receipts

**Document Upload:**

- Request vet records
- Home photos
- Identification
- References
- Background checks

**Form Templates:**

- Save custom forms
- Reuse across litters
- Share with network
- Import/export
- Industry standards

**Webhook Integration:**

- Connect to other systems
- Zapier integration
- Custom workflows
- Real-time sync
- Advanced automation

**Smart Forms:**

- AI-powered suggestions
- Auto-fill from previous
- Predictive validation
- Intelligent routing
- Personalized experience

## Lesson 28: Privacy Settings and Data Protection

### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Configure privacy settings for your data
- Control what information is publicly visible
- Comply with privacy regulations
- Manage customer data preferences
- Implement data retention policies
- Handle data deletion requests
- Secure sensitive information
- Maintain professional privacy standards

### Privacy Overview

#### Why Privacy Matters

**Legal Requirements:**

- GDPR (Europe)
- CCPA (California)
- Other state laws
- Industry standards
- Ethical obligation

**Benefits:**

- Build trust
- Protect customers
- Avoid liability
- Professional reputation
- Competitive advantage
- Peace of mind

**What You Control:**

- Public website visibility
- Customer data sharing
- Search engine indexing
- Social media integration
- Data retention
- Third-party access

![Screenshot: Privacy dashboard]

### Public Website Privacy

#### Controlling What's Visible

**Website Visibility Settings:**

**Public Information:**

- What shows to everyone
- No login required
- Search engines can find
- Shareable links

**Private Information:**

- Login required
- Not in search engines
- Restricted access
- Your control

**Configuration:**

```
Public Website Privacy Settings

General Visibility:
â— Public (anyone can view)
â—‹ Unlisted (link only, not searchable)
â—‹ Private (login required)

Show on Website:
â˜‘ Kennel name and location (city/state)
â˜‘ Breed(s)
â˜‘ Available litters
â˜‘ Past puppy gallery
â˜ Full address
â˜ Phone number (show email only)
â˜ Pricing details
â˜ Exact birth dates

Search Engine Indexing:
â˜‘ Allow Google/Bing to index site
â˜ Block all search engines

Social Media Integration:
â˜‘ Show social media links
â˜‘ Allow social sharing
â˜ Show social media feeds

[Save Privacy Settings]
```

#### Dog and Litter Privacy

**What to Show About Dogs:**

- â˜‘ Name
- â˜‘ Breed
- â˜‘ Gender
- â˜‘ Color
- â˜‘ Photos
- â˜ Exact age/birth date
- â˜ Registration number
- â˜ Microchip number
- â˜‘ Health testing (summary)
- â˜ Pedigree details
- â˜‘ Achievements/titles

**Litter Page Privacy:**

- â˜‘ Show current litters
- â˜‘ Show expected litters
- â˜ Show puppy prices publicly
- â˜‘ Show availability status
- â˜ Show individual puppy details before reservation
- â˜‘ Show dam and sire info
- â˜ Show exact location

**Past Puppies:**

- â˜‘ Show success stories
- â˜ Show customer names
- â˜ Show customer locations
- â˜‘ Show with customer permission only
- â˜‘ Watermark photos

### Customer Data Privacy

![Screenshot: Customer privacy settings]

#### Managing Customer Information

**Customer Data You Collect:**

- Personal information
- Contact details
- Address
- Family details
- Financial information
- Communications
- Photos/documents
- Preferences

**Privacy Principles:**

**1. Collect Only What's Needed:**

- Relevant to purpose
- No excessive data
- Justified collection
- Clear reason

**2. Use Only as Intended:**

- Purpose specified
- No secondary use without consent
- Transparent usage
- Customer expectations

**3. Secure Storage:**

- Encrypted data
- Access controls
- Regular backups
- Breach prevention

**4. Limited Retention:**

- Keep only as long as needed
- Delete when no longer necessary
- Clear retention policies
- Customer control

**5. Customer Rights:**

- Access their data
- Correct inaccuracies
- Request deletion
- Opt out of communications
- Data portability

#### Customer Consent

**What Requires Consent:**

**Explicit Consent Needed:**

- Marketing emails
- Photo/testimonial use
- Data sharing with third parties
- Cookies/tracking
- Special data categories

**Implied Consent:**

- Essential communications
- Transaction-related
- Account management
- Legal requirements

**Consent Management:**

```
Customer: Sarah Johnson
sarah@email.com

Consent Preferences:

Communication:
â˜‘ Application updates (required)
â˜‘ Litter announcements
â˜‘ Monthly newsletter
â˜ Promotional offers
â˜ SMS notifications

Content Usage:
â˜‘ Use puppy photos on website
â˜‘ Use testimonial
â˜ Use in marketing materials
â˜‘ Share on social media (with credit)

Data Sharing:
â˜ Share with partner breeders
â˜ Include in breed club directory
â˜‘ Veterinary information sharing (if needed)

Updated: Dec 1, 2024
[Edit Preferences]
```

**Obtaining Consent:**

- Clear language
- Separate consent per purpose
- Easy to understand
- Affirmative action required
- Can withdraw anytime
- Record of consent kept

### Privacy Policy

![Screenshot: Privacy policy editor]

#### Creating Your Privacy Policy

**Why You Need One:**

- Legal requirement (many jurisdictions)
- Builds trust
- Sets expectations
- Protects you legally
- Professional standard

**What to Include:**

**1. Information Collected:**

- What data you collect
- How you collect it
- Why you collect it
- Examples

**2. How Information Is Used:**

- Primary purposes
- Secondary purposes
- Who processes it
- Automated decisions

**3. Information Sharing:**

- Who data is shared with
- Why shared
- Safeguards in place
- Third-party processors

**4. Data Storage and Security:**

- Where data stored
- Security measures
- Retention periods
- Deletion process

**5. Customer Rights:**

- Access data
- Correct data
- Delete data
- Opt-out options
- Complaints process

**6. Cookies and Tracking:**

- What cookies used
- Why used
- How to disable
- Third-party cookies

**7. Children's Privacy:**

- Age requirements
- Parental consent
- Special protections

**8. Changes to Policy:**

- How notified
- When effective
- Version history

**9. Contact Information:**

- How to reach you
- Privacy questions
- Data requests

**Example Policy Excerpt:**

```
Privacy Policy - [Your Kennel Name]

Information We Collect

We collect information that you provide directly:
â€¢ Name, email, phone, address
â€¢ Application responses
â€¢ Communications with us
â€¢ Payment information
â€¢ Photos you share

We collect information automatically:
â€¢ Website usage (pages viewed, time spent)
â€¢ Device information
â€¢ IP address
â€¢ Cookies

How We Use Your Information

We use your information to:
â€¢ Process your puppy application
â€¢ Match you with suitable puppies
â€¢ Communicate about litters and availability
â€¢ Provide customer support
â€¢ Improve our website and services

We will never sell your personal information.

Your Rights

You have the right to:
â€¢ Access your data
â€¢ Request corrections
â€¢ Request deletion
â€¢ Opt out of marketing
â€¢ Withdraw consent

To exercise these rights, contact us at:
privacy@yourkennelname.com

[View Full Policy]
```

**Publishing Your Policy:**

1. Create policy using template
2. Customize for your practices
3. Review with attorney (recommended)
4. Publish on website
5. Link in footer
6. Include in applications
7. Update regularly

### Data Retention

![Screenshot: Data retention settings]

#### How Long to Keep Data

**Retention Policies:**

**Active Customers:**

- Keep indefinitely
- Ongoing relationship
- Future purchases
- Support needs

**Past Customers:**

- Keep for X years
- Health guarantee period
- Legal requirements
- Relationship building

**Declined Applicants:**

- Keep 1 year
- May reapply
- Then auto-delete
- Unless requested otherwise

**Inquiries (No Application):**

- Keep 6 months
- Marketing purposes
- Then auto-delete
- Can opt in for longer

**Financial Records:**

- Keep 7 years
- Tax requirements
- Legal protection
- Audit trail

**Configuration:**

```
Data Retention Settings

Customer Records:
Active Customers: Indefinitely
Past Customers: 10 years after last purchase
Declined Applicants: 1 year
Inquiries Only: 6 months

Financial Data:
Payment Records: 7 years
Invoices: 7 years
Contracts: Indefinitely

Communications:
Emails: 2 years
Messages: 1 year
Notes: With customer record

Photos/Documents:
Customer-provided photos: With consent
Documents: With customer record

Automatic Deletion:
â˜‘ Enable automatic cleanup
â˜‘ Notify before deletion
â˜‘ Allow customer download

[Save Retention Policy]
```

**Data Deletion:**

- Manual deletion option
- Bulk deletion
- Permanent removal
- Backup removal
- Cannot be undone
- Complies with regulations

### Handling Data Requests

![Screenshot: Data request management]

#### Customer Rights Requests

**Types of Requests:**

**1. Access Request:**

- Customer wants to see their data
- What you have stored
- How it's used
- Who it's shared with

**Response:**

1. Verify identity
2. Export all their data
3. Provide in readable format
4. Within 30 days
5. Free of charge

**2. Correction Request:**

- Data is inaccurate
- Needs updating
- Wrong information

**Response:**

1. Verify issue
2. Make corrections
3. Confirm with customer
4. Update everywhere
5. Notify if shared with others

**3. Deletion Request:**

- "Right to be forgotten"
- Remove all data
- Except legal requirements

**Response:**

1. Verify identity
2. Check legal obligations
3. Delete from all systems
4. Confirm deletion
5. May keep transaction records for taxes

**4. Opt-Out Request:**

- Stop marketing emails
- No more calls
- Remove from lists

**Response:**

1. Immediate opt-out
2. Confirm to customer
3. Update preferences
4. May take 1-2 days for systems

**5. Data Portability:**

- Provide data in portable format
- Can transfer to another system
- Machine-readable

**Response:**

1. Export to CSV/JSON
2. Provide download link
3. Includes all their data
4. Within 30 days

**Request Management:**

```
Data Request: Access Request
From: Sarah Johnson (sarah@email.com)
Date: Dec 1, 2024
Type: Access Request
Status: In Progress

Customer Message:
"I'd like to see what information you have
about me and my application."

Actions Taken:
âœ“ Identity verified (Dec 1)
âœ“ Data export generated (Dec 1)
â˜ Sent to customer
â˜ Closed

Data Package Includes:
â€¢ Personal information
â€¢ Application responses
â€¢ Communication history
â€¢ Contract and documents
â€¢ Payment records
â€¢ Notes and status

[Generate Export] [Send to Customer] [Close Request]
```

### Security Measures

![Screenshot: Security settings]

#### Protecting Customer Data

**Security Features:**

**Encryption:**

- Data encrypted at rest
- SSL/TLS in transit
- Database encryption
- Backup encryption
- End-to-end protection

**Access Controls:**

- Strong passwords required
- Two-factor authentication
- Role-based access
- Activity logging
- Session timeout

**Backups:**

- Daily automatic backups
- Multiple locations
- Encrypted backups
- Tested regularly
- Disaster recovery

**Monitoring:**

- Security scanning
- Breach detection
- Unusual activity alerts
- Regular audits
- Vulnerability testing

**Best Practices:**

**For You:**

- Use strong unique passwords
- Enable 2FA
- Don't share login
- Log out when done
- Use secure networks
- Keep software updated
- Review access logs

**For Customers:**

- Secure account creation
- Password requirements
- Optional 2FA
- Session security
- Privacy controls
- Educate on security

**Breach Response Plan:**

1. Detect and contain breach
2. Assess what data affected
3. Notify affected customers (72 hours)
4. Notify authorities (if required)
5. Offer protection services
6. Document incident
7. Prevent future breaches
8. Public statement if needed

### Third-Party Integrations

#### Managing Data Sharing

**Third-Party Services:**

- Email providers
- Payment processors
- Analytics tools
- Social media
- Cloud storage
- Backup services

**Due Diligence:**

- Review privacy policies
- Check security standards
- Understand data usage
- Verify compliance
- Assess necessity

**Configuration:**

```

IP Anonymization: âœ“ Enabled

Status: â—‹ Disabled

Purpose: Advertising
Privacy Policy: [Link]
Note: Requires cookie consent

[Review All Integrations]
```

**Data Processing Agreements:**

- Formal contracts
- With processors
- Define responsibilities
- Ensure compliance
- Legal protection

### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Privacy policy link not showing on website**

- Solution: Go to website settings, enable policy link, add to footer, publish

**Problem: Customer can't access their data**

- Solution: Generate export manually, verify email address, send direct link

**Problem: Old data not being deleted automatically**

- Solution: Check retention settings enabled, verify date calculations, run manual cleanup

**Problem: Third-party integration sharing too much data**

- Solution: Review integration settings, limit data sharing, consider disabling

**Problem: Customer consent not recorded**

- Solution: Update consent manually, document how obtained, set going forward process

**Problem: Security alert triggered**

- Solution: Review alert details, check if legitimate activity, change password if compromised

## Module 8: Advanced Features

### Lesson 29: Connections and Networking

#### Learning Objectives

By the end of this lesson, you will be able to:

- Connect with other breeders and professionals
- Manage breeder network contacts
- Send and receive connection requests
- Share data securely with trusted partners
- Collaborate on litters, co-ownership, and guardianship
- Track networking activity and history
- Use breeder directory and search tools
- Leverage networking for business growth

#### Overview

The Connections and Networking system helps you build professional relationships, collaborate on breeding projects, and expand your reach. It supports secure data sharing, co-ownership management, and breeder-to-breeder communication.

#### Key Features

- Breeder directory with search and filters
- Connection requests and approvals
- Data sharing preferences
- Collaboration tools (litters, contracts, guardianship)
- Messaging and notifications
- Activity tracking and history
- Privacy controls

![Screenshot: Breeder directory and connection request]

#### Step-by-Step Instructions

**1. Accessing the Breeder Directory**

1. Go to "Connections" in the main menu
2. Browse the breeder directory
3. Use filters (location, breed, program type)
4. View breeder profiles
5. See available litters, co-ownerships, and guardianships

**2. Sending a Connection Request**

1. Click "Connect" on a breeder profile
2. Add a message (optional)
3. Select data sharing preferences
4. Send request
5. Await approval

**3. Receiving and Managing Requests**

1. Notification appears for new requests
2. Review senderâ€™s profile and message
3. Accept, decline, or request more info
4. Set data sharing level (basic, full, custom)
5. Connection added to your network

**4. Collaborating on Litters and Contracts**

1. Open a connection profile
2. Click "Collaborate"
3. Select project type (litter, contract, guardianship)
4. Share relevant data (dog profiles, health records, contracts)
5. Set permissions (view, edit, comment)
6. Track collaboration status

**5. Messaging and Notifications**

1. Use built-in messaging to communicate
2. Send files, photos, and documents
3. Receive notifications for updates
4. Archive or delete conversations

**6. Tracking Networking Activity**

1. View activity log for each connection
2. See history of shared data, collaborations, and messages
3. Export activity for records

**7. Privacy and Data Sharing Controls**

1. Set global data sharing preferences
2. Customize per connection
3. Revoke access at any time
4. Monitor shared data

#### Practice Exercises

**Exercise 1: Find and Connect with a Breeder**

1. Go to Connections > Directory
2. Search for breeders in your state
3. Filter by breed
4. Send a connection request to one breeder
5. Add a personalized message

**Exercise 2: Approve a Connection Request**

1. Receive a new connection request
2. Review senderâ€™s profile
3. Accept the request
4. Set data sharing to "basic"
5. Send a welcome message

**Exercise 3: Collaborate on a Litter**

1. Open a connection profile
2. Click "Collaborate"
3. Select "Litter Project"
4. Share dam and sire profiles
5. Set permissions to "view only"
6. Track collaboration status

**Exercise 4: Adjust Data Sharing Preferences**

1. Go to Settings > Connections
2. Edit data sharing for one connection
3. Change from "basic" to "full"
4. Save changes

**Exercise 5: Send a Message and File**

1. Open a connection
2. Send a message about a litter
3. Attach a health certificate PDF
4. Confirm delivery

**Exercise 6: Export Networking Activity**

1. Go to Connections > Activity Log
2. Export last 30 days of activity
3. Save as CSV
4. Review exported data

#### Tooltips and Quick Help

> ðŸ¤ **Connect Easily**: Find breeders by location, breed, and program type
> ðŸ”’ **Secure Sharing**: Control what data is shared with each connection
> ðŸ“ **Collaborate**: Work together on litters, contracts, and guardianship
> ðŸ“¨ **Messaging**: Built-in chat for fast communication
> ðŸ•’ **Track History**: See all activity and shared data
> ðŸ›¡ï¸ **Privacy First**: Revoke access or adjust sharing anytime

#### Troubleshooting

**Problem: Canâ€™t find a breeder in directory**

- Solution: Check filters, expand search radius, verify breeder is active

**Problem: Connection request not received**

- Solution: Check notifications, refresh page, verify email settings

**Problem: Data sharing too broad**

- Solution: Edit sharing preferences, set to "custom", restrict access

**Problem: Collaboration permissions not working**

- Solution: Review permissions, ensure correct roles, contact support

**Problem: Messaging issues**

- Solution: Check internet connection, refresh, clear browser cache

#### Advanced Features

- Bulk connection requests for breed clubs
- Group collaborations (multi-breeder projects)
- Automated networking suggestions
- Verified breeder badges
- Connection analytics (engagement, collaboration frequency)
- API integration for external breeder networks

# Glossary of Terms

**AKC**: American Kennel Club
**CKC**: Canadian Kennel Club  
**Dam**: Mother dog
**Sire**: Father dog
**Heat/Estrus**: Female fertility cycle
**Whelping**: Birth of puppies
**Guardian Home**: Family raises breeder's dog
**External Stud**: Outside male for breeding
**Microchip**: ID chip implanted in dog
**DNA Profile**: Genetic test results
**Pedigree**: Family tree
**Co-ownership**: Shared ownership
**Breeding Rights**: Permission to breed
